CockroachDB v23.1 <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/releases/release-support-policy#support-types" data-versioned="true">(LTS)</a> is a required <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/releases#major-versions" data-versioned="true">Regular release</a>.

Refer to <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/releases/release-support-policy#support-types" data-versioned="true">Major release types</a> before installing or upgrading for release timing and support details. To learn what's new in this release, refer to its [Feature Highlights](#feature-highlights).

On this page, you can read about changes and find downloads for all production and testing releases of CockroachDB v23.1 <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/releases/release-support-policy#support-phases" data-versioned="true">(LTS)</a>

- For key feature enhancements in v23.1 and other upgrade considerations, refer to the notes for [v23.1.0](#v23-1-0).
- For details about release types, naming, and licensing, refer to the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/releases" data-versioned="true">Releases</a> page.
- Be sure to also review the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/releases/release-support-policy" data-versioned="true">Release Support Policy</a>.
- After downloading a supported CockroachDB binary, learn how to <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/install-cockroachdb" data-versioned="true">install CockroachDB</a> or <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/upgrade-cockroach-version" data-versioned="true">upgrade your cluster</a>.

Get future release notes emailed to you:

<MarketoEmailForm />

### Docker image

[Multi-platform images](https://docs.docker.com/build/building/multi-platform) include support for both Intel and ARM. Multi-platform images do not take up additional space on your Docker host.

Within the multi-platform image, both Intel and ARM images are **generally available** for production use.

To download the Docker image:

```shell
docker pull cockroachdb/cockroach:v23.1.30
```

### Source tag

To view or download the source code for CockroachDB v23.1.30 on Github, visit [v23.1.30 source tag](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/releases/tag/v23.1.30).

### Changelog

View a detailed changelog on GitHub: [v23.1.29...v23.1.30](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/compare/v23.1.29...v23.1.30)

### Security updates

- All cluster settings that accept strings are now fully redacted when transmitted as part of CockroachDB's diagnostics telemetry. The transmitted payload includes a record of modified cluster settings and their values when they are not strings. If you previously applied the mitigations in [Technical Advisory 133479](/docs/advisories/a133479), you can safely turn on diagnostic reporting via the `diagnostics.reporting.enabled` cluster setting without leaking sensitive cluster settings values. [#134063](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/134063)

### General changes

- `COCKROACH_SKIP_ENABLING_DIAGNOSTIC_REPORTING` is no longer mentioned in the `cockroach demo` command. [#134083](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/134083)

### Bug fixes

- Fixed a bug where CockroachDB could encounter an internal error `interface conversion: coldata.Column is` in an edge case. The bug was present in v22.2.13+, v23.1.9+, and v23.2+. [#133758](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/133758)
- Fixed a bug that caused incorrect `NOT NULL` constraint violation errors on `UPSERT` and `INSERT... ON CONFLICT... DO UPDATE` statements when those statements updated an existing row and a subset of columns that did not include a `NOT NULL` column of the table. This bug had been present since at least v20.1.0. [#133824](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/133824)
- Fixed an unhandled error that could occur when using `REVOKE... ON SEQUENCE FROM... user` on an object that is not a sequence. [#133706](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/133706)
- Addressed a panic that could occur inside `CREATE TABLE AS` if sequence builtin expressions had invalid function overloads. [#133866](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/133866)
- Previously, when executing queries with index / lookup joins where ordering needed to be maintained, CockroachDB's behavior could lead to increased query latency, potentially by several orders of magnitude. This bug was introduced in v22.2, and is now fixed. [#134363](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/134363)
- Fixed a bug where `DROP CASCADE` would occasionally panic with an `un-dropped backref` message on partitioned tables. [#134524](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/134524)
- Reduced the duration of partitions in the gossip network when a node crashes. This eliminates false positives in the `ranges.unavailable` metric. [#134603](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/134603)

### Docker image

[Multi-platform images](https://docs.docker.com/build/building/multi-platform) include support for both Intel and ARM. Multi-platform images do not take up additional space on your Docker host.

Within the multi-platform image, both Intel and ARM images are **generally available** for production use.

To download the Docker image:

```shell
docker pull cockroachdb/cockroach:v23.1.29
```

### Source tag

To view or download the source code for CockroachDB v23.1.29 on Github, visit [v23.1.29 source tag](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/releases/tag/v23.1.29).

### Changelog

View a detailed changelog on GitHub: [v23.1.28...v23.1.29](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/compare/v23.1.28...v23.1.29)

### General changes

- Changed the license CockroachDB is distributed under to the new CockroachDB Software License (CSL). [#131704](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/131704) [#131916](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/131916) [#131917](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/131917) [#131966](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/131966) [#131971](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/131971) [#131969](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/131969) [#131980](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/131980) [#131979](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/131979) [#131974](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/131974) [#131975](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/131975) [#132052](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/132052) [#132059](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/132059) [#132804](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/132804) [#132800](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/132800)
- Attempting to install a second enterprise trial license on the same cluster will now fail. [#131977](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/131977)
- The cluster setting `diagnostics.reporting.enabled` is now ignored if the cluster has a Trial or Free license, or if the reporting job is unable to load any license at all. [#132347](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/132347)

### Enterprise edition changes

- A new `changefeed.total_ranges` metric has been added and can be used to monitor the number of ranges that are watched by changefeed aggregators. It shares the same polling interval as `changefeed.lagging_ranges`, which is controlled by the existing `changefeed.lagging_ranges_polling_interval` cluster setting. [#131246](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/131246)
- Allowed access to DB console APIs via JWT, which can be supplied as a Bearer token in the Authorization header. [#133457](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/133457)

### DB Console changes

- DB Console will reflect any throttling behavior from the cluster due to an expired license or missing telemetry data. Enterprise licenses are not affected. [#131858](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/131858)

### Bug fixes

- Fixed a bug introduced in v23.1 that can cause incorrect results when:
  1. The query contains a correlated subquery.
  2. The correlated subquery has a `GroupBy` or `DistinctOn` operator with an outer-column reference in its input.
  3. The correlated subquery is in the input of a `Select` or `Join` operator
  4. The `Select` or `Join` has a filter that sets the outer-column reference from (2) equal to a non-outer column in the input of the grouping operator.
  5. The grouping column set does not include the replacement column, and functionally determines the replacement column. [#130987](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/130987)
- The AWS endpoint and cloud custom HTTP client configuration are now considered when implicit authentication is used, whereas previously these were only considered when using explicit credentials. [#131200](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/131200)
- Fixed a bug that could cause spurious user permission errors when multiple databases shared a common schema with a routine referencing a table. The bug has existed since UDFs were introduced in v22.2. [#126414](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/126414)
- Fixed a rare bug where a lease transfer could lead to a `side-transport update saw closed timestamp regression` panic. The bug could occur when a node was overloaded and failing to heartbeat its node liveness record. [#131838](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/131838)
- Fixed an error that could happen if an aggregate function was used as the value in a `SET` command. [#131957](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/131957)
- Fixed a bug where a span stats request on a mixed version cluster resulted in a null pointer exception (NPE). [#132685](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/132685)
- Fixed a rare bug in which an update of a primary key column which is also the only column in a separate column family can sometimes fail to update the primary index. This bug has existed since v22.2. Requirements to hit the bug are:
  1. A table with multiple column families.
  2. A column family containing a single primary key column.
  3. That column family is not the first column family.
  4. That column family existed before its column was in the primary key.
  5. That column must be of type `FLOAT4/8`, `DECIMAL`, `JSON`, collated `STRING`, or `ARRAY`.
  6. An update changes that column from a composite value to a non-composite value. [#132124](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/132124)
- The `proretset` column of the `pg_catalog.pg_proc` table is now properly set to `true` for set-returning builtin functions. [#132873](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/132873)
- Fixed a bug in the query optimizer which could cause CockroachDB nodes to crash in rare cases. The bug could occur when a query contained a filter of the form `col IN (elem0, elem1,..., elemN)` such that `N` is very large, e.g. 1.6+ million, and when `col` exists in a hash-sharded index or exists in a table with an indexed, computed column dependent on `col`. [#133068](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/133068)
- Users with the admin role can now run `ALTER DEFAULT PRIVILEGES FOR target_role...` on any `target_role`. Previously, this could result in a privilege error, which is incorrect as admins are allowed to perform any operation. [#133067](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/133067)
- `REASSIGN OWNED BY` will now transfer ownership of the public schema. Previously, it would always skip over the public schema even if it was owned by the target role. [#133067](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/133067)
- Fixed a bug where backup schedules could advance a protected timestamp too early, which caused incremental backups to fail. [#131388](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/131388)

        </a>
        <br />(
        <a href="https://binaries.cockroachdb.com/cockroach-sql-v23.1.28.darwin-11.0-arm64.tgz.sha256sum">SHA256</a>)

### Docker image

[Multi-platform images](https://docs.docker.com/build/building/multi-platform) include support for both Intel and ARM. Multi-platform images do not take up additional space on your Docker host.

Within the multi-platform image, both Intel and ARM images are **generally available** for production use.

To download the Docker image:

```shell
docker pull cockroachdb/cockroach:v23.1.28
```

### Source tag

To view or download the source code for CockroachDB v23.1.28 on Github, visit [v23.1.28 source tag](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/releases/tag/v23.1.28).

### Changelog

View a detailed changelog on GitHub: [v23.1.27...v23.1.28](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/compare/v23.1.27...v23.1.28)

### Security changes

- <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/show-jobs" data-versioned="true">
    `SHOW JOBS`
  </a>
  and its variants
  <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/show-jobs#show-changefeed-jobs" data-versioned="true">
    `SHOW CHANGEFEED JOB`
  </a>
  and
  <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/show-jobs#show-changefeed-jobs" data-versioned="true">
    `SHOW CHANGEFEED JOBS`
  </a>
  no longer expose user sensitive information like `client_key`.
  [#129910](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/129910)

### General changes

- Upgraded <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/architecture/distribution-layer#grpc" data-versioned="true">gRPC</a> to v1.56.3. [#130044](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/130044)

### Operational changes

- Added the `ranges.decommissioning` metric that represents the number of <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/architecture/glossary#range" data-versioned="true">ranges</a> which have a <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/architecture/glossary#replica" data-versioned="true">replica</a> on a <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/node-shutdown" data-versioned="true">decommissioning node</a>. [#130254](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/130254)

### DB Console changes

- DB Console will show an alert message when the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/licensing-faqs" data-versioned="true">license</a> is expired or there are less than 15 days left before it expires. [#130439](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/130439)
- DB Console will show a notification alerting customers without an Enterprise <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/licensing-faqs" data-versioned="true">license</a> to upcoming license changes with a link to more information. [#130439](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/130439)

### Bug fixes

- Fixed a bug where the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/with-storage-parameter#table-parameters" data-versioned="true">`schema_locked` table parameter</a> did not prevent a table from being referenced by a <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/foreign-key" data-versioned="true">foreign key</a>. [#129752](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/129752)
- Fixed a bug where the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/session-variables#require-explicit-primary-keys" data-versioned="true">`require_explicit_primary_keys`</a> session variable would overly aggressively prevent all <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/create-table" data-versioned="true">`CREATE TABLE`</a> statements from working. [#129905](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/129905)
- Fixed a rare bug where a <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/architecture/replication-layer#epoch-based-leases-table-data" data-versioned="true">lease transfer</a> could lead to a `side-transport update saw closed timestamp regression` panic. The bug could occur when a node was <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/ui-overload-dashboard" data-versioned="true">overloaded</a> and failing to heartbeat its <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cluster-setup-troubleshooting#node-liveness-issues" data-versioned="true">node liveness</a> record. [#130124](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/130124)
- Resolve a log message that read: `expiration of liveness record... is not greater than expiration of the previous lease... after liveness heartbeat`. This message is no longer possible. [#130623](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/130623)
- Fixed a potential memory leak in <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/change-data-capture-overview" data-versioned="true">changefeeds</a> using a <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/changefeed-sinks#cloud-storage-sink" data-versioned="true">cloud storage sink</a>. The memory leak could occur if both `changefeed.fast_gzip.enabled` and `changefeed.cloudstorage.async_flush.enabled` are `true` and the changefeed received an error while attempting to write to the cloud storage sink. [#130613](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/130613)

### Docker image

[Multi-platform images](https://docs.docker.com/build/building/multi-platform) include support for both Intel and ARM. Multi-platform images do not take up additional space on your Docker host.

Within the multi-platform image, both Intel and ARM images are **generally available** for production use.

To download the Docker image:

```shell
docker pull cockroachdb/cockroach:v23.1.26
```

### Source tag

To view or download the source code for CockroachDB v23.1.26 on Github, visit [v23.1.26 source tag](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/releases/tag/v23.1.26).

### Changelog

View a detailed changelog on GitHub: [v23.1.25...v23.1.26](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/compare/v23.1.25...v23.1.26)

### Security updates

- For clusters using <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/sso-sql" data-versioned="true">Cluster SSO using JSON Web Tokens (JWTs)</a>, the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cluster-settings" data-versioned="true">cluster setting</a> `server.jwt_authentication.issuers` can now take multiple values to support various kinds of providers and their mapped JWKS URI. You can set it to one of the following values, which are parsed by Go:
  1. A string that contains a single valid issuer URI. Example: `https://accounts.google.com`
  2. A string that contains a JSON array of valid issuer URIs. Example: `['example.com/adfs','https://accounts.google.com']`
  3. A string that contains a JSON map of valid issuer URIs to corresponding JWKS URIs and deserialized into a map of issuer URLs to corresponding JWKS URIs. A JSON map overrides the JWKS URI published in the issuer's `well-known/` endpoint. Example: `'{ "issuer_jwks_map": { "https://accounts.google.com": "https://www.googleapis.com/oauth2/v3/certs", "example.com/adfs": "https://example.com/adfs/discovery/keys" } }'`

     When `issuer_jwks_map` is set, the key set is fetched from the JWKS URI directly. Otherwise, when `JWKSAutoFetchEnabled` is set, the JWKS URI is fetched from the issuer's `well-known/` endpoint. [#128669](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/128669)

### Operational changes

- New <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/logging" data-versioned="true">structured logging events</a> in the `OPS` channel report broken connections and related transactions during node shutdown.
  - `node_shutdown_connection_timeout`: Logged if there are still open client connections after the timeout defined by `server.shutdown.connections.timeout` expires.
  - `node_shutdown_transaction_timeout`: Logged if there are still open transactions on those open client connections after the timeout defined by `server.shutdown.transactions.timeout` expires. [#128709](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/128709)

### Bug fixes

- Fixed a bug introduced in v23.1 in which output of <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/explain" data-versioned="true">`EXPLAIN (OPT, REDACT)`</a> of the following `CREATE` statements was not redacted:
  - `EXPLAIN (OPT, REDACT) CREATE TABLE`
  - `EXPLAIN (OPT, REDACT) CREATE VIEW`
  - `EXPLAIN (OPT, REDACT) CREATE FUNCTION`

    [#128487](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/128487)

- Fixed a bug where incorrect values could be produced for virtual <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/computed-columns" data-versioned="true">computed columns</a> in rare cases when the virtual column expression's type did not match the type of the virtual column. [#129008](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/129008)
- Fixed a bug where errors like `ERROR: column 'crdb_internal_idx_expr' does not exist` could be logged when accessing a table with an <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/expression-indexes" data-versioned="true">expression index</a> where the expression evaluates to an `ENUM` type. Example: `CREATE INDEX ON t ((col::an_enum))` [#129091](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/129091)
- Fixed a bug introduced in v23.1 where a <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/user-defined-functions" data-versioned="true">user-defined function's</a> return type's parameters could not be named when dropping a user-defined function or procedure. [#115906](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/115906)
- Fixed a slow-building memory leak when a cluster uses <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/gssapi_authentication" data-versioned="true">GSSAPI Kerberos authentication</a>. [#130320](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/130320)

### Docker image

[Multi-platform images](https://docs.docker.com/build/building/multi-platform) include support for both Intel and ARM. Multi-platform images do not take up additional space on your Docker host.

Within the multi-platform image, both Intel and ARM images are **generally available** for production use.

To download the Docker image:

```shell
docker pull cockroachdb/cockroach:v23.1.25
```

### Source tag

To view or download the source code for CockroachDB v23.1.25 on Github, visit [v23.1.25 source tag](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/releases/tag/v23.1.25).

### Changelog

View a detailed changelog on GitHub: [v23.1.24...v23.1.25](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/compare/v23.1.24...v23.1.25)

### Security updates

- Secrets are now sanitized from URLs before being written to unredacted <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/configure-logs" data-versioned="true">logs</a> when used in the following SQL statements:
  - <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/backup" data-versioned="true">
      `BACKUP`
    </a>
  - <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/restore" data-versioned="true">
      `RESTORE`
    </a>
  - <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/create-schedule-for-backup" data-versioned="true">
      `CREATE SCHEDULE FOR BACKUP`
    </a>
  - <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/alter-backup-schedule" data-versioned="true">
      `ALTER BACKUP SCHEDULE`
    </a>
  - <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/alter-backup" data-versioned="true">
      `ALTER BACKUP`
    </a>
  - <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/show-backup" data-versioned="true">
      `SHOW BACKUP`
    </a>
  - <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/create-changefeed" data-versioned="true">
      `CREATE CHANGEFEED`
    </a>
  - <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/create-schedule-for-changefeed" data-versioned="true">
      `CREATE SCHEDULE FOR CHANGEFEED`
    </a>
  - <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/alter-changefeed" data-versioned="true">
      `ALTER CHANGEFEED SET {sink}`
    </a>
  - <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/import" data-versioned="true">
      `IMPORT`
    </a>
  - <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/export" data-versioned="true">
      `EXPORT`
    </a>
  - <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/create-external-connection" data-versioned="true">
      `CREATE EXTERNAL CONNECTION`
    </a>
  - <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/copy" data-versioned="true">
      `COPY`
    </a>

    [#127537](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/127537)

- The cluster setting <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/sso-sql#cluster-settings" data-versioned="true">`server.jwt_authentication.issuers`</a> can now take multiple values to support various kinds of providers and their mapped JWKS URIs. This can be set to one of the following values:
  - Simple string that Go can parse as a valid issuer URL: `'https://accounts.google.com'`.
  - String that can be parsed as a valid JSON array of issuer URLs list: `['example.com/adfs','https://accounts.google.com']`.
  - String that can be parsed as a valid JSON and deserialized into a map of issuer URLs to corresponding JWKS URIs. In the third case, CockroachDB will override the JWKS URI present in the issuer's well-known endpoint: `'{ "issuer_jwks_map": { "https://accounts.google.com": "https://www.googleapis.com/oauth2/v3/certs", "example.com/adfs": "https://example.com/adfs/discovery/keys" } }'`.

    When `issuer_jwks_map` is set, CockroachDB directly uses the JWKS URI to get the key set. In all other cases where <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/sso-sql#cluster-settings" data-versioned="true">`server.jwt_authentication.jwks_auto_fetch.enabled`</a> is set CockroachDB obtains the JWKS URI first from the issuer's well-known endpoint and then uses this endpoint. [#128751](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/128751)

### SQL language changes

- Added the `sql.auth.grant_option_inheritance.enabled` <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cluster-settings#setting-sql-auth-grant-option-inheritance-enabled" data-versioned="true">cluster setting</a>. The default value is `true`, which results in behavior that matches the existing behavior of CockroachDB. When set to `false`, the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/grant" data-versioned="true">`GRANT OPTION`</a> is not inherited via role membership, which will prevent the descendant roles from being able to grant the privilege to others. The privilege itself is still inherited via role membership. [#126862](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/126862)
- Added the `sql.auth.grant_option_for_owner.enabled` <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cluster-settings#setting-sql-auth-grant-option-for-owner-enabled" data-versioned="true">cluster setting</a>. The default value is `true`, which results in behavior that matches the existing behavior of CockroachDB. When set to `false`, then the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/grant" data-versioned="true">`GRANT OPTION`</a> is not implcitly given to the owner of an object. The object owner still implicitly has all privileges on the object, just not the ability to grant them to other users. [#127005](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/127005)

### DB Console changes

- The <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/ui-databases-page" data-versioned="true">Database</a> details and Table details pages in the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/ui-overview" data-versioned="true">DB Console</a> now display the correct `"stats last created"` value. [#126415](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/126415)
- The <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/ui-databases-page" data-versioned="true">Database</a> and Tables pages in the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/ui-overview" data-versioned="true">DB Console</a> will show a loading state while loading information for databases and tables including size and <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/architecture/glossary#architecture-range" data-versioned="true">range</a> counts. [#127699](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/127699)
- In the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/ui-databases-page" data-versioned="true">Database</a> details page, the table name will no longer appear with quotes around the schema and table name. [#127763](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/127763)
- <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/alter-role" data-versioned="true">
    `ALTER ROLE`
  </a>
  events in the
  <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/ui-overview" data-versioned="true">
    DB Console
  </a>
  event log now render correctly when the event does not contain any role options.
  [#126563](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/126563)
- Fixed a bug where the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/ui-databases-page" data-versioned="true">Databases</a> page crashed if the range information was not available. [#127090](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/127090)

### Bug fixes

- Fixed a bug in which the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/alter-table" data-versioned="true">`DISCARD`</a> statement was disallowed with <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/session-variables" data-versioned="true">`default_transaction_read_only = on`</a>. [#127549](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/127549)
- Fixed a bug where <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/alter-database#drop-region" data-versioned="true">`ALTER DATABASE... DROP REGION`</a> could fail if any tables under the given database have <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/expression-indexes" data-versioned="true">indexes on expressions</a>. [#126600](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/126600)
- Fixed a bug when <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/restore" data-versioned="true">restoring</a> a database with a <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/create-type#create-a-composite-data-type" data-versioned="true">composite type</a>. [#126847](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/126847)
- Fixed a bug when inputting <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/security-reference/authorization#default-roles" data-versioned="true">`public` role</a> as user name for <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/functions-and-operators#compatibility-functions" data-versioned="true">built-in compatibility functions</a>, such as `has_database_privilege` and `has_schema_privilege`. [#126853](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/126853)
- Fixed a bug where CockroachDB could incorrectly evaluate an <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/null-handling#nulls-and-simple-comparisons" data-versioned="true">`IS NOT NULL`</a> filter if it was applied to non- `NULL` tuples that had `NULL` elements, such as `(1, NULL)` or `(NULL, NULL)`. This bug has existed since v20.2. [#126942](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/126942)
- Fixed a bug where <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/create-table" data-versioned="true">`CREATE TABLE`</a> with <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/expression-indexes" data-versioned="true">index expressions</a> could hit undefined column errors on <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/transaction-retry-error-reference" data-versioned="true">transaction retries</a>. [#126200](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/126200)
- Fixed a bug that caused a memory leak when executing SQL statements with comments, for example, `SELECT /* comment */ 1;`. Memory owned by a SQL session would continue to grow as these types of statements were executed. The memory would only be released when closing the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/show-sessions" data-versioned="true">SQL session</a>. This bug has been present since v23.1. [#127757](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/127757)
- Fixed a bug where <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/create-index" data-versioned="true">`CREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS`</a> would not correctly short-circuit if the given index already existed. [#128239](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/128239)
- Fixed a bug in syntax validation, in which the `DESCENDING` clause was not allowed for non-terminal columns of an <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/inverted-indexes" data-versioned="true">inverted index</a>. Only the last column of an inverted index should be prevented from being `DESCENDING`. This is now properly checked. [#128239](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/128239)
- Fixed a bug where an <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/indexes" data-versioned="true">index</a> could store a column in the primary index if that column had a mixed-case name. [#128239](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/128239)
- Fixed a memory leak that could occur when specifying a non-existent virtual cluster name in the connection string. [#128110](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/128110)
- Setting or dropping a default value on a <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/computed-columns" data-versioned="true">computed column</a> is now blocked, even for `NULL` defaults. Previously, setting or dropping a default value on a computed column was a no-op. [#128468](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/128468)

### Docker image

[Multi-platform images](https://docs.docker.com/build/building/multi-platform) include support for both Intel and ARM. Multi-platform images do not take up additional space on your Docker host.

Within the multi-platform image, both Intel and ARM images are **generally available** for production use.

To download the Docker image:

```shell
docker pull cockroachdb/cockroach:v23.1.24
```

### Source tag

To view or download the source code for CockroachDB v23.1.24 on Github, visit [v23.1.24 source tag](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/releases/tag/v23.1.24).

### Changelog

View a detailed changelog on GitHub: [v23.1.23...v23.1.24](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/compare/v23.1.23...v23.1.24)

### Enterprise edition changes

- <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/alter-changefeed" data-versioned="true">
    `ALTER CHANGEFEED`
  </a>
  no longer removes the CDC query when modifying
  <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/change-data-capture-overview" data-versioned="true">
    changefeed
  </a>
  properties. [#125436](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/125436)

### Operational changes

- Improved disk usage metric reporting over volumes that dynamically change their size over the life of the `cockroach` process. [#125106](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/125106)
- Removed `crdb_internal.cluster_execution_insights.txt` and `crdb_internal.cluster_txn_execution_insights.txt` from the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cockroach-debug-zip" data-versioned="true">`debug zip`</a>. These files contained cluster-wide insights for statements and transactions. Users can still rely on the per-node execution insights in `crdb_internal.node_execution_insights.txt` and `crdb_internal.node_txn_execution_insights.txt`. [#125810](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/125810)
- Some debugging-only information about physical plans is no longer collected in the `system.job_info` table for changefeeds, because it has the potential to grow very large. [#126102](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/126102)

### Bug fixes

- Fixed handling in the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/online-schema-changes" data-versioned="true">declarative schema changer</a> when columns are included in the `STORING()` clause of <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/create-index" data-versioned="true">`CREATE INDEX`</a>. CockroachDB now checks if the column is virtual up-front, and properly detects when a column is already handled by an existing index when the column name has `UTF-8` characters. [#125208](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/125208)
- Fixed a bug where a change to a <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/create-type" data-versioned="true">user-defined type (UDT)</a> could cause queries against tables using that type to fail with an error message like: `histogram.go:694: span must be fully contained in the bucket`. The change to the user-defined type could occur either directly from an [ `ALTER TYPE` ](https://www.cockroachlabs.com/docs/v23.1/alter-type.html statement or indirectly from an <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/alter-database#add-region" data-versioned="true">`ALTER DATABASE... ADD REGION`</a> or <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/alter-database#drop-region" data-versioned="true">`ALTER DATABASE... DROP REGION`</a> statement, which implicitly modifies the `crdb_internal_region` UDT. This bug had existed since UDTs were introduced in v20.2. [#124855](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/124855)
- Fixed an issue where <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/alter-table#add-column" data-versioned="true">adding a column</a> with a default value of an empty array would not succeed. [#125328](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/125328)
- <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/alter-table#add-constraint" data-versioned="true">
    `ALTER TABLE... ADD CONSTRAINT UNIQUE`
  </a>
  will now fail with a well-formed error message and code `42601` if a statement tries to add a unique constraint on an
  expression. [#125420](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/125420)
- Fixed a bug in v24.1, v23.2, and v23.1 where using <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cluster-settings#setting-changefeed-aggregator-flush-jitter" data-versioned="true">`changefeed.aggregator.flush_jitter`</a> with <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/create-changefeed#min-checkpoint-frequency" data-versioned="true">`min_checkpoint_frequency`</a> set to zero could cause panics. [#125495](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/125495)
- Fixed a bug in which constant `LIKE` patterns containing certain sequences of backslashes did not become constrained scans. This bug has been present since v21.1.13 when support for building constrained scans from `LIKE` patterns containing backslashes was added. [#125537](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/125537)
- Fixed a bug that could cause calling a routine to return an unexpected `function... does not exist` error. The bug is triggered when the routine is called twice using the exact same SQL query, and either: (a) the routine has polymorphic arguments, or: (b) in between the two calls, the routine is replaced by a routine with the same name and different parameters. This bug had existed since alpha versions of v23.1. [#123513](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/123513)
- Fixed the statistics estimation code in the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cost-based-optimizer" data-versioned="true">optimizer</a> so it does not use the empty histograms produced if histogram collection has been disabled during statistics collection due to excessive memory utilization. Now the optimizer will rely on distinct counts instead of the empty histograms and should produce better plans as a result. This bug had existed since v22.1. [#126158](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/126158)

### Contributors

This release includes 56 merged PRs by 27 authors.

## v23.1.23

Release Date: June 20, 2024

### Downloads

<Note>
  Experimental downloads are not qualified for production use and not eligible for support or uptime SLA commitments,
  whether they are for testing releases or production releases.
</Note>

<table>

### Docker image

[Multi-platform images](https://docs.docker.com/build/building/multi-platform) include support for both Intel and ARM. Multi-platform images do not take up additional space on your Docker host.

Within the multi-platform image, both Intel and ARM images are **generally available** for production use.

To download the Docker image:

```shell
docker pull cockroachdb/cockroach:v23.1.23
```

### Source tag

To view or download the source code for CockroachDB v23.1.23 on Github, visit [v23.1.23 source tag](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/releases/tag/v23.1.23).

### Changelog

View a detailed changelog on GitHub: [v23.1.22...v23.1.23](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/compare/v23.1.22...v23.1.23)

### Enterprise edition changes

- Fixed a bug that was present since v22.2 where <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/change-data-capture-overview" data-versioned="true">changefeeds</a> with long-running <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/create-changefeed#initial-scan" data-versioned="true">initial scans</a> might incorrectly restore checkpoint job progress and drop events during <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/changefeed-messages#duplicate-messages" data-versioned="true">changefeed restarts</a> due to transient errors or node restarts. The bug was most likely to occur in clusters with the following contributing factors:
  - The <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cluster-settings" data-versioned="true">cluster settings</a> `changefeed.frontier_checkpoint_frequency` and `changefeed.frontier_highwater_lag_checkpoint_threshold` were set low, which resulted in the initial scan taking many multiples of the configured frequency to complete.
  - There were multiple target tables with significant differences in row counts in one changefeed.
  - The changefeed target tables were large with many ranges.
  - The initial scan took a long time to complete (an hour or longer). [#123970](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/123970) [#124759](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/124759)
- Introduced the `changefeed.random_replica_selection.enabled` <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cluster-settings" data-versioned="true">cluster setting</a> that changes the behavior of changefeed planning work distribution. When `changefeed.random_replica_selection.enabled` is set to `true`, <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/change-data-capture-overview" data-versioned="true">changefeeds</a> will evenly distribute their work across all <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/architecture/glossary#replica" data-versioned="true">replicas</a>, including <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/architecture/replication-layer#raft" data-versioned="true">followers</a>, regardless of <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/architecture/glossary#leaseholder" data-versioned="true">leaseholder</a> placement. `changefeed.random_replica_selection.enabled` is disabled by default. [#124930](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/124930)

### SQL language changes

- Introduced three new <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cluster-settings" data-versioned="true">cluster settings</a> for controlling <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/show-statistics#display-forecasted-statistics" data-versioned="true">table statistics forecasting</a>:
  - <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cluster-settings" data-versioned="true">
      `sql.stats.forecasts.min_observations`
    </a>
    is the minimum number of observed statistics required to produce a forecast.
  - <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cluster-settings" data-versioned="true">
      `sql.stats.forecasts.min_goodness_of_fit`
    </a>
    is the minimum R² (goodness of fit) measurement required from all predictive models to use a forecast.
  - <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cluster-settings" data-versioned="true">
      `sql.stats.forecasts.max_decrease`
    </a>
    is the most a prediction can decrease, expressed as the minimum ratio of the prediction to the lowest prior
    observation. [#124076](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/124076)
- Added a new <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/session-variables" data-versioned="true">session setting</a> `optimizer_use_improved_multi_column_selectivity_estimate`, which if enabled, causes the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cost-based-optimizer" data-versioned="true">optimizer</a> to use an improved selectivity estimate for multi-column predicates. This setting will default to `true` on v24.2 and later, and `false` on earlier versions. [#124076](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/124076)
- The <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/row-level-ttl" data-versioned="true">row-level TTL</a> setting <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/row-level-ttl#ttl-storage-parameters" data-versioned="true">`ttl_delete_rate_limit`</a> is now set to `100` by default, which sets the rate limit for deleting expired rows to `100`. [#124362](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/124362)
- CockroachDB no longer limits precision when converting <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/architecture/glossary#data-types" data-versioned="true">spatial data types</a> to <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/jsonb" data-versioned="true">JSON</a>. [#124534](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/124534)

### Operational changes

- - The `client_authentication_ok` and `client_session_end` events are now logged to the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/logging-use-cases#sessions" data-versioned="true">`SESSIONS` log channel</a> unconditionally. Previously, these would only be logged if the `server.auth_log.sql_sessions.enabled` <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cluster-settings" data-versioned="true">cluster setting</a> was set to `true`. All other `SESSIONS` log messages are still only logged if `server.auth_log.sql_sessions.enabled` or `server.auth_log.sql_connections.enabled` are set to `true`. To not show `client_authentication_ok` and `client_session_end` events, disable the `SESSIONS` log channel entirely. [#124375](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/124375)

### DB Console changes

- Viewing the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/ui-statements-page#statement-fingerprints-results" data-versioned="true">**SQL Activity**</a> sorted by `% of Runtime` now correctly sorts entries by the runtime amount. [#123899](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/123899)
- The <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/ui-overview" data-versioned="true">DB Console</a> favicon and other image files now render properly. [#122702](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/122702)

### Bug fixes

- Fixed a bug where a failed <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/restore" data-versioned="true">restore</a> job could leave the system in a state where re-attempting the restore was not possible without manual intervention. [#123462](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/123462)
- <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/ui-databases-page#index-recommendations" data-versioned="true">
    Index recommendations
  </a>
  in the
  <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/ui-overview" data-versioned="true">
    DB Console
  </a>
  will now function properly for indexes on tables or columns whose names contain quotation marks or whitespace. For
  example: `CREATE INDEX ON "my table" ("my col");`. [#122117](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/122117)
- Fixed a bug introduced in v23.1 where <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/authentication#client-authentication" data-versioned="true">client certificate authentication</a> combined with <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/sso-sql#identity-map-configuration" data-versioned="true">identity maps</a> ( `server.identity_map.configuration` ) did not work. For the feature to work correctly, the client must specify a valid database user in the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/connection-parameters" data-versioned="true">connection string</a>. [#124076](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/124076)
- Statistics forecasts of zero rows can cause suboptimal <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cost-based-optimizer" data-versioned="true">query plans</a>. Forecasting will now avoid predicting zero rows for most downward-trending statistics. [#124076](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/124076)
- Fixed a bug where <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/drop-role" data-versioned="true">`DROP ROLE`</a> and <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/drop-user" data-versioned="true">`DROP USER`</a> could leave references behind inside <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/create-type" data-versioned="true">`TYPE`s</a>, which could prevent <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/show-grants" data-versioned="true">`SHOW GRANTS`</a> from working. [#124645](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/124645)
- Scattering a range with a replication factor of 1 now no longer erroneously up-replicates the range to two replicas. Leases will also no longer thrash between nodes when perturbed with a replication factor of 1. [#124500](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/124500)
- Fixed a bug where, if the `ttl_row_stats_poll_interval` storage parameter was non-zero for a table with <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/row-level-ttl" data-versioned="true">row-level TTL</a> enabled, the queries issued to update row statistics could block the job from completing. Now, if the job completes, these statistics queries are cancelled. This means that the `jobs.row_level_ttl.total_rows` and `jobs.row_level_ttl.total_expired_rows` metrics will report `0` if the job finishes before the row stats queries complete. [#124625](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/124625)
- Fixed a bug where the `results_buffer_size` <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/session-variables" data-versioned="true">session variable</a> could not be configured by using the "options" query parameter in the connection string, but only as a top-level query parameter. Now, `results_buffer_size` can be configured in either part of the connection string. This variable still cannot be changed with the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/set-vars" data-versioned="true">`SET`</a> command after the session begins. [#124773](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/124773)
- <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/show-types" data-versioned="true">
    `SHOW TYPES`
  </a>
  now includes user-defined
  <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/create-type#create-a-composite-data-type" data-versioned="true">
    composite types
  </a>
  . `SHOW TYPES` previously omitted composite types, which were added in v23.1.0.
  [#124815](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/124815)
- Fixed a bug where a change to a <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/create-type" data-versioned="true">user-defined type</a> could cause queries against tables using that type to fail with the error `histogram.go:694: span must be fully contained in the bucket`. The change to the user-defined type could come directly from an <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/alter-type" data-versioned="true">`ALTER TYPE`</a> statement, or indirectly from an <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/alter-database#add-region" data-versioned="true">`ALTER DATABASE ADD REGION`</a> or <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/alter-database#drop-region" data-versioned="true">`DROP REGION`</a> statement (which implicitly change the `crdb_internal_region` type). This bug was present since user-defined types were introduced in v20.2. [#125473](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/125473)

### Performance improvements

- More efficient <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cost-based-optimizer" data-versioned="true">query plans</a> are now generated for queries with text similarity filters, for example, `text_col % 'foobar'`. These plans are generated if the `optimizer_use_trigram_similarity_optimization` <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/session-variables" data-versioned="true">session setting</a> is enabled. It is disabled by default. [#124076](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/124076)
- Added a new <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/session-variables" data-versioned="true">session setting</a> `optimizer_use_improved_zigzag_join_costing`. When enabled and when the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cluster-settings" data-versioned="true">cluster setting</a> `enable_zigzag_join` is also enabled, the cost of zigzag joins is updated such that a zigzag join will be chosen over a scan only if it produces fewer rows than a scan. [#124076](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/124076)
- Improved the selectivity estimation of multi-column filters when the multi-column distinct count is high. This prevents the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cost-based-optimizer" data-versioned="true">optimizer</a> from choosing a suboptimal query plan due to over-estimating the selectivity of a multi-column predicate. [#124076](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/124076)

### Contributors

This release includes 48 merged PRs by 23 authors.

### Docker image

[Multi-platform images](https://docs.docker.com/build/building/multi-platform) include support for both Intel and ARM. Multi-platform images do not take up additional space on your Docker host.

Within the multi-platform image, both Intel and ARM images are **generally available** for production use.

To download the Docker image:

```shell
docker pull cockroachdb/cockroach:v23.1.22
```

### Source tag

To view or download the source code for CockroachDB v23.1.22 on Github, visit [v23.1.22 source tag](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/releases/tag/v23.1.22).

### Changelog

View a detailed changelog on GitHub: [v23.1.21...v23.1.22](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/compare/v23.1.21...v23.1.22)

### Enterprise edition changes

- Fixed a bug that was present since v22.2 where <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/change-data-capture-overview" data-versioned="true">changefeeds</a> with long-running <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/create-changefeed#initial-scan" data-versioned="true">initial scans</a> might incorrectly restore checkpoint job progress and drop events during <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/changefeed-messages#duplicate-messages" data-versioned="true">changefeed restarts</a> due to transient errors or node restarts. The bug was most likely to occur in clusters with the following contributing factors:
  - The `changefeed.shutdown_checkpoint.enabled` <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cluster-settings" data-versioned="true">cluster setting</a> was enabled.
  - The cluster settings `changefeed.frontier_checkpoint_frequency` and `low changefeed.frontier_highwater_lag_checkpoint_threshold` were set low, which resulted in the initial scan taking many multiples of the configured frequency to complete.
  - There were multiple target tables with significant differences in row counts in one changefeed.
  - The changefeed target tables were large with many ranges.
  - The initial scan took a long time to complete (an hour or longer). [#124454](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/124454)

### SQL language changes

- Updated the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/show-grants" data-versioned="true">`SHOW GRANTS`</a> responses to display the `object_type` and `object_name`, which has replaced the `relation_name` column. [#122718](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/122718)
- Added <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/create-external-connection" data-versioned="true">external connection</a> granted privileges to the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/show-grants" data-versioned="true">`SHOW GRANTS`</a> command. [#122718](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/122718)
- Introduced three new <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cluster-settings" data-versioned="true">cluster settings</a> for controlling table statistics forecasting:
  - <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cluster-settings" data-versioned="true">
      `sql.stats.forecasts.min_observations`
    </a>
    is the minimum number of observed statistics required to produce a forecast.
  - <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cluster-settings" data-versioned="true">
      `sql.stats.forecasts.min_goodness_of_fit`
    </a>
    is the minimum R² (goodness of fit) measurement required from all predictive models to use a forecast.
  - <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cluster-settings" data-versioned="true">
      `sql.stats.forecasts.max_decrease`
    </a>
    is the most a prediction can decrease, expressed as the minimum ratio of the prediction to the lowest prior
    observation. [#122594](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/122594)
- Added a new <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/session-variables" data-versioned="true">session setting</a> `optimizer_use_improved_multi_column_selectivity_estimate`, which if enabled, causes the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cost-based-optimizer" data-versioned="true">optimizer</a> to use an improved selectivity estimate for multi-column predicates. This setting will default to `true` on v24.2 and later, and `false` on earlier versions. [#123083](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/123083)

### Command-line changes

- Changed the default `debug compact` maximum compaction concurrency to the number of processors, and added a `--max-concurrency` flag for overriding the new default. [#123070](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/123070)

### Bug fixes

- Fixed a bug where a <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/restore" data-versioned="true">`RESTORE`</a> of a backup that itself contained a table created by the `RESTORE` of a table with an in-progress <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/import-into" data-versioned="true">`IMPORT INTO`</a> would fail to restore all rows. [#120542](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/120542)
- Fixed a bug where <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/authentication#client-authentication" data-versioned="true">client certificate authentication</a> combined with <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/sso-sql#identity-map-configuration" data-versioned="true">identity maps</a> ( `server.identity_map.configuration` ) did not work. For the feature to work correctly, the client must specify a valid database user in the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/connection-parameters" data-versioned="true">connection string</a>. [#122747](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/122747)
- Fixed a bug where the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/architecture/sql-layer#query-execution" data-versioned="true">row-based execution engine</a> could drop a <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/limit-offset" data-versioned="true">`LIMIT`</a> clause when there was an <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/order-by" data-versioned="true">`ORDER BY`</a> clause, and the ordering was partially provided by an input operator. For example, this bug could occur with an ordering such as `ORDER BY a, b` when the scanned index was only ordered on column `a`. The impact of this bug was that more rows may have been returned than specified by the `LIMIT` clause. This bug is only present when not using the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/architecture/sql-layer#vectorized-query-execution" data-versioned="true">vectorized execution engine</a>. That is, when running with `SET vectorize = off;`. This bug has existed since CockroachDB v22.1. [#122835](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/122835)
- Statistics forecasts of zero rows can cause suboptimal <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cost-based-optimizer" data-versioned="true">query plans</a>. Forecasting will now avoid predicting zero rows for most downward-trending statistics. [#122594](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/122594)
- Fixed a bug in the DB Console's <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/ui-custom-chart-debug-page" data-versioned="true">**Custom Chart**</a> tool where store-level metrics were displayed only for the first store ID associated with the node. Now data is displayed for all stores present on a node, and a single time series is shown for each store, rather than an aggregated value for all of the node's stores. This allows finer-grained monitoring of store-level metrics. [#122806](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/122806)
- Fixed a bug where a <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/show-jobs" data-versioned="true">job</a> would fail if it reported an out-of-bound progress fraction. The error is now logged and no longer causes the job to fail. [#122963](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/122963)
- Fixed a bug where, in certain cases, using virtual tables such as `crdb_internal.system_jobs` could result in the internal error `attempting to append refresh spans after the tracked timestamp has moved forward`. [#123154](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/123154)

### Performance improvements

- More efficient <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cost-based-optimizer" data-versioned="true">query plans</a> are now generated for queries with text similarity filters, for example, `text_col % 'foobar'`. These plans are generated if the `optimizer_use_trigram_similarity_optimization` <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/set-vars" data-versioned="true">session setting</a> is enabled. It is disabled by default. [#122723](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/122723)
- The <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cost-based-optimizer" data-versioned="true">optimizer</a> now costs `distinct-on` operators more accurately. It may produce more efficient query plans in some cases. [#122851](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/122851)
- Added a new <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/session-variables" data-versioned="true">session setting</a> `optimizer_use_improved_zigzag_join_costing`. When enabled and when the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cluster-settings" data-versioned="true">cluster setting</a> `enable_zigzag_join` is also enabled, the cost of zigzag joins is updated such that a zigzag join will be chosen over a scan only if it produces fewer rows than a scan. [#123083](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/123083)
- Improved the selectivity estimation of multi-column filters when the multi-column distinct count is high. This prevents the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cost-based-optimizer" data-versioned="true">optimizer</a> from choosing a bad query plan due to over-estimating the selectivity of a multi-column predicate. [#123083](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/123083)
- Improved the efficiency of error handling in the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/vectorized-execution" data-versioned="true">vectorized execution engine</a> to reduce the CPU overhead of statement timeout handling and reduce the potential for more statement timeouts. [#123503](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/123503)

### Contributors

This release includes 51 merged PRs by 23 authors.

### Docker image

[Multi-platform images](https://docs.docker.com/build/building/multi-platform) include support for both Intel and ARM. Multi-platform images do not take up additional space on your Docker host.

Within the multi-platform image, both Intel and ARM images are **generally available** for production use.

To download the Docker image:

```shell
docker pull cockroachdb/cockroach:v23.1.21
```

### Source tag

To view or download the source code for CockroachDB v23.1.21 on Github, visit [v23.1.21 source tag](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/releases/tag/v23.1.21).

### Changelog

View a detailed changelog on GitHub: [v23.1.20...v23.1.21](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/compare/v23.1.20...v23.1.21)

### SQL language changes

- The `FORCE_INVERTED_INDEX` hint causes the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cost-based-optimizer" data-versioned="true">optimizer</a> to prefer a query plan scan over any <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/inverted-indexes" data-versioned="true">inverted index</a> of the hinted table. An error is emitted if no such query plan can be generated. [#122301](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/122301)
- Introduced three new <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cluster-settings" data-versioned="true">cluster settings</a> for controlling <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cost-based-optimizer#table-statistics" data-versioned="true">table statistics</a> forecasting:
  - <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cluster-settings" data-versioned="true">
      `sql.stats.forecasts.min_observations`
    </a>
    is the minimum number of observed statistics required to produce a forecast.
  - <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cluster-settings" data-versioned="true">
      `sql.stats.forecasts.min_goodness_of_fit`
    </a>
    is the minimum R² (goodness of fit) measurement required from all predictive models to use a forecast.
  - <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cluster-settings" data-versioned="true">
      `sql.stats.forecasts.max_decrease`
    </a>
    is the most a prediction can decrease, expressed as the minimum ratio of the prediction to the lowest prior
    observation. [#122990](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/122990)
- Added a <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/set-vars" data-versioned="true">session variable</a> `optimizer_use_improved_multi_column_selectivity_estimate`, which if enabled, causes the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cost-based-optimizer" data-versioned="true">optimizer</a> to use an improved selectivity estimate for multi-column predicates. This setting will default to `true` on v24.2 and later, and `false` on prior versions. [#123068](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/123068)

### Operational changes

- A minimum <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/architecture/replication-layer#raft" data-versioned="true">Raft scheduler</a> concurrency is now enforced per <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/architecture/storage-layer#overview" data-versioned="true">store</a> so that nodes with many stores do not spread workers too thinly. This helps to avoid high scheduler latency across replicas on a store when load is imbalanced. [#120797](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/120797)

### Bug fixes

- Fixed a bug introduced in v22.2.9 that could cause a slow memory leak that can accumulate when opening many new connections. [#121056](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/121056)
- <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/create-sequence" data-versioned="true">
    Sequence
  </a>
  options for `NO MINVALUE` and `NO MAXVALUE` now match [PostgreSQL
  behavior](https://www.postgresql.org/docs/current/sql-createsequence). Sequence `MINVALUE` and `MAXVALUE` now
  automatically adjust to the bounds of a new integer type in
  <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/alter-sequence" data-versioned="true">
    `ALTER SEQUENCE... AS`
  </a>
  , matching PostgreSQL behavior. [#121307](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/121307)
- Fixed a bug where the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/ui-statements-page#charts" data-versioned="true">timeseries graphs shown on the **SQL Activity Statement Fingerprint** page</a> in the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/ui-overview" data-versioned="true">DB Console</a> were not rendering properly. This involved fixing a bug related to setting the time range of the charts. [#121382](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/121382) [#122235](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/122235)
- Fixed a bug where CockroachDB could incorrectly evaluate `IN` expressions that had `INT2` or `INT4` type on the left side, and values on the right side that were outside the range of the left side. The bug had been present since at least v21.1. [#121955](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/121955)
- Previously, on long-running <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/show-sessions" data-versioned="true">sessions</a> that issue many (hundreds of thousands or more) <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/transactions" data-versioned="true">transactions</a>, CockroachDB's internal memory accounting system, the limit for which is configured via the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cockroach-start#general" data-versioned="true">`--max-sql-memory` flag</a> could leak. This bug, in turn, could result in the error message `"root: memory budget exceeded"` for other queries. The bug was present in v23.1.17 and is now fixed. [#121949](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/121949) [#122235](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/122235)
- Reintroduced <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cluster-settings" data-versioned="true">cluster setting</a> `sql.auth.modify_cluster_setting_applies_to_all.enabled` so that mixed-version clusters can migrate off of this setting, which is deprecated in favor of the privilege <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/set-cluster-setting#required-privileges" data-versioned="true">`MODIFYSQLCLUSTERSETTING`</a>. [#122055](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/122055) [#122635](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/122635)
- Fixed a bug where a <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/grant" data-versioned="true">`GRANT... ON ALL TABLES`</a> statement could fail if sequences existed and they did not support a privilege (e.g., `BACKUP` ). [#122057](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/122057)
- Fixed a bug where <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/authentication#client-authentication" data-versioned="true">client certificate authentication</a> combined with <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/sso-sql#identity-map-configuration" data-versioned="true">identity maps</a> ( `server.identity_map.configuration` ) did not work. For the feature to work correctly, the client must specify a valid database user in the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/connection-parameters" data-versioned="true">connection string</a>. This bug had been present since v23.1. [#122746](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/122746)
- Statistics forecasts of zero rows can cause suboptimal <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cost-based-optimizer" data-versioned="true">query plans</a>. Forecasting will now avoid predicting zero rows for most downward-trending statistics. [#122990](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/122990)

### Performance improvements

- More efficient <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cost-based-optimizer" data-versioned="true">query plans</a> are now generated for queries with text similarity filters, for example, `text_col % 'foobar'`. These plans are generated if the `optimizer_use_trigram_similarity_optimization` <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/set-vars" data-versioned="true">session setting</a> is enabled. It is disabled by default. [#122683](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/122683)
- Added a new <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/set-vars" data-versioned="true">session variable</a> `optimizer_use_improved_zigzag_join_costing`. When enabled, the cost of <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cost-based-optimizer#zigzag-joins" data-versioned="true">zigzag joins</a> is updated so zigzag joins will only be chosen over scans if the zigzag joins produce fewer rows. This change only applies if the session variable `enable_zigzag_join` is also `on`. [#123068](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/123068)
- Improved the selectivity estimation of multi-column filters by the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cost-based-optimizer" data-versioned="true">optimizer</a> when the multi-column distinct count is high. This avoids cases where CockroachDB significantly over-estimates the selectivity of a multi-column predicate and as a result can prevent the optimizer from choosing a bad query plan. [#123068](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/123068)

### Contributors

This release includes 59 merged PRs by 26 authors.

          cockroach-v23.1.20.darwin-11.0-arm64.tgz

          cockroach-sql-v23.1.20.darwin-11.0-arm64.tgz
        </a>
        <br />(
        <a href="https://binaries.cockroachdb.com/cockroach-sql-v23.1.20.darwin-11.0-arm64.tgz.sha256sum">SHA256</a>)
      </td>
    </tr>
    <tr>
      <td>
        Windows
        <br />
        (Experimental)
      </td>
      <td>Intel</td>
      <td>
        <a href="https://binaries.cockroachdb.com/cockroach-v23.1.20.windows-6.2-amd64.zip">
          cockroach-v23.1.20.windows-6.2-amd64.zip
        </a>
        <br />(<a href="https://binaries.cockroachdb.com/cockroach-v23.1.20.windows-6.2-amd64.zip.sha256sum">SHA256</a>)

        <a href="https://binaries.cockroachdb.com/cockroach-sql-v23.1.20.windows-6.2-amd64.zip">
          cockroach-sql-v23.1.20.windows-6.2-amd64.zip
        </a>
        <br />(
        <a href="https://binaries.cockroachdb.com/cockroach-sql-v23.1.20.windows-6.2-amd64.zip.sha256sum">SHA256</a>)
      </td>

### Docker image

[Multi-platform images](https://docs.docker.com/build/building/multi-platform) include support for both Intel and ARM. Multi-platform images do not take up additional space on your Docker host.

Within the multi-platform image, both Intel and ARM images are **generally available** for production use.

To download the Docker image:

```shell
docker pull cockroachdb/cockroach:v23.1.20
```

### Source tag

To view or download the source code for CockroachDB v23.1.20 on Github, visit [v23.1.20 source tag](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/releases/tag/v23.1.20).

### Changelog

View a detailed changelog on GitHub: [v23.1.19...v23.1.20](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/compare/v23.1.19...v23.1.20)

### SQL language changes

- Added a <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/set-vars" data-versioned="true">session variable</a> `optimizer_use_improved_multi_column_selectivity_estimate`, which if enabled, causes the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cost-based-optimizer" data-versioned="true">optimizer</a> to use an improved selectivity estimate for multi-column predicates. This setting will default to `true` on versions 24.2+, and `false` on prior versions. [#123152](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/123152)
- Added three new <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cluster-settings" data-versioned="true">cluster settings</a> for controlling <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cost-based-optimizer#table-statistics" data-versioned="true">optimizer table statistics</a> forecasting:
  1. `sql.stats.forecasts.min_observations` is the minimum number of observed statistics required to produce a forecast.
  2. `sql.stats.forecasts.min_goodness_of_fit` is the minimum R² (goodness of fit) measurement required from all predictive models to use a forecast.
  3. `sql.stats.forecasts.max_decrease` is the most a prediction can decrease, expressed as the minimum ratio of the prediction to the lowest prior observation. [#123149](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/123149)

### Bug fixes

- Statistics forecasts of zero rows by <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cost-based-optimizer#table-statistics" data-versioned="true">the optimizer</a> can cause bad plans. This commit changes forecasting to avoid predicting zero rows for most downward-trending statistics. [#123149](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/123149)
- A <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/show-jobs" data-versioned="true">job</a> will now <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/logging#ops" data-versioned="true">log</a> rather than fail if it reports an out-of bound progress fraction. [#123133](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/123133)

### Performance improvements

- Added a new <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/set-vars" data-versioned="true">session variable</a> `optimizer_use_improved_zigzag_join_costing`. When enabled, the cost of <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cost-based-optimizer#zigzag-joins" data-versioned="true">zigzag joins</a> is updated so zigzag joins will only be chosen over scans if the zigzag joins produce fewer rows. This change only applies if the session variable `enable_zigzag_join` is also `on`. [#123152](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/123152)
- Improved the selectivity estimation of multi-column filters by the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cost-based-optimizer" data-versioned="true">optimizer</a> when the multi-column distinct count is high. This avoids cases where CockroachDB significantly over-estimates the selectivity of a multi-column predicate and as a result can prevent the optimizer from choosing a bad query plan. [#123152](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/123152)

### Contributors

This release includes 5 merged PRs by 5 authors.

### Bug fixes

- Reintroduced <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cluster-settings" data-versioned="true">cluster setting</a> `sql.auth.modify_cluster_setting_applies_to_all.enabled` so that mixed-version clusters can migrate off of this setting, which is deprecated in favor of the privilege <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/set-cluster-setting#required-privileges" data-versioned="true">`MODIFYSQLCLUSTERSETTING`</a>. [#122455](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/122455)
