### Docker image

[Multi-platform images](https://docs.docker.com/build/building/multi-platform) include support for both Intel and ARM. Multi-platform images do not take up additional space on your Docker host.

Within the multi-platform image, both Intel and ARM images are **generally available** for production use.

To download the Docker image:

```shell
docker pull cockroachdb/cockroach:v23.1.18
```

### Source tag

To view or download the source code for CockroachDB v23.1.18 on Github, visit [v23.1.18 source tag](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/releases/tag/v23.1.18).

### Changelog

View a detailed changelog on GitHub: [v23.1.17...v23.1.18](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/compare/v23.1.17...v23.1.18)

### SQL language changes

- Fixed an oversight where CockroachDB was allowing mutation statements (such as <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/update" data-versioned="true">`UPDATE`</a> or <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/delete" data-versioned="true">`DELETE`</a> ) and locking statements (such as <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/select-for-update" data-versioned="true">`SELECT... FOR UPDATE`</a> ) in implicit single-statement <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/transactions" data-versioned="true">transactions</a> using <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/as-of-system-time" data-versioned="true">`AS OF SYSTEM TIME`</a>. [#120159](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/120159)

### Operational changes

- The `admission.kv.bulk_only.enabled` <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cluster-settings" data-versioned="true">cluster setting</a>, when set to `true`, only skips store-level <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/admission-control" data-versioned="true">admission control</a> for normal priority work, and continues to subject the work to CPU admission control. [#119173](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/119173)

### DB Console changes

- Resolved an issue where clusters with multiple <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cockroach-start#store" data-versioned="true">stores</a> per node could list inaccurate region/node information on the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/ui-databases-page" data-versioned="true">Databases Page</a>. [#120234](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/120234)
- Fixed a bug where the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/ui-statements-page#charts" data-versioned="true">timeseries graphs shown on the **SQL Activity Statement Fingerprint** page</a> in <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/ui-overview" data-versioned="true">DB Console</a> were not rendering properly. This involved fixing a bug related to setting the time range of the charts. [#121783](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/121783)

### Bug fixes

- Previously, on long-running <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/show-sessions" data-versioned="true">sessions</a> that issue many (hundreds of thousands or more) <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/transactions" data-versioned="true">transactions</a>, CockroachDB's internal memory accounting system, the limit for which is configured via the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cockroach-start#general" data-versioned="true">`--max-sql-memory` flag</a> ), could leak. This bug, in turn, could result in the error message `"root: memory budget exceeded"` for other queries. The bug was present in v23.1.17 and is now fixed. [#121874](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/121874)
- Fix a bug where running <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/restore" data-versioned="true">`RESTORE`</a> on certain <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/backup-and-restore-overview" data-versioned="true">backups</a> would open a very large number of connections to the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/use-cloud-storage" data-versioned="true">backup storage provider</a>. [#119925](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/119925)
- A user with the `VIEWACTIVITYREDACTED` <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/security-reference/authorization#managing-privileges" data-versioned="true">privilege</a> can no longer see constants inside of queries that originate from other <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/security-reference/authorization#roles" data-versioned="true">users</a> in the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/show-sessions" data-versioned="true">`SHOW SESSIONS`</a> result. Previously, this redaction did not occur. [#119963](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/119963)
- Previously, the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/show-statements#aliases" data-versioned="true">`SHOW QUERIES`</a> and <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/show-statements" data-versioned="true">`SHOW STATEMENTS`</a> required the user to have the `VIEWACTIVITY` or `VIEWACTIVITYREDACTED` <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/security-reference/authorization#managing-privileges" data-versioned="true">privilege</a>. However, a user should always be able to view their own queries, even without these privileges. This is now fixed. [#119963](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/119963)
- Fixed a bug in which it was possible to `SET transaction_read_only = false` during an <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/as-of-system-time" data-versioned="true">`AS OF SYSTEM TIME`</a> transaction. [#120159](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/120159)
- Fixed a slow memory leak that could accumulate when opening many new <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/connection-pooling" data-versioned="true">connections</a>. The bug was present in v22.2.9+ and v23.1+. [#120242](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/120242)
- Users will no longer see <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/views" data-versioned="true">views</a> displayed on the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/ui-databases-page" data-versioned="true">**Databases** page</a> in <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/ui-overview" data-versioned="true">DB Console</a>. Previously, views would be listed with no information, only displaying errors. [#120213](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/120213)

### Performance improvements

- Enabled the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/admission-control" data-versioned="true">admission control</a> CPU limiter for <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/row-level-ttl" data-versioned="true">row-level TTL</a> to reduce latency impact from CPU-intensive scans issued as part of <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/row-level-ttl#view-scheduled-ttl-jobs" data-versioned="true">row-level TTL jobs</a>. [#120516](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/120516)

### Contributors

This release includes 45 merged PRs by 27 authors.

### Docker image

[Multi-platform images](https://docs.docker.com/build/building/multi-platform) include support for both Intel and ARM. Multi-platform images do not take up additional space on your Docker host.

Within the multi-platform image, both Intel and ARM images are **generally available** for production use.

To download the Docker image:

```shell
docker pull cockroachdb/cockroach:v23.1.17
```

### Source tag

To view or download the source code for CockroachDB v23.1.17 on Github, visit [v23.1.17 source tag](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/releases/tag/v23.1.17).

### Changelog

View a detailed changelog on GitHub: [v23.1.16...v23.1.17](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/compare/v23.1.16...v23.1.17)

### Security updates

- A user with the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/security-reference/authorization#supported-privileges" data-versioned="true">`VIEWACTIVITY` privilege</a> can now request a statement bundle from the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/ui-statements-page" data-versioned="true">**Statements** page</a> in the DB Console or with the internal builtin function `crdb_internal.requests_statement_bundle`. [#119638](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/119638)
- Clusters using <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/sso-sql" data-versioned="true">Cluster Single Sign-on (SSO) with JSON web tokens (JWTs)</a> can now optionally fetch signing keys from configured issuers instead of configuring static signing keys for each issuer. When the new <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cluster-settings" data-versioned="true">cluster setting</a> `server.jwt_authentication.jwks_auto_fetch.enabled` is set to `true`, signing keys are automatically fetched from the issuer using metadata published in its OpenID configuration. In this case, static signing keys in `server.jwt_authentication.jwks` are ignored. When automatic fetching is enabled, there may be a slight increase in network latency for each JWT authentication request, proportional to the latency between the cluster and the issuer's endpoint. [#120063](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/120063)
- <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/ui-overview" data-versioned="true">
    DB Console
  </a>
  cookies are marked `Secure` for the browser when the cluster is running in secure mode.
  [#119262](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/119262)
- The <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/ui-overview" data-versioned="true">DB Console</a> `session` cookie is now marked `HttpOnly` to prevent it from being read by any Javascript code. [#119262](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/119262)

### SQL language changes

- The new [cluster setting](https://cockroachlabs.com/docs/v23.1/cluster-settings) `server.max_open_transactions_per_gateway`, when set to a non-negative value, prevents users without the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/security-reference/authorization#admin-role" data-versioned="true">`admin` role</a> from executing a query if more than this number of <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/transactions" data-versioned="true">transactions</a> are open on the current <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/architecture/life-of-a-distributed-transaction#gateway" data-versioned="true">gateway node</a>. [#118949](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/118949)
- Added support for <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/table-expressions#force-index-selection" data-versioned="true">index hinting</a> with <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/insert" data-versioned="true">`INSERT`</a> and <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/upsert" data-versioned="true">`UPSERT`</a> statements. This allows `INSERT... ON CONFLICT` and `UPSERT` queries to use index hints in the same way as <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/update" data-versioned="true">`UPDATE`</a> and <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/delete" data-versioned="true">`DELETE`</a> statements. [#119600](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/119600)

### Operational changes

- You can now pass the `--include-range-info` flag when <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cockroach-debug-zip" data-versioned="true">generating a diagnostic bundle</a> to include problem ranges. [#119233](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/119233)
- In unredacted diagnostic bundles, two columns have been added to the `crdb_internal.transaction_contention_events` table:
  - `waiting_stmt_query`: the query of the statement that is waiting to run.
  - `blocking_txn_queries_unordered`: an unordered list of the blocking transaction's queries.

    [#119422](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/119422)

### DB Console changes

- The <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/ui-statements-page" data-versioned="true">**Statements** page</a> now always shows the entire selected period, instead of only the period that contains data. [#118811](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/118811)
- The <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/ui-overload-dashboard" data-versioned="true">**Overload Dashboard**</a> page now includes two additional graphs:
  - **Elastic CPU Utilization**: Shows the actual CPU used for elastic work compared with the configured limit.
  - **Elastic CPU Exhausted Duration Per Second**: Shows how much time, in milliseconds, that elastic work has been subject to CPU exhaustion. [#118908](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/118908)

### Bug fixes

- Fixed a bug where creating a <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/change-data-capture-overview" data-versioned="true">changefeed</a> that targeted tables with a zero-scale <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/decimal" data-versioned="true">`DECIMAL(n)`</a> column, `format='avro'`, and `diff` would cause a panic. [#118848](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/118848)
- Fixed a bug where a <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/change-data-capture-overview" data-versioned="true">changefeed</a> could omit events in rare cases, logging the error `cdc ux violation: detected timestamp... that is less or equal to the local frontier`. This could happen in the following scenario:
  1. A <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/create-and-configure-changefeeds#enable-rangefeeds" data-versioned="true">rangefeed</a> runs on a follower <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/architecture/glossary#cockroachdb-architecture-terms" data-versioned="true">replica</a> that lags significantly behind the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/architecture/glossary#cockroachdb-architecture-terms" data-versioned="true">leaseholder</a>.
  2. A transaction commits and removes its <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/architecture/transaction-layer#transaction-records" data-versioned="true">transaction record</a> before its <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/architecture/transaction-layer#writing" data-versioned="true">intent</a> resolution is applied on the follower.
  3. The follower's <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/architecture/transaction-layer#closed-timestamps" data-versioned="true">closed timestamp</a> has advanced past the transaction commit timestamp.
  4. The rangefeed attempts to push the transaction to a new timestamp (at least 10 seconds after the transaction began).
  5. This may cause the rangefeed to prematurely emit a checkpoint before emitting writes at lower timestamps, which in turn may cause the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/change-data-capture-overview" data-versioned="true">changefeed</a> to drop these events entirely, never emitting them.

     [#118415](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/118415)

- Fixed a bug introduced in v22.2 where queries issued by <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/row-level-ttl#view-scheduled-ttl-jobs" data-versioned="true">TTL jobs</a> did not use optimal plans. [#118496](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/118496)
- Fixed a bug introduced in v23.1.0 where a <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/node-shutdown?filters=decommission#decommission-the-node" data-versioned="true">decommissioning</a> replica that is part of a mis-replicated range could get stuck on a rebalance operation that was falsely determined to be unsafe. [#118437](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/118437)
- Fixed a bug introduced in v22.2 where adding multiple columns with <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/unique" data-versioned="true">`UNIQUE` constraints</a> in a single statement could result in the error `secondary index for backfill contains physical column not present in source primary index`. [#118137](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/118137)
- Fixed a bug where an `unable to get CPU capacity` error could be logged every 10 seconds when running outside of a CPU `cgroup`. [#118670](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/118670)
- Fixed a bug where an <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/show-jobs#show-automatic-jobs" data-versioned="true">`AUTO CREATE STATS` job</a> could cause an internal system table to grow, and this could cause slow queries related to the job system. [#118944](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/118944)
- Fixed a bug that caused a confusing error when a sequence name allocated by <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/serial" data-versioned="true">`SERIAL`</a> conflicted with an existing type name. [#118948](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/118948)
- Fixed a bug where an <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/alter-table#alter-primary-key" data-versioned="true">`ALTER PRIMARY KEY`</a> query could fail with the error `non-nullable column {x} with no value! Index scanned..` when validating a recreated <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/indexes" data-versioned="true">secondary index</a>. [#118972](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/118972)
- Fixed a bug introduced in v23.1 that could cause the internal error `attempting to append refresh spans after the tracked timestamp has moved forward` to be logged in some cases when using virtual tables such as`crdb_internal.system_jobs`. [#119186](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/119186)
- Fixed a bug in the `crdb_internal.leases` table where a deadlock in the leasing system could cause a node to become unavailable. [#119374](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/119374)
- Fixed a bug introduced in v23.1.15 where a <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/create-and-configure-changefeeds#enable-rangefeeds" data-versioned="true">rangefeed</a>-resolved timestamp could get stuck after a <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/architecture/distribution-layer#range-merges" data-versioned="true">range merge</a> if the range cache thinks the barrier spans multiple ranges. The log message `pushing old intents failed: range barrier failed, range split` is constantly emitted. [#119543](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/119543)
- Fixed a rare panic that could happen during a <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/import" data-versioned="true">`pg_dump` import</a> that contains a subquery in one of its arguments, such as a function like `SELECT addgeometrycolumn(...)`. Now, attempting to import a `pg_dump` with a function that has a subquery in one of its arguments results in an error rather than a panic. [#118611](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/118611)
- Fixed a bug in the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/changefeed-sinks#webhook-sink" data-versioned="true">webhook sink</a> where the `http` request body may not be initialized on retries, resulting in the error `http: ContentLength=... with Body length 0`. [#119495](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/119495)
- Fixed a bug where some files were not closed when inspecting backup metadata during <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/backup" data-versioned="true">`BACKUP`</a> and <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/restore" data-versioned="true">`RESTORE`</a> operations. [#119634](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/119634)
- Fixed a bug that could cause internal errors to be logged when executing an <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/export" data-versioned="true">`EXPORT`</a> statement. [#119712](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/119712)
- Fixed a bug where a <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/online-schema-changes" data-versioned="true">schema change</a> with a large number of descriptors could perform a <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/show-full-table-scans" data-versioned="true">full table scan</a> on the `system.leases` table. [#119466](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/119466)
- Fixed a bug introduced in v22.1.0 that could cause the `sql.txns.open.internal` and `sql.statements.active.internal` gauge metrics never to be updated, leading to an incorrect count of the number of transactions and statements executed by operations internal to CockroachDB. These metrics do not include operations executed by external SQL clients. [#119338](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/119338)
- Fixed a bug introduced in v22.2.9 that could cause a slow memory leak that can accumulate when opening many new connections. [#120244](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/120244)

### Contributors

This release includes 94 merged PRs by 33 authors.

### Docker image

[Multi-platform images](https://docs.docker.com/build/building/multi-platform) include support for both Intel and ARM. Multi-platform images do not take up additional space on your Docker host.

Within the multi-platform image, both Intel and ARM images are **generally available** for production use.

To download the Docker image:

```shell
docker pull cockroachdb/cockroach:v23.1.16
```

### Source tag

To view or download the source code for CockroachDB v23.1.16 on Github, visit [v23.1.16 source tag](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/releases/tag/v23.1.16).

### Changelog

View a detailed changelog on GitHub: [v23.1.15...v23.1.16](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/compare/v23.1.15...v23.1.16)

### Bug fixes

- Fixed a bug where <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/create-and-configure-changefeeds#enable-rangefeeds" data-versioned="true">rangefeed</a> resolved timestamps could get stuck, continually emitting the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/logging" data-versioned="true">log message</a> `"pushing old intents failed: range barrier failed, range split"`, typically following a <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/architecture/distribution-layer#range-merges" data-versioned="true">range merge</a>. This bug was introduced in v23.1.15. [#119559](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/119559)

### Contributors

This release includes 2 merged PRs by 2 authors.

        <a href="https://binaries.cockroachdb.com/cockroach-sql-v23.1.15.darwin-10.9-amd64.tgz">
          cockroach-sql-v23.1.15.darwin-10.9-amd64.tgz
        </a>
        <br />(
        <a href="https://binaries.cockroachdb.com/cockroach-sql-v23.1.15.darwin-10.9-amd64.tgz.sha256sum">SHA256</a>)
      </td>
    </tr>

      <td>ARM</td>

        <a href="https://binaries.cockroachdb.com/cockroach-v23.1.15.darwin-11.0-arm64.tgz">

        </a>

### Docker image

[Multi-platform images](https://docs.docker.com/build/building/multi-platform) include support for both Intel and ARM. Multi-platform images do not take up additional space on your Docker host.

Within the multi-platform image, both Intel and ARM images are **generally available** for production use.

To download the Docker image:

```shell
docker pull cockroachdb/cockroach:v23.1.15
```

### Source tag

To view or download the source code for CockroachDB v23.1.15 on Github, visit [v23.1.15 source tag](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/releases/tag/v23.1.15).

### Changelog

View a detailed changelog on GitHub: [v23.1.14...v23.1.15](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/compare/v23.1.14...v23.1.15)

### Security updates

- The <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/ui-overview" data-versioned="true">DB Console</a> `session` cookie is now marked `HttpOnly` to prevent it from being read by any Javascript code and is marked `Secure` by the browser when the cluster operates in secure mode. [#119248](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/119248)

### Bug fixes

- Fixed a bug where <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/change-data-capture-overview" data-versioned="true">changefeeds</a> that targeted schema-locked tables could fail due to an old high-water timestamp being incorrectly persisted. [#117960](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/117960)
- Fixed a bug where creating a <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/change-data-capture-overview" data-versioned="true">changefeed</a> that targeted tables with a `DECIMAL(n)` column (that is, zero-scale <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/decimal" data-versioned="true">`DECIMAL`</a> column), `format='avro'`, and `diff` would cause a panic. [#118893](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/118893)
- Fixed a bug that could cause a <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/create-changefeed" data-versioned="true">`CREATE CHANGEFEED WITH {key_column}`</a> statement to retry forever. [#116966](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/116966)
- Fixed a bug that prevented database <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/restore" data-versioned="true">restore</a> when the database contained a view or routine that referenced a user-defined type in the body string. For views, this bug was introduced in v20.2 when UDTs were introduced. For routines, this bug was introduced in v22.2 when UDFs were introduced. [#116903](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/116903)
- Fixed a durability issue in the Raft log storage mechanism due to improper synchronization of filesystem metadata, potentially leading to the loss of specific write operations ( `AddSSTable` ), notably utilized by operations such as `RESTORE`. This vulnerability was exposed only under conditions of power failure or operating system crashes, potentially causing CockroachDB to enter a crash loop upon restart. In extreme scenarios, such as a simultaneous power outage or crash across multiple nodes, it could result in an irrecoverable quorum loss. [#117383](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/117383)
- Fixed an issue in Raft log truncation that had the potential to cause crash loops and irretrievable quorum loss, especially in the rare but severe scenario where all replicas concurrently enter a crash loop. This issue emerged under conditions where the cluster was processing a bulk write operation (such as schema changes, imports, or restores), while a log truncation command was active, and the CockroachDB process experienced a crash. [#117299](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/117299)
- Fixed the total runtime value referenced in SQL stats, resolving the bug where the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/ui-overview" data-versioned="true">Console</a> erroneously displayed percentages over 100%. [#117496](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/117496)
- Fixed an issue where the values for the current and past hour in the top Activity table were calculated incorrectly, causing a missing data issue in SQL stats and, consequently, on the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/ui-overview#sql-activity" data-versioned="true">SQL Activity</a> page. [#118427](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/118427)
- Fixed a bug where CockroachDB would erroneously return an error if an empty search path parameter was encountered during search path setting. [#117556](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/117556)
- Fixed a bug in the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/row-level-ttl" data-versioned="true">Row-Level TTL</a> job that would cause it to skip expired rows if the primary key of the table included columns of the collated string type. This bug was present since the initial release of row-level TTL in v22.2.0. [#117513](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/117513)
- Fixed a bug that could cause <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/delete" data-versioned="true">`DELETE`</a> queries sent by the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/row-level-ttl" data-versioned="true">Row-Level TTL</a> job to use a secondary index rather than the primary index to find the rows to delete. This could lead to some `DELETE` operations taking a much longer time than they should. This bug was present since v22.2.0. [#118336](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/118336)
- Fixed a bug where concurrent <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/grant" data-versioned="true">`GRANT`</a> statements can cause deadlocks. [#117712](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/117712)
- Reduced the impact of bulk deletions ( <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/drop-table" data-versioned="true">`DROP TABLE`</a>, <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/truncate" data-versioned="true">`TRUNCATE`</a>, or replica removals) on foreground traffic by altering storage engine compaction priorities. [#116560](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/116560)
- Resolved an issue where DML operations would fail during the creation of a hash-sharded index, resulting in an error stating column `crdb_internal_val_shard_16` does not exist. This bug was present since v23.1.0. [#118238](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/118238)
- <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/show-jobs#show-automatic-jobs" data-versioned="true">
    `AUTO CREATE STATS`
  </a>
  jobs no longer lead to growth in an internal system table resulting in slower job-system related queries.
  [#118980](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/118980)
- <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/alter-table#alter-primary-key" data-versioned="true">`ALTER PRIMARY KEY`</a> no longer fail with an `non-nullable column <x> with no value! Index scanned..` error when validating recreated secondary indexes. [#118969](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/118969)
- Fixed a bug where CockroachDB could encounter an error `unable to encode table key: *tree.DTSQuery` when operating on columns of <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/tsquery" data-versioned="true">`TSQuery`</a> type in some contexts (e.g. when collecting table statistics or when performing a `DISTINCT` operation). The bug has been present since 23.1 when support for TSQuery type was added. [#118320](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/118320)
- Fixed a bug where in some cases CockroachDB could incorrectly evaluate queries that scanned an inverted index and had a `WHERE` filter in which two sides of the `AND` expression had "similar" expressions (e.g. `ARRAY['str1'] <@ col AND (ARRAY['str1'] && col OR...)` ). The bug has been present since pre-22.2 version. [#118359](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/118359)
- CockroachDB now correctly logs the top 5 hot ranges per cluster instead of per node. [#118371](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/118371)
- Fixed a bug where a <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/change-data-capture-overview" data-versioned="true">changefeed</a> could omit events in rare cases, logging the error `cdc ux violation: detected timestamp... that is less or equal to the local frontier`. This can happen if a <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/create-and-configure-changefeeds#enable-rangefeeds" data-versioned="true">rangefeed</a> runs on a follower replica that lags significantly behind the leaseholder, a transaction commits and removes its transaction record before its intent resolution is applied on the follower, the follower's closed timestamp has advanced past the transaction commit timestamp, and the rangefeed attempts to push the transaction to a new timestamp (at least 10 seconds after the transaction began). This may cause the rangefeed to prematurely emit a checkpoint before emitting writes at lower timestamps, which in turn may cause the changefeed to drop these events entirely, never emitting them. [#119270](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/119270)

### Contributors

This release includes 96 merged PRs by 39 authors. We would like to thank the following contributors from the CockroachDB community:

- Nikolai Vladimirov (first-time contributor)

### Docker image

[Multi-platform images](https://docs.docker.com/build/building/multi-platform) include support for both Intel and ARM. Multi-platform images do not take up additional space on your Docker host.

Within the multi-platform image, both Intel and ARM images are **generally available** for production use.

To download the Docker image:

```shell
docker pull cockroachdb/cockroach:v23.1.14
```

### Source tag

To view or download the source code for CockroachDB v23.1.14 on Github, visit [v23.1.14 source tag](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/releases/tag/v23.1.14).

### Changelog

View a detailed changelog on GitHub: [v23.1.13...v23.1.14](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/compare/v23.1.13...v23.1.14)

### SQL language changes

- CockroachDB now supports <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/import-into" data-versioned="true">importing into</a> a table that has columns typed as arrays of user-defined types (such as enums). Tables that use multiple user-defined types with the same name but different schemas are still unsupported. [#116361](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/116361)
- Added a new field, `StmtPosInTxn`, to the `CommonSQLExecDetails` (included in SQL audit logs, SQL execution logs, and telemetry events) to represent the statement's index (position) in the transaction. The first statement's `StmtPosInTxn` is `1`. [#116558](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/116558)

### Operational changes

- Updated the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cluster-settings#settings" data-versioned="true">`changefeed.lagging_ranges_threshold`</a> and <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cluster-settings#settings" data-versioned="true">`changefeed.lagging_ranges_polling_interval`</a> cluster settings to be public in v23.1. [#115803](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/115803)

### DB Console changes

- The <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/ui-cluster-overview-page" data-versioned="true">**Cluster Overview** page</a> now correctly renders the background color for email signups, fixing an issue where it was difficult to read the text. [#114546](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/114546)
- Updated the **CPU Time** label to **SQL CPU Time** on the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/ui-overview-dashboard" data-versioned="true">Overview page</a> and clarified the tooltip. [#116448](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/116448)
- Fixed an issue where the following `AggHistogram`-powered metrics reported quantiles incorrectly in the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/ui-overview-dashboard" data-versioned="true">Overview page</a>. The list of affected metrics is:
  - `changefeed.message_size_hist`
  - `changefeed.parallel_io_queue_nanos`
  - `changefeed.sink_batch_hist_nanos`
  - `changefeed.flush_hist_nanos`
  - `changefeed.commit_latency`
  - `changefeed.admit_latency`
  - `jobs.row_level_ttl.span_total_duration`
  - `jobs.row_level_ttl.select_duration`
  - `jobs.row_level_ttl.delete_duration`

    This bug affected only DB Console dashboards and not the Prometheus-compatible endpoint `/_status/vars`. [#114747](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/114747)

- In the **SQL Activity Transaction Details** page, you can now view a transaction fingerprint ID across multiple applications by passing a comma-separated encoded string of transaction fingerprint IDs in the `appNames` URL search parameter. [#116102](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/116102)

### Bug fixes

- Fixed a bug in in the TimeScale component's **Now** button behavior that could prevent charts from updating after a custom time range was selected. [#115513](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/115513)
- Fixed a bug where an active replication report update could get stuck in a retry loop on clusters with over 10000 ranges, which would prevent a node from shutting down cleanly. [#114242](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/114242)
- Fixed a nil pointer dereference bug in the error handling for `GetFiles`. [#114829](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/114829)
- Fixed a bug that prevented the **SQL Activity** page from showing internal statements when the `sql.stats.response.show_internal.enabled` <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cluster-settings" data-versioned="true">cluster setting</a> was set to `true`. [#114819](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/114819)
- Fixed a bug that could cause a discrepancy between computed statistics and the stored value for statics when a delete was rolled back. [#113772](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/113772)
- Fixed a bug introduced in v23.1 that could cause an internal error Previously, CockroachDB could encounter an internal error when using a prepared statement using the `text` format with a user-defined composite type. [#115063](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/115063)
- Fixed a bug that would cause a <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/sql-grammar#prepare_stmt" data-versioned="true">prepared statement</a> to fail if it references an enum as well as a table that has undergone a schema change. [#115174](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/115174)
- Fixed a bug that could cause finalization during a major-version upgrade to contend with descriptor lease renewals on a large cluster. Descriptor lease renewals now always have a lower priority than finalization. [#114672](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/114672)
- <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/backup" data-versioned="true">
    Backups
  </a>
  now evenly distribute their work across all replicas, including followers, regardless of leaseholder placement.
  [#115018](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/115018)
- Fixed a bug that could cause replica processing in store queues to get stuck if a the replica's ID has changed. [#115036](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/115036)
- Fixed an bug introduced in v22.2 that could lead to stuck queries or inaccurate results when using lookup <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/joins" data-versioned="true">joins</a> involving equality columns and multiple ranges. [#115581](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/115581)
- Fixed a bug in the declarative schema changer that could cause <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/create-index" data-versioned="true">`CREATE INDEX`</a> with expressions to fail on materialized <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/views" data-versioned="true">views</a>. [#115596](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/115596)
- Fixed a bug that could cause an inaccorate "too few columns" error for a query that used `ANY {array}` syntax with a subquery. [#115591](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/115591)
- Fixed a bug that could cause a "too few/many columns" errors for a query that used an `IN` or `NOT IN` clause with a non-trivial right operand, such as a subquery (rather than a constant tuple). [#115591](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/115591)
- Fixed a bug introduced in v22.2 that could cause errors or inaccurate results when performing a lookup or index <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/joins" data-versioned="true">join</a> on a table with three or more column families. [#115899](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/115899)
- Fixed a bug that could cause an internal error or a panic while attempting to forecast statistics on a numeric column. [#115899](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/115899)
- Fixed a bug when issuing a <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/begin-transaction" data-versioned="true">`BEGIN`</a> statement where incorrect `Age` field could be logged in the statement log. This bug could also cause statements to incorrectly appear in the slow query log. [#115257](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/115257)
- Fixed a bug in the SQL Statistics UI where the runtime was incorrectly calculated. This bug could cause recorded values to appear to exceed 100%. [#117497](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/117497)
- Fixed a bug that could cause a `CREATE CHANGEFEED WITH {key_column}` statement to retry forever. [#117555](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/117555)

### Performance improvements

- Reduced query planning time significantly for some queries that join multiple tables. [#114512](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/114512) [#116107](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/116107)

### Contributors

This release includes 128 merged PRs by 42 authors.

## v23.1.13

Release Date: December 11, 2023

### Downloads

<Note>
  Experimental downloads are not qualified for production use and not eligible for support or uptime SLA commitments,
  whether they are for testing releases or production releases.
</Note>

<table>
  <thead>
    <tr>
      <th>Operating System</th>
      <th>Architecture</th>
      <th>Full executable</th>
      <th>SQL-only executable</th>
    </tr>
  </thead>
  <tbody>
    <tr>
      <td rowspan="2">Linux</td>
      <td>Intel</td>
      <td>
        <a href="https://binaries.cockroachdb.com/cockroach-v23.1.13.linux-amd64.tgz">
          cockroach-v23.1.13.linux-amd64.tgz
        </a>
        <br />(<a href="https://binaries.cockroachdb.com/cockroach-v23.1.13.linux-amd64.tgz.sha256sum">SHA256</a>)
      </td>
      <td>
        <a href="https://binaries.cockroachdb.com/cockroach-sql-v23.1.13.linux-amd64.tgz">
          cockroach-sql-v23.1.13.linux-amd64.tgz
        </a>
        <br />(<a href="https://binaries.cockroachdb.com/cockroach-sql-v23.1.13.linux-amd64.tgz.sha256sum">SHA256</a>)
      </td>
    </tr>
    <tr>
      <td>ARM</td>

### Docker image

[Multi-platform images](https://docs.docker.com/build/building/multi-platform) include support for both Intel and ARM. Multi-platform images do not take up additional space on your Docker host.

Within the multi-platform image, both Intel and ARM images are **generally available** for production use.

To download the Docker image:

```shell
docker pull cockroachdb/cockroach:v23.1.13
```

### Source tag

To view or download the source code for CockroachDB v23.1.13 on Github, visit [v23.1.13 source tag](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/releases/tag/v23.1.13).

### Changelog

View a detailed changelog on GitHub: [v23.1.12...v23.1.13](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/compare/v23.1.12...v23.1.13)

### SQL language changes

- A new option for the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/restore" data-versioned="true">`RESTORE`</a> syntax, `strip_localities`, has been added. This can be used to strip the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/alter-table#set-locality" data-versioned="true">locality information</a> from a backup when there are mismatched <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/multiregion-overview#cluster-regions" data-versioned="true">cluster regions</a> between the backup's cluster and the target cluster. The following are behaviors that will most likely not be encountered with the specific use case that this patch provides, but are documented nonetheless:
  - Adding a <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/alter-database#set-primary-region" data-versioned="true">primary region</a> to a regionless restore (with or without <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/table-localities#regional-by-row-tables" data-versioned="true">regional by row table(s)</a> ) will not work out-of-the-box, but does produce an accurate message instructing a user to <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/drop-type" data-versioned="true">`DROP TYPE {database}.public.crdb_internal_region;`</a> (and for cluster restores, <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/alter-database#remove-a-replication-zone" data-versioned="true">`ALTER DATABASE {database} CONFIGURE ZONE DISCARD;`</a> ).
  - Restoring a cluster/database/table with a <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/table-localities#regional-by-row-tables" data-versioned="true">regional by row table</a> will not work out-of-the box. In particular, when performing writes, the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/alter-table#crdb_region" data-versioned="true">`crdb_region` column</a> needs to specify the region of the new row(s) being written to the table. The user will need to alter said column and set a default that makes sense, along with discarding the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/configure-replication-zones" data-versioned="true">zone configuration</a> (this latter is due to the fact that the zone config holds all outdated info related to the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/partitioning" data-versioned="true">partitions</a>, <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/constraints" data-versioned="true">constraints</a>, etc.). These are due to a conflict with the `crdb_region` column already being present in the regionless restore. This column specifies each row's home region and is a prefix to the table's primary key. Stripping localities does not touch this column as it would be an expensive operation that includes rewriting the entire table. [#111863](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/111863)
- The <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/restore" data-versioned="true">`RESTORE`</a> option `strip_localities` has been renamed to `remove_regions`. [#111863](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/111863)
- You can no longer perform a <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/restore" data-versioned="true">`RESTORE`</a> with the `remove_regions` option if the object being restored contains a <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/table-localities#regional-by-row-tables" data-versioned="true">regional by row table</a>. [#111863](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/111863)
- Added a <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/functions-and-operators" data-versioned="true">builtin function</a> `jsonb_array_to_string_array` that converts a <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/jsonb" data-versioned="true">JSONB</a> array to a string array. [#112864](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/112864)
- Updated the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/functions-and-operators" data-versioned="true">builtin function</a> `jsonb_array_to_string_array` to return <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/null-handling" data-versioned="true">_NULL_</a> objects. Previously, they were removed from the output. [#112864](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/112864)
- Fixed the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/monitoring-and-alerting#sql-activity-pages" data-versioned="true">**SQL Activity** page</a> update job to avoid conflicts on update, reduce the amount of data cached to just what the overview page requires, and fix the correctness of the top queries. [#112864](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/112864)

### Operational changes

- Added <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/metrics" data-versioned="true">metrics</a> for <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/architecture/replication-layer#raft" data-versioned="true">Raft</a> proposals and reproposals, specifically:
  - `raft.commands.proposed`: commands proposed to Raft by <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/architecture/overview#architecture-leaseholder" data-versioned="true">leaseholders</a>. (Note that this metric includes both of the reproposed metrics below.)
  - `raft.commands.reproposed.unchanged`: commands retried/reproposed to Raft because they take too long to apply (so they might be dropped).
  - `raft.commands.reproposed.new-lai`: commands retried/reproposed to Raft because they were committed to Raft out of order (failed the LAI (lease applied index) or <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/architecture/transaction-layer#closed-timestamps" data-versioned="true">closed timestamp</a> check). [#113153](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/113153)
- Added a new <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cluster-settings" data-versioned="true">cluster setting</a> `kv.gc.sticky_hint.enabled` that helps expedite <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/architecture/storage-layer#garbage-collection" data-versioned="true">garbage collection</a> after range deletions, such as when a SQL table or index is dropped. This setting is disabled by default. [#110643](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/110643)

### DB Console changes

- <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/ui-overview" data-versioned="true">
    DB Console
  </a>
  instances proxied at different subpaths that use
  <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cockroachcloud/configure-cloud-org-sso#oidc" data-versioned="true">
    OIDC
  </a>
  will now point to the correct relative path when attempting to use OIDC login.
  [#111290](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/111290)

### Bug fixes

- Fixed a bug where the `pg_attribute` could have sparsely populated `attnum` s since dropped columns were not included. Previously, the attribute number generated inside `pg_attribute` could be sparse because there would be gaps after columns were dropped. This could be problematic for ORMs since this would mean that attribute numbers could be sparse, and they may not be designed to handle such gaps. To address this, this patch adds dropped synthetic columns into the `pg_attribute` table, which allows these tools to work correctly. [#111119](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/111119)
- Fixed a bug that could prevent <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/restore" data-versioned="true">`RESTORE`</a> from working if it was performed during a <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/upgrade-cockroach-version" data-versioned="true">cluster upgrade</a>. [#112758](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/112758)
- Fixed a bug where queries with the `st_union` <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/functions-and-operators#aggregate-functions" data-versioned="true">aggregate function</a> could produce incorrect results in some cases due to the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cost-based-optimizer" data-versioned="true">query optimizer</a> performing invalid optimizations. This bug has been present since the `st_union` function was introduced in v20.2.0. [#112795](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/112795)
- A warning for [Technical Advisory 99561](/docs/advisories/a99561) could incorrectly surface when <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/drop-index" data-versioned="true">dropping secondary indexes</a> that store <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/primary-key" data-versioned="true">primary key</a> columns. This is now fixed. [#112906](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/112906)
- Fixed a bug where creating a <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/trigram-indexes" data-versioned="true">trigram index</a> and later displaying it via <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/show-create" data-versioned="true">`SHOW CREATE TABLE`</a>, would not show the opclass for this trigram index. [#113077](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/113077)
- Fixed a bug introduced in v22.2 where CockroachDB could incorrectly evaluate <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/joins" data-versioned="true">lookup and index joins</a> into tables with at least 3 <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/column-families" data-versioned="true">column families</a> in some cases (either a `non-nullable column with no value` internal error would occur, or the query would return incorrect results). [#113108](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/113108)
- Fixed a bug that could occasionally cause <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/online-schema-changes" data-versioned="true">schema change jobs</a> (e.g., table/index drops) to appear stuck in state "waiting for MVCC GC" for much longer than expected. This fix only applies to future schema changes. Existing stuck jobs can be processed by manually force-enqueueing the relevant <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/architecture/overview#architecture-range" data-versioned="true">ranges</a> in the MVCC GC queue under the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/ui-debug-pages" data-versioned="true">DB Console's **Advanced Debug** page</a>. [#110643](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/110643)
- Fixed a bug that could cause internal errors or panics while attempting to forecast <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cost-based-optimizer#table-statistics" data-versioned="true">statistics</a> on a numeric column. [#113798](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/113798)
- Fixed a bug where <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/alter-table#alter-primary-key" data-versioned="true">`ALTER PRIMARY KEY`</a> would incorrectly disable <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/indexes" data-versioned="true">secondary indexes</a> while new secondary indexes were being backfilled when using the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/online-schema-changes" data-versioned="true">declarative schema changer</a>. [#113183](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/113183)
- Previously, when executing queries with <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/joins" data-versioned="true">index / lookup joins</a> when the ordering needs to be maintained, CockroachDB could in some cases inadvertently increase query latency, possibly by 1 or 2 orders of magnitude. This bug was introduced in v22.2 and is now fixed. [#114143](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/114143)
- Fixed a bug where the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/show-statistics" data-versioned="true">`SHOW STATISTICS`</a> command would incorrectly require the user to have the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/security-reference/authorization#admin-role" data-versioned="true">admin role</a>. It was intended to only require the user to have any privilege on the table being inspected. [#114479](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/114479)
- Fixed a bug that could cause a query plan to skip scanning rows from the local region when performing a <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/joins" data-versioned="true">lookup join</a> with a <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/table-localities#regional-by-row-tables" data-versioned="true">`REGIONAL BY ROW`</a> table as the input. [#114456](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/114456)
- Fixed a bug that could cause <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/alter-database#add-region" data-versioned="true">`ALTER DATABASE... ADD/DROP REGION`</a> to hang if node localities were changed after regions were added. [#114197](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/114197)

### Performance improvements

- Addressed a performance regression that could happen when the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/online-schema-changes" data-versioned="true">declarative schema changer</a> is being used to <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/create-index" data-versioned="true">create an index</a> with a concurrent workload. [#113724](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/113724)
- Added an off-by-default <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cluster-settings" data-versioned="true">cluster setting</a>, `kv.dist_sender.follower_reads_unhealthy.enabled`, which when enabled will prevent failed requests from being issued on followers that are <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/node-shutdown#draining" data-versioned="true">draining</a>, <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/node-shutdown?filters=decommission" data-versioned="true">decommissioning</a>, or otherwise unhealthy. This will prevent <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/follower-reads" data-versioned="true">follower reads</a> against nodes in such states. This prevents latency spikes if those nodes later go offline. [#114367](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/114367)
- <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cost-based-optimizer" data-versioned="true">
    Query planning
  </a>
  time has been reduced significantly for some queries in which many tables are
  <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/joins" data-versioned="true">
    joined
  </a>
  . [#114835](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/114835)

### Contributors

This release includes 118 merged PRs by 42 authors.

### Docker image

[Multi-platform images](https://docs.docker.com/build/building/multi-platform) include support for both Intel and ARM. Multi-platform images do not take up additional space on your Docker host.

Within the multi-platform image:

- The ARM image is **Experimental** and not yet qualified for production use and not eligible for support or uptime SLA commitments.
- The Intel image is **Generally Available** for production use.

To download the Docker image:

```shell
docker pull cockroachdb/cockroach:v23.1.12
```

### Source tag

To view or download the source code for CockroachDB v23.1.12 on Github, visit [v23.1.12 source tag](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/releases/tag/v23.1.12).

### Changelog

View a detailed changelog on GitHub: [v23.1.11...v23.1.12](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/compare/v23.1.11...v23.1.12)

### Security updates

- The `SIGHUP` signal now clears the cached expiration times for <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cockroach-cert#how-security-certificates-work" data-versioned="true">client certificates</a> that are reported by the `security.certificate.expiration.client` metric. [#111006](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/111006)
- SQL commands that were previously limited to the `admin` <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/security-reference/authorization#supported-privileges" data-versioned="true">system privilege</a> can now be used by users with the `VIEWCLUSTERMETADATA` or `REPAIRCLUSTERMETADATA` system privilege, depending on whether the operation is read-only or modifies state. [#111131](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/111131)

### General changes

- The maximum permitted value of the `COCKROACH_RPC_INITIAL_WINDOW_SIZE` environment variable has been increased to `64MB`. By increasing this environment variable, in conjunction with tuning OS-level maximum TCP window size, you can increase the throughput that <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/architecture/replication-layer#raft" data-versioned="true">Raft replication</a> can sustain over high latency network links. [#111287](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/111287)
- Updated Go version to 1.19.13. [#112204](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/112204)

### SQL language changes

- New datetime built-ins ( `make_date`, `make_timestamp`, and `make_timestamptz` ) have been added, allowing for the creation of timestamps, timestamps with time zones, and dates. In addition, `date_trunc` now allows for a timestamp to be truncated in a specified timezone (to a specified precision). [#110338](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/110338)
- New system privileges `CREATEROLE`, `CREATELOGIN`, `CREATEDB`, and `CONTROLJOB` have been introduced. Each is analogous to its existing <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/create-user#role-options" data-versioned="true">role option</a> counterpart but can additionally be inherited through role membership. [#110359](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/110359), [#110359](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/110359), [#110359](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/110359), [#110359](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/110359)
- <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/restore" data-versioned="true">
    `RESTORE`
  </a>
  can now be passed a `WITH EXECUTION LOCALITY` option similar to `BACKUP` to restrict execution of the job to nodes
  with matching localities. [#110611](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/110611)
- The `statement_activity` and `transaction_activity` table column `execution_total_cluster_seconds` is now accurate. The `combinedstmts` endpoint returns the correct value for the `StmtsTotalRuntimeSecs` and `TxnsTotalRuntimeSecs` properties. [#109639](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/109639)
- The `discard` <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/logging-overview" data-versioned="true">log message</a> is now limited to once per minute by default. The message now includes both the number of transactions and the number of statements that were discarded. [#110983](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/110983)

### Operational changes

- The <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cockroach-debug-zip" data-versioned="true">`cockroach debug zip`</a> command now has an option to omit goroutine stack dumps. This impacts the creation of `nodes/*/stacks.txt` and `nodes/*/stacks_with_labels.txt` within debug ZIP bundles. Users can opt to exclude these goroutine stacks by using the `--include-goroutine-stacks=false` flag. Fetching stack traces for all goroutines is a "stop-the-world" operation, which can momentarily but significantly increase SQL service latency. Any periodic goroutine dumps previously taken on the node will still be included in `nodes/*/goroutines/*.txt.gz`, since they have already been generated and don't require any stop-the-world operations. [#110266](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/110266)
- Requests for database details or table details from the UI, or usages of `SHOW RANGES WITH DETAILS` are no longer subject to errors if the number of requested spans is too large. [#109902](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/109902)
- Added a new <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/metrics" data-versioned="true">metric</a> `changefeed.lagging_ranges` that shows the number of <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/architecture/overview#architecture-range" data-versioned="true">ranges</a> which are behind in changefeeds. This metric can be used with the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/create-changefeed#options" data-versioned="true">`metrics_label` changefeed option</a>. The calculation of this metric is controlled by two new <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cluster-settings" data-versioned="true">cluster settings</a>: (1) `lagging_ranges_threshold`, with a default of 3 minutes, is the amount of time a range needs to be behind to be considered lagging, and (2) `lagging_ranges_polling_interval`, with a default of 1 minute, controls how often the lagging ranges calculation is done. Note that polling adds latency to the metric being updated. For example, if a range falls behind by 3 minutes, the metric may not update until an additional minute afterwards. Also note that ranges undergoing an initial scan for longer than the threshold are considered to be lagging. Starting a changefeed with an initial scan on a large table will likely increment the metric for each range in the table. However, as ranges complete the initial scan, the number of lagging ranges will decrease. [#110963](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/110963)
- The <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/ui-overview" data-versioned="true">DB Console</a> now constructs client-side requests using relative URLs instead of absolute ones. This enables proxying of the DB Console at arbitrary subpaths. [#111652](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/111652)
- Added a new <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cluster-settings" data-versioned="true">cluster setting</a> `server.http.base_path` that controls the redirection of the browser after successful login with <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/sso-db-console" data-versioned="true">OIDC SSO</a>. Most users do not need to modify this setting. However, it is helpful in cases where CockroachDB is running behind a load balancer or proxy that serves CockroachDB under a subpath, such as `https:// <hostname>/crdb/`. In those cases, it is necessary for the browser to redirect to `/ crdb` after login instead of `/`, which has always been the hard-coded default. [#112038](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/112038)

### DB Console changes

- Non-admin users can now view the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/ui-databases-page" data-versioned="true">**Database**, **Database Details**, and **Database table** pages</a>. [#110342](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/110342)
- The <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/ui-sql-dashboard#sql-connection-rate" data-versioned="true">SQL Connection Rate metric</a> on the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/ui-sql-dashboard" data-versioned="true">SQL Dashboard</a> is downsampled using the MAX function instead of SUM. This improves situations where zooming out would cause the connection rate to increase for downsampled data. [#110497](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/110497)
- Fixed a bug in DB Console's <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cockroachcloud/statements-page#diagnostics" data-versioned="true">Statement Diagnostic page</a> that could cause the page to crash if the response was larger than 50 KB. The page now keeps pulling results until no maximum size errors are encountered. [#111278](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/111278)
- Fixed an error on the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/ui-overview#sql-activity" data-versioned="true">SQL Activity page</a> when there was a workload, and then the workload stopped so that no queries ran against the database in the last hour. [#111496](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/111496)
- The <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/ui-jobs-page" data-versioned="true">**Jobs** table</a> will now correctly display timestamps for creation, last modified, and the completed time fields. [#111901](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/111901)
- The `Reset Sql Stats` button is now visible to users with the admin role on the DB Console. [#110256](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/110256)
- Reduced memory usage in <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cockroachcloud/statements-page" data-versioned="true">SQL activity</a> jobs. [#112323](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/112323)

### Bug fixes

- The new backup option `updates_cluster_monitoring_metrics` tracks the timestamp of the last backup failure due to a KMS error. This option is disabled by default. [#111310](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/111310)
- Fixed a bug where vectorized `COPY FROM` could produce a plan with more than one RenderNodes, when only zero or one should be allowed. This could result in multiple render nodes in a table with a hash sharded primary key. [#111412](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/111412)
- Fixed a bug that caused CockroachDB to stop collecting new statistics about <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/ui-statements-page#statement-fingerprint-page" data-versioned="true">Statement fingerprints</a> and <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/ui-transactions-page" data-versioned="true">Transaction fingerprints</a>. [#111641](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/111641)
- Fixed a bug where, internally, printing a 0 decimal with a very low exponent uses excessive memory. The <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/decimal" data-versioned="true">DECIMAL</a> type type is not impacted, but `crdb_internal` functions may be. [#110564](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/110564)
- Fixed a bug where executing the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/export#export-a-table-into-parquet" data-versioned="true">`EXPORT INTO PARQUET`</a> statement could cause an <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cluster-setup-troubleshooting#out-of-memory-oom-crash" data-versioned="true">out-of-memory crash (OOM)</a>. Now, if memory is exceeded, the `EXPORT INTO PARQUET` statement returns an error. If you see an error related to memory, retry the `EXPORT INTO PARQUET` statement using a smaller value for the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/export#export-options" data-versioned="true">`chunk_rows` option</a>. Cockroach Labs <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/export-data-with-changefeeds" data-versioned="true">recommends using changefeeds to export data</a> because they provide better performance for growing workloads. Additionally, changefeeds <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/show-jobs" data-versioned="true">operate as jobs</a>, which offer <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/monitor-and-debug-changefeeds" data-versioned="true">observability</a> and <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/create-and-configure-changefeeds" data-versioned="true">job management</a>. [#110717](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/110717) [#110717](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/110717)
- Added limited `statement_statistics` to the `debug.zip` output. [#110662](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/110662)
- Fixed a nil dereference panic during node startup that could be caused by an incorrect initialization order. [#109684](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/109684)
- Fixed a bug where the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/begin-transaction" data-versioned="true">`BEGIN` statement</a> incorrectly displayed a transaction ID in telemetry logs. It now correctly shows no transaction ID, since there is no open transaction when `BEGIN` is executed. [#109840](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/109840)
- Fixed a bug that could cause a transaction performing multiple parallel foreign key checks to return a `concurrent txn use detected` error. [#109849](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/109849)
- Fixed a bug where dependencies on sequences from tables would be reported with the wrong value for the `classid` column in the `pg_catalog.pg_depend` table. [#110207](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/110207)
- Fixed edge cases in decimal and float evaluation for division operators. `'NaN'::DECIMAL / 0` will now return `NaN` instead of a division-by-zero error, and `0 / 'inf'::DECIMAL` will return `0` instead of `0E-2019`. [#110296](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/110296)
- Fixed a DB Console issue where the `DROP_UNUSED` index recommendations produced by the table details page produced an invalid `DROP INDEX` statement. [#110453](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/110453)
- Executing two <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/alter-range#configure-zone" data-versioned="true">`ALTER RANGE default CONFIGURE ZONE`</a> statements on the same line no longer triggers an error. [#110337](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/110337)
- Removed a buggy TTL descriptor repair. Previously, upgrading from v22.2.x to 23.1.9 incorrectly removed <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/row-level-ttl#ttl-storage-parameters" data-versioned="true">TTL storage parameters</a> from tables (visible via <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/show-create" data-versioned="true">`SHOW CREATE TABLE <ttl-table>`</a> ) while attempting to repair table descriptors. A node that attempts to run the TTL <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/show-jobs" data-versioned="true">job</a> could crash due to a panic caused by the missing TTL storage parameters. Clusters currently on v22.2.x should **not** be upgraded to v23.1.9, but should move directly to v23.1.10 or later. For more information, refer to [Technical Advisory 110363](/docs/advisories/a110363). [#110500](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/110500)
- Fixed a performance regression when disabling `sql.metrics.statement_details.enabled`, which caused execution stats to be collected for all queries instead of the default 1% of queries. [#109881](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/109881)
- `cockroach debug pebble` commands now work correctly with encrypted stores which don't use the default `cockroach-data` path, and you no longer need to pass the `--store` option. [#110507](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/110507)
- The <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cockroachcloud/databases-page" data-versioned="true">**Database** pages</a> no longer displays `undefined` regions or outdated node information. [#110741](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/110741)
- Fixed a bug where `RESET (ttl_expire_after)` could incorrectly remove `ttl_expiration_expression`. [#110746](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/110746)
- Fixed a bug where an <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/alter-table#add-constraint" data-versioned="true">`ALTER TABLE... ADD CONSTRAINT CHECK...`</a> statement with a user-defined function (UDF) in the `CHECK` could cause a validation error. [#110720](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/110720)
- Fixed a bug where `CREATE INDEX` for <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/partial-indexes" data-versioned="true">partial indexes</a> could fail with `ERROR: duplicate key value violates unique constraint` if concurrent inserts happened simultaneously. [#110584](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/110584)
- Fixed a bug where a <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/create-table" data-versioned="true">`CREATE TABLE`</a> command with an `IDENTITY` column did not properly propagate the type of the column into the sequence. [#111014](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/111014)
- Fixed a bug where the `format_type` built-in did not honor `typemod` information for array types, leading to incorrect output. [#110940](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/110940)
- Fixed compaction behavior to prevent rapid sublevel growth when removing replicas from a store, such as during decommissioning. [#111141](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/111141)
- Fixed a bug that could occur when the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/postgresql-compatibility#multiple-active-portals" data-versioned="true">multiple active portals</a> execution mode (Preview) was enabled to evaluate queries such as lookup joins. The bug could result in an internal error like `unexpected 40960 leftover bytes` if the portal was not fully consumed. [#110666](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/110666)
- External connection URLs now accept the scheme `azure-blob` for connections to Azure Blob Storage and the scheme `azure-kms` for connections to Azure KMS. For backward compatibility, schemes `azure` and `azure-storage` schemes continue to work for connections to Azure Blob Storage. [#111246](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/111246)
- Fixed a bug where changing the setting `server.telemetry.hot_ranges_stats.interval` had no effect. [#111373](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/111373)
- Added a check for values before using `mean` on the DB Console <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/ui-statements-page" data-versioned="true">Plan Details page</a>, fixing a crash. [#111505](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/111505)
- Fixed a bug where dependencies on sequences from tables would be reported with the wrong value for the `classid` column in the `pg_catalog.pg_depend` table. [#111600](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/111600)
- Fixed a bug where `atttypmod` in `pg_attribute` was not populated for <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/timestamp" data-versioned="true">`TIMESTAMP`</a> / <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/interval" data-versioned="true">`INTERVAL`</a> types, which meant that ORMs could not know the precision of these types properly. [#111727](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/111727)
- Fixed a bug in the DB Console <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/ui-insights-page" data-versioned="true">Transaction Insight Details</a> page, which showed contention details of other transactions. Now, CockroachDB will only surface contention details for the current transaction. [#111880](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/111880)
- Fixed a bug where `indoption` inside `pg_index` was not properly encoded. Clients were unable to decode it as `int2vector`. [#111957](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/111957)
- RPC failures on writes now use the parallel commit protocol and execute in parallel to the commit operation. This change prevents incorrect retryable failures and `transaction unexpectedly committed` assertions by detecting when writes cannot be retried idempotently, instead returning an `AmbiguousResultError`. [#111876](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/111876)
- Fixed a bug that prevented the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cost-based-optimizer" data-versioned="true">optimizer</a> from honoring the `statement_timeout` session setting when generating constrained index scans for queries with large `IN` lists or `= ANY` predicates on multiple index key columns. This bug could cause an Out-of-Memory (OOM) condition on the node. [#112076](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/112076)
- Fixed a bug that caused internal errors during query optimization in rare cases. The bug has been present since version v2.1.11, but it is more likely to occur in version v21.2.0 and later, though it is still rare. The bug only presents when a query contains `min` and `max` <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/functions-and-operators#aggregate-functions" data-versioned="true">aggregate functions</a> [#112254](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/112254)
- Fixed a bug where a lookup or index join on a table with at least three column families could be evaluated incorrectly, leading to a "non-nullable column with no value" error or incorrect query results. The bug was introduced in v22.2. [#113107](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/113107)
- Fixed a bug that could cause internal errors or panics while attempting to forecast statistics on a numeric column. [#113881](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/113881)

### Performance improvements

- Queries that compare collated strings now use less memory and may execute faster. [#110147](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/110147)
- Reduced the impact of high-concurrency blind writes to the same key on goroutine scheduling latency. [#109370](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/109370)

### Contributors

This release includes 207 merged PRs by 64 authors.

Release Date: October 2, 2023
