### Docker image

[Multi-platform images](https://docs.docker.com/build/building/multi-platform) include support for both Intel and ARM. Multi-platform images do not take up additional space on your Docker host.

Within the multi-platform image:

- The ARM image is **Experimental** and not yet qualified for production use and not eligible for support or uptime SLA commitments.
- The Intel image is **Generally Available** for production use.

To download the Docker image:

```shell
docker pull cockroachdb/cockroach:v23.1.11
```

### Source tag

To view or download the source code for CockroachDB v23.1.11 on Github, visit [v23.1.11 source tag](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/releases/tag/v23.1.11).

### Changelog

View a detailed changelog on GitHub: [v23.1.10...v23.1.11](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/compare/v23.1.10...v23.1.11)

### SQL language changes

- Added a new syntax to <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/show-default-privileges" data-versioned="true">`SHOW DEFAULT PRIVILEGES`</a>, `SHOW DEFAULT PRIVILEGES FOR GRANTEE <grantee>` that shows the default privileges that a grantee received. [#108285](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/108285)
- The admin API <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cluster-api" data-versioned="true">database details</a> endpoint now returns authoritative range statistics. [#108727](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/108727)
- Added the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cluster-settings" data-versioned="true">cluster setting</a> `sql.stats.limit_table_size.enabled`, which controls whether or not CockroachDB enforces the row limit set by `sql.stats.persisted_rows.max` in the `system.statement_statistics` and `system.transaction_statistics` tables. [#108912](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/108912)
- Optimized the `sql-stats-compaction` <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/show-jobs" data-versioned="true">job</a> 's <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/delete" data-versioned="true">delete query</a> to avoid a <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/sql-tuning-with-explain#issue-full-table-scans" data-versioned="true">full scan</a>. This helps avoid a <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/common-errors#restart-transaction" data-versioned="true">transaction retry error</a>, which can cause the job to fail. [#108987](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/108987)
- Fixed an issue where the UI was missing query text and details when looking at the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/ui-sql-dashboard#transactions" data-versioned="true">SQL activity transactions page</a> if there were more than 500 transactions or statements. The `crdb_internal.statement_activity` table now includes all statements for a transaction that are in the `crdb_internal.transaction_activity` table. [#109479](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/109479)
- Added the `VIEWSYSTEMTABLE` <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/security-reference/authorization#supported-privileges" data-versioned="true">system privilege</a>. Users with this privilege have <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/selection-queries" data-versioned="true">`SELECT`</a> privileges for all tables in the `system` database. [#109525](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/109525)
- The `oidvectortypes` <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/functions-and-operators" data-versioned="true">built-in function</a> has been implemented, which can format an `oidvector`. [#109711](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/109711)
- The internal persisted <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cost-based-optimizer#table-statistics" data-versioned="true">statistics</a> table max size check is now done once an hour instead of every 10 minutes. This reduces the risk of serialization errors on the statistics tables. [#109707](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/109707)
- Introspection queries will now show the internal `node` user as the owner of tables in <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/pg-catalog" data-versioned="true">`pg_catalog`</a> and <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/information-schema" data-versioned="true">`information_schema`</a>. Previously, the owner was shown as `admin`, but that was inaccurate since users with the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/security-reference/authorization#admin-role" data-versioned="true">`admin` role</a> could not modify these tables in any way. [#109735](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/109735)

### Operational changes

- Added the `kv.enqueue_in_replicate_queue_on_span_config_update.enabled` <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cluster-settings" data-versioned="true">cluster setting</a>. When set to `true`, <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cockroach-start#store" data-versioned="true">stores</a> in the cluster will enqueue <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/architecture/overview#architecture-replica" data-versioned="true">replicas</a> for <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/architecture/replication-layer" data-versioned="true">replication changes</a> upon receiving config updates that could affect the replica. This setting is off by default. Enabling this setting speeds up how quickly config-triggered replication changes begin, but adds additional CPU overhead. The overhead scales with the number of leaseholders. [#108812](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/108812)
- Added a new <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cluster-settings" data-versioned="true">cluster setting</a> named `server.hot_ranges_request.node.timeout`, with a default value of 5 minutes. The setting controls the maximum amount of time that a <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/ui-hot-ranges-page" data-versioned="true">hot ranges request</a> will spend waiting for a node to provide a response. Set it to `0` to disable timeouts. [#109015](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/109015)
- Span stats requests will return a partial result if the request encounters any errors. Errors that would have previously terminated the request are now included in the response. [#109008](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/109008)
- <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/backup" data-versioned="true">
    `BACKUP`
  </a>
  now skips contacting the ranges for tables on which
  <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/alter-table#exclude-a-tables-data-from-backups" data-versioned="true">
    `exclude_data_from_backup`
  </a>
  is set, and can thus succeed even if an excluded table is unavailable.
  [#109123](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/109123)
- The <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/architecture/distribution-layer#grpc" data-versioned="true">RPC</a> dial and heartbeat timeouts can now be configured via the environment variables `COCKROACH_RPC_DIAL_TIMEOUT` (default 2x `COCKROACH_NETWORK_TIMEOUT` or 2x2=4 seconds) and `COCKROACH_RPC_HEARTBEAT_TIMEOUT` (default 3x `COCKROACH_NETWORK_TIMEOUT` or 3x2=6 seconds). This allows configuring these values independently of `COCKROACH_NETWORK_TIMEOUT`. [#109358](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/109358)
- The default <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/architecture/distribution-layer#grpc" data-versioned="true">gRPC</a> server-side send timeout has been increased from 2 seconds to 4 seconds (1x to 2x of `COCKROACH_NETWORK_TIMEOUT` ), to avoid spurious connection failures in certain scenarios. This can be controlled via the new environment variable `COCKROACH_RPC_SERVER_TIMEOUT`. [#109620](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/109620)
- Added a new gauge <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/metrics" data-versioned="true">metric</a> `sql.schema.invalid_objects`. This gauge is periodically updated based on the schedule set by the `sql.schema.telemetry.recurrence` <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cluster-settings" data-versioned="true">cluster setting</a>. When the metric is updated, it counts the number of schema objects ( <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/create-table" data-versioned="true">tables</a>, <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/create-type" data-versioned="true">types</a>, <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/create-schema" data-versioned="true">schemas</a>, <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/create-database" data-versioned="true">databases</a>, and <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/user-defined-functions" data-versioned="true">functions</a> ) that are in an invalid state according to CockroachDB's internal validation checks. This metric is expected to be zero ( `0` ) in a healthy cluster. If it is not zero, it indicates that there is a problem that must be repaired. [#109733](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/109733)
- Added two new <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/monitor-and-debug-changefeeds#recommended-changefeed-metrics-to-track" data-versioned="true">changefeed metrics</a>: `changefeed.checkpoint_progress` is similar to `changefeed.max_behind_nanos`, but it also supports <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/monitor-and-debug-changefeeds#using-changefeed-metrics-labels" data-versioned="true">metrics labels</a>. `changefeed.aggregator_progress` tracks the progress of individual aggregators (the lowest timestamp for which all aggregators with the label have emitted all values they're responsible for). [#109744](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/109744)

### Command-line changes

- Removed the command `\demo recommission` from <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cockroach-demo" data-versioned="true">`cockroach demo`</a>. It had been obsolete and non-functional since v20.2. [#108631](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/108631)

### DB Console changes

- Users without the `VIEWCLUSTERSETTINGS` <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/security-reference/authorization#supported-privileges" data-versioned="true">permission</a>, but with the `VIEWACTIVITY` or `VIEWACTIVITYREDACTED` permissions, can now see <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/ui-databases-page#index-recommendations" data-versioned="true">index recommendations</a>. [#109466](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/109466)
- CockroachDB will now show a warning when the time period selected on the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/ui-overview#sql-activity" data-versioned="true">SQL Activity page</a> is older than the oldest data available. [#109468](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/109468)

### Bug fixes

- Fixed a buggy TTL descriptor repair by removing it. Previously, upgrading from v22.2.x to 23.1.9 incorrectly removed <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/row-level-ttl#ttl-storage-parameters" data-versioned="true">TTL storage params</a> from tables (visible via <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/show-create" data-versioned="true">`SHOW CREATE TABLE <ttl-table>`</a> ) while attempting to repair table descriptors. This resulted in the node that attempts to run the TTL <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/show-jobs" data-versioned="true">job</a> crashing due to a panic caused by the missing TTL storage parameters. Clusters currently on v22.2.x should **not** be upgraded to v23.1.9 and should be upgraded directly to v23.1.10 or later. For more information, see [Technical Advisory 110363](/docs/advisories/a110363). [#110562](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/110562)
- Users with the `VIEWACTIVITY` <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/security-reference/authorization#supported-privileges" data-versioned="true">privilege</a> should be able to see other users' sessions from both the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cockroach-sql" data-versioned="true">CLI</a> and the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/ui-overview" data-versioned="true">DB Console</a>. [#108571](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/108571)
- Fixed errors on the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/ui-sessions-page" data-versioned="true">**Sessions** page</a> in the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/ui-overview" data-versioned="true">DB Console</a> when a session's memory usage is zero bytes. [#108619](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/108619)
- Fixed a bug in <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cockroach-demo" data-versioned="true">`cockroach demo`</a> whereby `\demo add` could sometimes crash with an error " `index out of range [...] with length...` ". This bug was introduced in v19.x. [#108631](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/108631)
- Fixed a bug whereby the command `\demo decommission` in <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cockroach-demo" data-versioned="true">`cockroach demo`</a> could sometime leave the demo cluster in a broken state. This bug was introduced in v20.2. [#108631](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/108631)
- Fixed a bug in the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/indexes" data-versioned="true">index</a> recommendations provided in the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/explain" data-versioned="true">`EXPLAIN`</a> output where <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/alter-index" data-versioned="true">`ALTER INDEX... VISIBLE`</a> index recommendations may suggest making the wrong index visible when there are multiple invisible indexes in a table. [#108646](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/108646)
- Fixed a bug that could cause a query with <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/limit-offset" data-versioned="true">`LIMIT`</a> and <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/order-by" data-versioned="true">`ORDER BY`</a> to return results in the wrong order. This bug could cause incorrect results as well if the `LIMIT` was nested within an outer query, e.g. under another `LIMIT`. This bug had existed since before v22.2. [#106798](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/106798)
- Fixed a bug with <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/collate" data-versioned="true">collated string</a> type checking with nested <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/scalar-expressions#simple-case-expressions" data-versioned="true">case expressions</a> where an inner case had no explicit collated type. [#108345](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/108345)
- Fixed a bug where <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/release-savepoint" data-versioned="true">`RELEASE SAVEPOINT`</a> could incorrectly emit the message `"cannot publish new versions for descriptors"` instead of a <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/common-errors#restart-transaction" data-versioned="true">retryable error</a> to applications. [#108478](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/108478)
- Fixed a bug that could cause CPU usage to increase over time. [#108801](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/108801)
- Fixed a bug introduced in v22.1 that could cause a <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/joins" data-versioned="true">join</a> to infinite-loop in rare cases when (1) the join filter is not an equality and (2) no columns from the left input are returned. [#106875](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/106875)
- Users with the `VIEWACTIVITY` <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/security-reference/authorization#supported-privileges" data-versioned="true">permission</a> can now view correct values for the current timezone in the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/ui-overview" data-versioned="true">DB Console</a>. [#108780](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/108780)
- Fixed a bug present since v23.1.0 that would cause queries on the `pg_catalog.pg_statistic_ext` table to fail if a table was dropped recently. This bug also caused the `\d` <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cockroach-sql" data-versioned="true">CLI</a> shortcut to encounter errors. [#108909](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/108909)
- Fixed a bug where `pg_attribute` and `pg_attrdef` did not properly return results for generated columns. [#109035](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/109035)
- The <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/ui-insights-page#schema-insights-tab" data-versioned="true">Schema Insights</a> view should hit request timeouts less frequently, if at all. [#109014](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/109014)
- Fixed a bug that caused nodes to crash when attempting to `EXECUTE` a prepared statement with an argument that referenced a <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/user-defined-functions" data-versioned="true">user-defined function</a>. This bug was present since user-defined functions were introduced in v22.2. [#108469](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/108469)
- Fixed a bug so the filter on the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/ui-statements-page" data-versioned="true">Statements Page</a> works when the app name is an empty string (represented as 'unset'). [#108985](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/108985)
- Fixed a bug where a `SpanStatsRequest` would return post-replicated MVCC stats, which was causing incorrect output in <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/show-ranges" data-versioned="true">`SHOW RANGES... WITH DETAILS`</a>. Now, a `SpanStatsRequest` returns the logical MVCC stats for the requested span. [#109234](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/109234)
- Fixed an issue with <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/ui-sql-dashboard#full-table-index-scans" data-versioned="true">the "full scan" filter in the UI</a>, where the filter was not returning any results. [#109274](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/109274)
- Going to the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/ui-transactions-page#transaction-details-page" data-versioned="true">Transaction Details Page</a> from <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/ui-insights-page#high-contention" data-versioned="true">Workload Insights &gt; High Contention</a> is fixed. Previously, the link would not show any results. [#109253](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/109253)
- Fixed the column names on the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/selection-queries" data-versioned="true">`SELECT` queries</a> against the tables `crdb_internal.node_txn_execution_insights` and `crdb_internal.cluster_txn_execution_insights` during the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cockroach-debug-zip" data-versioned="true">creation of debug.zip files</a>. [#109515](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/109515)
- Fixed a bug that could cause some rows to be silently skipped during <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/import" data-versioned="true">`IMPORT`</a> when a node failed. [#109663](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/109663)
- Fixed a bug in <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/spatial-data-overview" data-versioned="true">geospatial queries</a> where more rows could be returned by the query than expected. This could happen when a query filter of the form `ST_Distance(geog1, geog2) > constant` or `ST_MaxDistance(geom1, geom2) > constant`, where the operator was one of `>`, `<`, `>=`, `<=`, or a filter of the form `ST_Distance(geog1, geog2, false) = 0` would sometimes mistakenly evaluate to `true` when one or both of the inputs was `NULL` or an empty <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/architecture/glossary#geography" data-versioned="true">geography</a> or <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/architecture/glossary#geometry" data-versioned="true">geometry</a>. [#109393](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/109393)
- Fixed an issue where a <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/architecture/distribution-layer#range-splits" data-versioned="true">split</a> can be called on an invalid key that's in the form of `someValidKey.Next()` during <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/restore" data-versioned="true">restore</a>. This split key can land in the middle of a row with <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/column-families" data-versioned="true">column families</a>, and thus result in failing SQL queries when querying the restored table. [#109777](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/109777)
- Fixed an issue where a <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/architecture/distribution-layer#range-splits" data-versioned="true">split</a> can be called on an invalid key that's in the form of `someValidKey.Next()` during <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/restore" data-versioned="true">restore</a> with the `bulkio.restore.use_simple_import_spans` <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cluster-settings" data-versioned="true">cluster setting</a> set to `true`. This split key can land in the middle of a row with <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/column-families" data-versioned="true">column families</a>, and thus result in failing SQL queries when querying the restored table. [#109940](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/109940)
- The `difference` <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/functions-and-operators" data-versioned="true">built-in function</a> had its return type incorrectly set to <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/string" data-versioned="true">`string`</a> instead of <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/int" data-versioned="true">`integer`</a>. [#109752](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/109752)
- Fixed a bug where dependencies on <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/show-sequences" data-versioned="true">sequences</a> from <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/show-tables" data-versioned="true">tables</a> would be reported with the wrong value for the `classid` column in the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/pg-catalog" data-versioned="true">`pg_catalog.pg_depend` table</a>. [#110206](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/110206)
- Fixed a bug that could cause a <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/transactions" data-versioned="true">transaction</a> performing multiple parallel <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/foreign-key" data-versioned="true">foreign key</a> checks to return a `concurrent txn use detected` error. [#110273](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/110273)
- Various observability pages in the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/ui-overview" data-versioned="true">DB Console</a> no longer crash when they encounter zeros (e.g., a session with no memory allocated). [#108785](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/108785)

### Performance improvements

- Improved the cost of resolving a user-defined <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/enum" data-versioned="true">enum</a> type that has many values. [#109470](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/109470)
- Queries that access the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/pg-catalog" data-versioned="true">`pg_catalog`</a> and <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/information-schema" data-versioned="true">`information_schema`</a> that perform introspection on other tables in those schemas are now significantly faster. [#109735](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/109735)

### Contributors

This release includes 204 merged PRs by 63 authors.

Release Date: September 18, 2023

        <a href="https://binaries.cockroachdb.com/cockroach-v23.1.10.windows-6.2-amd64.zip">
          cockroach-v23.1.10.windows-6.2-amd64.zip
        </a>
        <br />(<a href="https://binaries.cockroachdb.com/cockroach-v23.1.10.windows-6.2-amd64.zip.sha256sum">SHA256</a>)
      </td>
      <td>
        <a href="https://binaries.cockroachdb.com/cockroach-sql-v23.1.10.windows-6.2-amd64.zip">
          cockroach-sql-v23.1.10.windows-6.2-amd64.zip
        </a>
        <br />(
        <a href="https://binaries.cockroachdb.com/cockroach-sql-v23.1.10.windows-6.2-amd64.zip.sha256sum">SHA256</a>)
      </td>
    </tr>
  </tbody>
</table>

### Docker image

[Multi-platform images](https://docs.docker.com/build/building/multi-platform) include support for both Intel and ARM. Multi-platform images do not take up additional space on your Docker host.

Within the multi-platform image:

- The ARM image is **Experimental** and not yet qualified for production use and not eligible for support or uptime SLA commitments.
- The Intel image is **Generally Available** for production use.

To download the Docker image:

```shell
docker pull cockroachdb/cockroach:v23.1.10
```

### Source tag

To view or download the source code for CockroachDB v23.1.10 on Github, visit [v23.1.10 source tag](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/releases/tag/v23.1.10).

### Changelog

View a detailed changelog on GitHub: [v23.1.9...v23.1.10](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/compare/v23.1.9...v23.1.10)

### Bug fixes

- Removed buggy <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/row-level-ttl" data-versioned="true">TTL</a> descriptor repair. In v23.1.9, upgrading from v22.2 to v23.1.9 incorrectly removed TTL storage parameters from tables (visible by running `SHOW CREATE TABLE <ttl-table>;` ) while attempting to repair the table descriptors. This resulted in the node that attempted to run the TTL job crashing due to a panic caused by the missing TTL storage parameters. Clusters currently on v22.2 should upgrade to v23.1.10 and higher, **not** to v23.1.9. [#110569](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/110569)

### Contributors

This release includes 2 merged PRs by 2 authors.

Release Date: September 7, 2023

### Docker image

[Multi-platform images](https://docs.docker.com/build/building/multi-platform) include support for both Intel and ARM. Multi-platform images do not take up additional space on your Docker host.

Within the multi-platform image:

- The ARM image is **Experimental** and not yet qualified for production use and not eligible for support or uptime SLA commitments.
- The Intel image is **Generally Available** for production use.

To download the Docker image:

```shell
docker pull cockroachdb/cockroach:v23.1.9
```

### Source tag

To view or download the source code for CockroachDB v23.1.9 on Github, visit [v23.1.9 source tag](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/releases/tag/v23.1.9).

### Changelog

View a detailed changelog on GitHub: [v23.1.8...v23.1.9](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/compare/v23.1.8...v23.1.9)

### General changes

- All <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/upgrade-cockroach-version" data-versioned="true">cluster version upgrades</a> perform a <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/system-catalogs" data-versioned="true">catalog</a> health check and repair upgrade step before proceeding to other upgrade steps. [#105826](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/105826)
- <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/upgrade-cockroach-version" data-versioned="true">
    Upgrading the cluster version
  </a>
  to a new release will not only check for descriptor and other
  <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/system-catalogs" data-versioned="true">
    catalog
  </a>
  corruptions, but will attempt to repair some of them on a best-effort basis. This should seamlessly get rid of all
  longstanding descriptor back-reference corruptions, which typically don't manifest themselves until a
  <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/online-schema-changes" data-versioned="true">
    schema change
  </a>
  or an upgrade are performed. [#106217](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/106217)

### Enterprise edition changes

- <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/create-and-configure-changefeeds" data-versioned="true">
    Changefeeds
  </a>
  should no longer fail when upgrading to
  <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/releases/v23.1#v23-1-5" data-versioned="true">
    v23.1.5
  </a>
  . [#106399](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/106399)
- Fixed an issue where <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/create-changefeed" data-versioned="true">changefeeds</a> emitting to a cloud sink with compression could experience resource leakage (memory and goroutines) when experiencing transient errors. [#106857](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/106857)
- Augmented the credentials lookup chain for the implicit authentication method in Azure storage and KMS to first look for credentials in a file before proceeding on to the rest of the chain specified in the `DefaultAzureCredential` class (env vars, Managed Identity, etc.). The path of this file is specified by the environment variable `COCKROACH_AZURE_APPLICATION_CREDENTIALS_FILE` and, if not empty, is expected to point to a file that provides the Azure Tenant ID, Client ID, and Client Secret that will be used to access the storage or KMS resource in the following YAML format: `azure_tenant_id: MY_TENANT_ID, azure_client_id: MY_CLIENT_ID, azure_client_secret: MY_CLIENT_SECRET` [#106688](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/106688)
- Fixed a rare <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/create-changefeed" data-versioned="true">changefeed</a> issue that was triggered when the parent database or types were dropped, and instead of exiting with a descriptive error message, the changefeed would observe the following opaque error instead: `value type is not BYTES: UNKNOWN`. [#107933](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/107933)
- Fixed a potential deadlock when running <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/create-changefeed" data-versioned="true">changefeeds</a> with the `end_time` option set. [#108074](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/108074)

### SQL language changes

- Added a `crdb_internal.reset_activity_tables` <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/functions-and-operators" data-versioned="true">builtin function</a> to allow users to reset the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cost-based-optimizer#table-statistics" data-versioned="true">statistics</a> in the `system.statement_activity` and `system.transaction_activity` tables. Users require <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/security-reference/authorization#admin-role" data-versioned="true">`admin`</a> to use this builtin. [#106129](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/106129)
- CockroachDB now reports <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/performance-best-practices-overview#transaction-contention" data-versioned="true">contention</a> time encountered while executing the mutation statements ( <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/insert" data-versioned="true">`INSERT`</a>, <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/upsert" data-versioned="true">`UPSERT`</a>, <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/update" data-versioned="true">`UPDATE`</a>, and <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/delete" data-versioned="true">`DELETE`</a> ) when run via <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/explain-analyze" data-versioned="true">`EXPLAIN ANALYZE`</a>. [#106432](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/106432)
- Fixed a bug in <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/copy" data-versioned="true">`COPY CSV WITH HEADER`</a> that was first introduced in <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/releases/v23.1" data-versioned="true">v23.1</a>. On previous versions of CockroachDB, a workaround is to disable <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/vectorized-execution" data-versioned="true">vectorized</a> `COPY` by setting the `vectorize` <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/set-vars#supported-variables" data-versioned="true">session variable</a> to `false` or to remove the header row from the `COPY` data. [#106967](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/106967)
- Added a new boolean <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cluster-settings" data-versioned="true">cluster setting</a> `sql.telemetry.query_sampling.internal.enabled`. If `true`, internal app queries will be reported to telemetry when query sampling to telemetry is enabled. [#107182](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/107182)
- The `SHOW QUERIES` and <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/show-sessions" data-versioned="true">`SHOW SESSIONS`</a> commands will now display timestamps using the session's timezone setting. [#108144](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/108144)
- Added the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cluster-settings" data-versioned="true">cluster setting</a> `sql.stats.limit_table_size.enabled`, which controls whether or not we enforce the row limit set by the `sql.stats.persisted_rows.max` cluster setting in the `system.statement_statistics` and `system.transaction_statistics` tables. [#108913](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/108913)
- Optimized the `sql-stats-compaction` <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/show-jobs" data-versioned="true">job</a> 's <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/delete" data-versioned="true">delete query</a> to avoid a <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/sql-tuning-with-explain#issue-full-table-scans" data-versioned="true">full scan</a>. This helps avoid a <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/common-errors#restart-transaction" data-versioned="true">transaction retry error</a> which can cause the job to fail. [#108990](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/108990)
- Introspection queries will now show the internal `node` user as the owner of tables in <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/pg-catalog" data-versioned="true">`pg_catalog`</a> and <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/information-schema" data-versioned="true">`information_schema`</a>. Previously, the owner was shown as `admin`, but that was inaccurate since users with <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/security-reference/authorization#admin-role" data-versioned="true">the `admin` role</a> could not modify these tables in any way. [#109736](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/109736)

### Operational changes

- Added two new <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/metrics" data-versioned="true">metrics</a> to monitor <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/configure-replication-zones#lease_preferences" data-versioned="true">lease range preference</a> conformance: `leases.preferences.violating` indicates the number of valid leases a <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cockroach-start#store" data-versioned="true">store</a> owns that satisfy none of the preferences applied; `leases.preferences.less-preferred` indicates the number of valid leases a store owns that satisfy some of the preferences applied, but not the first preference. [#107622](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/107622)
- Added the `kv.enqueue_in_replicate_queue_on_span_config_update.enabled` <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cluster-settings" data-versioned="true">cluster setting.</a>. When set to `true`, <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cockroach-start#store" data-versioned="true">stores</a> in the cluster will enqueue <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/architecture/overview#architecture-replica" data-versioned="true">replicas</a> for <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/architecture/replication-layer" data-versioned="true">replication changes</a> upon receiving config updates which could affect the replica. This setting is off by default. Enabling this setting speeds up how quickly config-triggered replication changes begin, but adds additional CPU overhead. The overhead scales with the number of leaseholders. [#108816](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/108816)
- The RPC dial and heartbeat timeouts can now be configured via the following environment variables: `COCKROACH_RPC_DIAL_TIMEOUT`, which defaults to 2x the value of `COCKROACH_NETWORK_TIMEOUT`; `COCKROACH_RPC_HEARTBEAT_TIMEOUT`, which defaults to 3x `COCKROACH_NETWORK_TIMEOUT`. This allows configuring these values independently of <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/architecture/distribution-layer#grpc" data-versioned="true">`COCKROACH_NETWORK_TIMEOUT`</a>, which defaults to 2s. [#109359](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/109359)
- The default gRPC server-side send timeout has been increased from 2 seconds to 4 seconds (that is, from 1x to 2x the default value of <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/architecture/distribution-layer#grpc" data-versioned="true">`COCKROACH_NETWORK_TIMEOUT`</a> ), to avoid spurious connection failures in certain scenarios. This can be controlled via the new environment variable `COCKROACH_RPC_SERVER_TIMEOUT`. [#109621](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/109621)
- Added a new gauge <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/metrics" data-versioned="true">metric</a> `sql.schema.invalid_objects`. This gauge is periodically updated based on the schedule set by the `sql.schema.telemetry.recurrence` <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cluster-settings" data-versioned="true">cluster setting</a>. When the metric is updated, it counts the number of schema objects ( <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/create-table" data-versioned="true">tables</a>, <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/create-type" data-versioned="true">types</a>, <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/create-schema" data-versioned="true">schemas</a>, <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/create-database" data-versioned="true">databases</a>, and <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/user-defined-functions" data-versioned="true">functions</a> ) that are in an invalid state according to CockroachDB's internal validation checks. This metric is expected to be zero ( `0` ) in a healthy cluster. If it is not zero, it indicates that there is a problem that must be repaired. [#109739](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/109739)
- The <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cluster-settings" data-versioned="true">cluster setting</a> `kv.allocator.lease_rebalance_threshold` can now be used to control the minimum fraction away from the mean a <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cockroach-start#store" data-versioned="true">store's</a> lease count before it is considered for lease transfers. The default setting is 0.05. [#105950](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/105950)
- On Linux/ARM64, 16k page sizes are now used in jemalloc. This allows Linux/ARM64 users with 16k pages to run `cockroach`. [#107131](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/107131)

### DB Console changes

- The generic DB Console "unexpected error" message now includes details about the actual error, along with other context to make it easier to root cause. [#106404](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/106404)
- Fixed a bug where the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/ui-jobs-page" data-versioned="true">job details page</a> would flicker between the job details and a loading animation when a job was still executing. [#106153](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/106153)
- Added a timescale label to the **Diagnostics** tab of the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/ui-statements-page" data-versioned="true">Statement Details page</a>. Users are now able to see the time window for which the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/explain-analyze#explain-analyze-debug" data-versioned="true">statement diagnostics</a> are displayed. [#107082](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/107082)
- Fixed the options selection in the **Sort** dropdown on the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/ui-network-latency-page" data-versioned="true">Network Latency page</a>. [#107213](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/107213)
- Search is performed on all ID fields of the **Transaction Executions** and **Statement Executions** views on the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/ui-insights-page" data-versioned="true">Insights Page</a>. [#107762](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/107762)
- Enabled the `Now` option on the time picker that appears on several pages of the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/ui-overview" data-versioned="true">DB Console</a>. [#107837](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/107837)

### Bug fixes

- Fixed a bug where the **node** and **regions** columns on the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/ui-databases-page" data-versioned="true">Databases Page</a> did not properly render. This column is shown for clusters with more than 1 node. [#105824](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/105824)
- Fixed an internal error when using <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/explain#types-option" data-versioned="true">`EXPLAIN (TYPES)`</a> on a <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/delete" data-versioned="true">`DELETE FROM... USING... RETURNING`</a> statement. This error was introduced in v23.1.0. [#106196](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/106196)
- Fixed a bug which manifested itself in error messages containing "failed to drop all of the relevant elements" when executing DDL statements with the declarative <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/online-schema-changes" data-versioned="true">schema changer</a>. What this really means is that there's a concurrent schema change that is ongoing. Instead we now behave as expected and wait for it to finish. [#106286](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/106286)
- Fixed a panic executing <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/create-table-as" data-versioned="true">`CREATE AS`</a> with `pg_catalog.pg_prepared_statements` as a source. For example: <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/create-table-as" data-versioned="true">`CREATE TABLE t AS SELECT * FROM pg_catalog.pg_prepared_statements`</a>; <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/create-view" data-versioned="true">`CREATE MATERIALIZED VIEW v AS SELECT * FROM pg_catalog.pg_prepared_statements`</a>. [#106274](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/106274)
- Fixed a panic executing <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/create-table-as" data-versioned="true">`CREATE AS`</a> with `pg_catalog.cursors` as a source. For example: <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/create-table-as" data-versioned="true">`CREATE TABLE t AS SELECT * FROM pg_catalog.pg_cursors`</a>; <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/create-view" data-versioned="true">`CREATE MATERIALIZED VIEW v AS SELECT * FROM pg_catalog.pg_cursors`</a>. [#106274](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/106274)
- Fixed a panic executing <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/create-table-as" data-versioned="true">`CREATE AS`</a> with `crdb_internal.create_statements` as a source. For example: <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/create-table-as" data-versioned="true">`CREATE TABLE t AS SELECT * FROM crdb_internal.create_statements`</a>; <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/create-view" data-versioned="true">`CREATE MATERIALIZED VIEW v AS SELECT * FROM crdb_internal.create_statements`</a>. [#106274](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/106274)
- Fixed a bug where the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/ui-key-visualizer" data-versioned="true">Key Visualizer</a> was crashing with an "invalid conversion to int" message. [#106357](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/106357)
- Fixed a bug in the declarative <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/online-schema-changes" data-versioned="true">schema changer</a> where adding a <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/foreign-key" data-versioned="true">foreign key</a> or setting a column to `NOT NULL` with a non-existent column produced an assertion error instead of the proper pgcode. [#105719](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/105719)
- <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/show-schemas" data-versioned="true">
    `SHOW SCHEMAS FROM db_name`
  </a>
  will no longer incorrectly show schemas from the current database when the current database has a schema named
  `db_name`. [#106199](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/106199)
- Fixed a bug in <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cost-based-optimizer" data-versioned="true">optimizer</a> row count estimates of a scan from a partitioned <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/partial-indexes" data-versioned="true">partial index</a>, which may cause an underestimated row count or a panic if the row count goes to zero. [#106309](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/106309)
- Fixed a bug where a <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/transactions#transaction-retries" data-versioned="true">transaction retry</a> during the backfill of the `job_type` column in the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/show-jobs" data-versioned="true">jobs table</a> could result in some job records with no `job_type` value. [#106412](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/106412)
- Fixed a bug where some <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/indexes" data-versioned="true">secondary indexes</a> would incorrectly be treated internally as <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/primary-key" data-versioned="true">primary indexes</a>, which could cause some <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/online-schema-changes" data-versioned="true">schema change</a> operations to fail. The bug could occur if <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/alter-table#alter-primary-key" data-versioned="true">`ALTER TABLE... ALTER PRIMARY KEY`</a> was used on CockroachDB <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/releases/v21.1" data-versioned="true">v21.1</a> or earlier, and the cluster was upgraded. [#106426](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/106426)
- In the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/ui-overview" data-versioned="true">DB Console</a>, selecting a database filter from the filters menu in the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/ui-overview#sql-activity" data-versioned="true">SQL Activity Page</a> should function as expected. This fixes a bug where the filter would break and not show any results when the results were retrieved from the statement activity table instead of the persisted table. [#106434](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/106434)
- The statement tag for <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/show-sequences" data-versioned="true">`SHOW SEQUENCES`</a> is now corrected to be `SHOW SEQUENCES` instead of <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/show-schemas" data-versioned="true">`SHOW SCHEMAS`</a>. [#106797](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/106797)
- Fixed a rare bug in which some uploads via <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cockroach-userfile-upload" data-versioned="true">`cockroach userfile upload`</a> would silently upload incorrect data. [#106698](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/106698)
- Under prolonged unavailability (such as loss of <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/architecture/overview#architecture-overview-consensus" data-versioned="true">quorum</a> ), affected <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/architecture/overview#architecture-range" data-versioned="true">ranges</a> would exhibit <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/architecture/replication-layer#raft-logs" data-versioned="true">Raft log</a> growth that was quadratic as a function of the duration of the outage. Now this growth is approximately linear instead. [#106054](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/106054)
- Fixed a bug on the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/metrics" data-versioned="true">**Metrics**</a> page that was causing it to not update automatically on rolling window options. [#106766](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/106766)
- Blocked dropping of <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/indexes" data-versioned="true">indexes</a> impacted by [Technical Advisory 99561](/docs/advisories/a99561) if dropping those indexes could cause data loss to occur. [#106863](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/106863)
- <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cockroach-debug-zip" data-versioned="true">
    Debug zips
  </a>
  are now properly showing the information from
  <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/crdb-internal" data-versioned="true">
    `crdb_internal.cluster_settings`
  </a>
  . The file `crdb_internal.cluster_settings.txt` in debug zips was empty due to this bug on CockroachDB
  <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/releases/v23.1#v23-1-5" data-versioned="true">
    v23.1.5
  </a>
  (which was the only version affected). [#107105](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/107105)
- A bug has been fixed that caused internal errors instead of user errors when queries contained labelled <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/scalar-expressions#tuple-constructors" data-versioned="true">tuples</a> with a different number of elements and labels, e.g., `(ROW(1, 2) AS a)`. This bug had been present since CockroachDB <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/releases/v23.1" data-versioned="true">v23.1.0</a>. [#106959](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/106959)
- Fixed a failing <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/online-schema-changes" data-versioned="true">schema change</a> <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/show-jobs" data-versioned="true">job</a> when <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/create-table-as" data-versioned="true">CREATE TABLE AS</a> or <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/create-view" data-versioned="true">`CREATE MATERIALIZED VIEW AS`</a> sources from a `SHOW` command as in the following examples [#107226](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/107226):
  - `CREATE TABLE t AS SELECT * FROM [SHOW CREATE TABLE tbl];`
  - `CREATE TABLE t AS SELECT * FROM [SHOW INDEXES FROM tbl];`
  - `CREATE TABLE t AS SELECT * FROM [SHOW COLUMNS FROM tbl];`
  - `CREATE TABLE t AS SELECT * FROM [SHOW CONSTRAINTS FROM tbl];`
  - `CREATE TABLE t AS SELECT * FROM [SHOW PARTITIONS FROM TABLE tbl];`
  - `CREATE TABLE t AS SELECT * FROM [SHOW PARTITIONS FROM INDEX tbl@tbl_pkey];`
- Index recommendations in the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/ui-overview" data-versioned="true">DB Console</a> no longer use the fully qualified name of a table to create an index name, allowing the creating of <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/indexes" data-versioned="true">indexes</a> directly from the DB Console to work. [#107218](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/107213)
- Fixed a bug where <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/show-grants" data-versioned="true">`SHOW GRANTS`</a> could fail if any objects were offline, which can happen during a <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/restore" data-versioned="true">`RESTORE`</a>. [#107238](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/107238)
- The `pg_get_serial_sequence` <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/functions-and-operators" data-versioned="true">builtin function</a> can now handle mixed-case names correctly. [#107372](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/107372)
- Fixed a bug with the "SQL statement diagnostic request" <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cluster-api" data-versioned="true">HTTP API</a> that would affect CockroachDB Serverless clusters was fixed. This bug had existed since CockroachDB <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/releases/v22.1" data-versioned="true">v22.1</a>. [#107385](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/107385)
- Fixed a bug where under rare circumstances, a <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/architecture/replication-layer" data-versioned="true">replication</a> change could get stuck when proposed near lease/leadership changes (and likely under overload), and the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/architecture/replication-layer#per-replica-circuit-breakers" data-versioned="true">replica circuit breakers</a> could trip. [#107059](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/107059)
- Fixed a bug in upstream `etcd-io/raft` which could result in pulling unlimited amount of logs into memory, and lead to out-of-memory errors. Now the log scan has a limited memory footprint. [#104483][#104483]
- Fixed a bug where, in rare circumstances, a [replication](https://cockroachlabs.com/docs/v23.1/architecture/replication-layer) could get stuck when proposed near lease or leadership changes, especially under overload, and the [replica circuit breakers]( [../v23.1](https://cockroachlabs.com/docs/v23.1/architecture/replication-layer#per-replica-circuit-breakers) could trip. A previous attempt to fix this issue has been reverted in favor of this fix. [#106515][#106515]
- Fixed a bug in the SQL syntax for <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/create-table-as" data-versioned="true">`CREATE TABLE AS`</a> <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/online-schema-changes" data-versioned="true">schema change</a> <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/show-jobs" data-versioned="true">job</a> description. [#107404](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/107404)
- Fixed an internal error in <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/update" data-versioned="true">`UPDATE`</a>, <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/upsert" data-versioned="true">`UPSERT`</a>, <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/insert" data-versioned="true">`INSERT`</a>, or <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/delete" data-versioned="true">`DELETE`</a> statements run concurrently with <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/alter-table#add-column" data-versioned="true">`ALTER TABLE... ADD COLUMN`</a> of a <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/computed-columns#virtual-computed-columns" data-versioned="true">virtual computed column</a> on the same table. [#107403](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/107403)
- Fixed a bug that caused internal errors when using <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/create-type" data-versioned="true">user-defined types</a> in <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/views" data-versioned="true">views</a> and <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/user-defined-functions" data-versioned="true">user-defined functions</a> that have <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/subqueries" data-versioned="true">subqueries</a>. This bug was present when using views since version v21.2. It was present when using user-defined functions since <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/releases/v23.1" data-versioned="true">v23.1</a>. [#106955](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/106955)
- The timeout duration when loading the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/ui-hot-ranges-page" data-versioned="true">**Hot Ranges** page</a> has been increased to 30 minutes. [#107497](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/107497)
- Fixed the SQL syntax for <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/views#materialized-views" data-versioned="true">`CREATE MATERIALIZED VIEW AS`</a> <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/online-schema-changes" data-versioned="true">schema change</a> <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/show-jobs" data-versioned="true">job</a> descriptions. [#107471](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/107471)
- Reduced <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/performance-best-practices-overview#transaction-contention" data-versioned="true">contention</a> on the `system.statement_statistics` table which has caused the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cost-based-optimizer#table-statistics" data-versioned="true">SQL statistics</a> compaction <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/show-jobs" data-versioned="true">job</a> to fail. [#107573](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/107573)
- The `ST_ClosestPoint` <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/functions-and-operators#spatial-functions" data-versioned="true">spatial function</a> previously did not preserve the correct <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/srid-4326" data-versioned="true">SRID</a> when comparing two different <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/point" data-versioned="true">points</a>. This is now resolved. [#107595](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/107595)
- CockroachDB would previously crash when evaluating the `ST_AsEncodedPolyline` <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/functions-and-operators#spatial-functions" data-versioned="true">builtin function</a> on a <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/geometrycollection" data-versioned="true">`GEOMETRYCOLLECTION` geometry type</a>. The bug was introduced before CockroachDB <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/releases/v22.1" data-versioned="true">v22.1</a> and is now fixed. [#107901](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/107901)
- Fixed a bug where dropping an <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/indexes" data-versioned="true">index</a> could end up failing or cleaning <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/foreign-key" data-versioned="true">foreign keys</a> (when `CASCADE` is specified) on other tables referencing the target table with this index. [#107793](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/107793)
- Fixed a bug where CockroachDB would return an error when using <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/show-range-for-row" data-versioned="true">`SHOW RANGE... FOR ROW...`</a> in a <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/create-table-as" data-versioned="true">`CREATE TABLE AS`</a> construct. [#107603](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/107603)
- Cloud buckets containing <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/backup" data-versioned="true">backups</a> can now be copied via AWS DataSync and other third-party services which insert empty objects with a trailing `/`. Previously, <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/restore" data-versioned="true">restore</a> would fail with the following error message: `read LATEST path: path does not contain a completed latest backup: NoSuchKey`. [#106235](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/106235)
- Fixed a bug where <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/alter-table#drop-column" data-versioned="true">`DROP COLUMN CASCADE`</a> involving a <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/primary-key" data-versioned="true">primary key</a> column could end up hanging. [#107987](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/107987)
- Fixed a nil pointer dereference caused by a race condition when using the `to_char` <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/functions-and-operators" data-versioned="true">builtin function</a>. [#108079](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/108079)
- Since <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/releases/v22.2" data-versioned="true">v22.2.0</a>, using a PTP clock device (enabled by the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cockroach-start#flags-clock-device" data-versioned="true">`--clock-device` flag</a> ) would generate timestamps in the far future. It now generates the correct time. This could cause nodes to crash due to incorrect timestamps, or in the worst case irreversibly advance the cluster's <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/architecture/transaction-layer#time-and-hybrid-logical-clocks" data-versioned="true">HLC clock</a> into the far future. [#108113](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/108113)
- Previously, CockroachDB, when planning expressions containing many sub-expressions (e.g., deeply-nested `AND` / `OR` structures), would use memory quadratic in the number of sub-expressions. In the worst cases (thousands of sub-expressions), this could lead to <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cluster-setup-troubleshooting#out-of-memory-oom-crash" data-versioned="true">OOMs</a>. The bug had been present since at least <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/releases/v22.1" data-versioned="true">v22.1</a> and has now been fixed. [#107368](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/107368)
- When losing a <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/architecture/overview#architecture-leaseholder" data-versioned="true">leaseholder</a> and using <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/configure-replication-zones#lease_preferences" data-versioned="true">lease preferences</a>, the lease can be acquired by any other <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/architecture/overview#architecture-replica" data-versioned="true">replica</a> (regardless of lease preferences) in order to restore availability as soon as possible. The new leaseholder will now immediately check if it violates the lease preferences, and attempt to transfer the lease to a replica that satisfies the preferences if possible. [#107625](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/107625)
- Fixed the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/online-schema-changes" data-versioned="true">schema changer</a> <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/show-jobs" data-versioned="true">job</a> when <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/create-table-as" data-versioned="true">`CREATE AS`</a> sources from <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/show-create#show-the-create-function-statement-for-a-function" data-versioned="true">`SHOW CREATE FUNCTION`</a>, e.g.: `CREATE TABLE t AS SELECT * FROM [SHOW CREATE FUNCTION f]`. [#108195](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/108195)
- Added cancel checking to <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/indexes" data-versioned="true">index</a> constraint initialization code to allow queries to timeout during <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cost-based-optimizer" data-versioned="true">query optimization</a> if analyzing predicates to constrain an index starts using too many resources. Example of setting a timeout using the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/set-vars#statement-timeout" data-versioned="true">`statement_timeout` session setting</a>: `SET statement_timeout='5.0s';` [#106942](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/106942)
- Previously, CockroachDB could encounter an internal error `unexpected non-zero bytes limit for txnKVStreamer` when evaluating <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cost-based-optimizer#locality-optimized-search-in-multi-region-clusters" data-versioned="true">locality-optimized</a> lookup <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/joins" data-versioned="true">joins</a> in case it had to perform the remote regions' lookup. The bug was introduced in <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/releases/v22.2" data-versioned="true">v22.2</a> and is now fixed. A temporary workaround can be accomplished without upgrading by setting the `streamer_enabled` <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/session-variables" data-versioned="true">session variable</a>: `SET streamer_enabled = false;`. [#108251](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/108251)
- Fixed a spurious error `no data source matches prefix` that could occur during <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cost-based-optimizer" data-versioned="true">planning for a query</a> with `DISTINCT ON` and <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/order-by" data-versioned="true">`ORDER BY ASC NULLS LAST`</a> or `ORDER BY DESC NULLS FIRST`. [#108303](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/108303)
- Fixed an <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cost-based-optimizer" data-versioned="true">optimizer</a> costing bug introduced in <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/releases/v23.1" data-versioned="true">v23.1</a> that could cause a query involving two or more <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/joins" data-versioned="true">joins</a> with <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/table-localities#regional-by-row-tables" data-versioned="true">`REGIONAL BY ROW`</a> tables to not pick the most optimal <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/joins#lookup-joins" data-versioned="true">lookup joins</a>. [#108308](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/108308)
- Fixed an <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cost-based-optimizer" data-versioned="true">optimizer</a> costing bug introduced in <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/releases/v23.1" data-versioned="true">v23.1</a> that could cause a query whose best-cost query plan is a string of <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/joins#lookup-joins" data-versioned="true">lookup joins</a> with <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/table-localities#regional-by-row-tables" data-versioned="true">`REGIONAL BY ROW`</a> tables, one after the other in sequence, to not pick the most optimal join plan. [#108308](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/108308)
- Previously, using <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/import-into" data-versioned="true">`IMPORT INTO`</a> for `DELIMITED DATA` or MySQL imports would error with `column... does not exist` if it was importing into a <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/collate" data-versioned="true">collated string</a> column. This is now fixed. [#108286](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/108286)
- Fixed a bug introduced in <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/releases/v23.1" data-versioned="true">v23.1</a> that could cause the precision of some values to be incorrectly truncated for a query with a correlated <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/subqueries" data-versioned="true">subquery</a> and an equality between a column from the subquery and the outer query. This applies to types that are "equivalent" but have different precision levels, e.g., <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/decimal" data-versioned="true">`DECIMAL(10, 0)`</a> vs `DECIMAL(10, 2)` or `NAME` vs <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/string" data-versioned="true">`CHAR`</a>. [#108198](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/108198)
- Fixed a bug where <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/begin-transaction" data-versioned="true">`BEGIN`</a>, <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/commit-transaction" data-versioned="true">`COMMIT`</a>, <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/set-vars" data-versioned="true">`SET`</a>, <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/rollback-transaction" data-versioned="true">`ROLLBACK`</a>, and <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/savepoint" data-versioned="true">`SAVEPOINT`</a> statements would not be written to the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/logging-overview#logging-destinations" data-versioned="true">execution</a> or <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/sql-audit-logging" data-versioned="true">audit logs</a>. [#108411](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/108411)
- Fixed a bug where a session migration performed by `SHOW TRANSFER STATE` would not handle prepared statements that used the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/as-of-system-time" data-versioned="true">`AS OF SYSTEM TIME` clause</a>. Users who encountered this bug would see errors such as `expected 1 or 0 for number of format codes, got N`. This bug was present since <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/releases/v22.2" data-versioned="true">v22.2.0</a>. [#108548](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/108548)
- Fixed errors on the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/ui-sessions-page" data-versioned="true">**Sessions** page</a> in the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/ui-overview" data-versioned="true">DB Console</a> when a session's memory usage is zero bytes. [#108733](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/108733)
- Fixed a bug introduced in <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/releases/v22.1" data-versioned="true">v22.1</a> that could cause a <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/joins" data-versioned="true">join</a> to infinite-loop in rare cases when (1) the join filter is not an equality and (2) no columns from the left input are returned. [#108821](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/108821)
- Fixed an issue with the full scan filter on the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/ui-statements-page" data-versioned="true">**Statements** page</a> where the filter was always evaluating to false, even if a full scan had occurred. [#109254](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/109254)
- Fixed a bug that could cause CPU usage to increase over time. [#109298](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/109298)
- Fixed a bug that could cause some rows to be silently skipped during <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/import" data-versioned="true">`IMPORT`</a> when a node's import worker failed. [#109664](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/109664)
- Fixed a bug in <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/spatial-data-overview" data-versioned="true">geospatial</a> queries, where a query filter of the form `ST_Distance(geog1, geog2) > constant`, or `ST_MaxDistance(geom1, geom2) > constant`, where the operator is one of `>`, `<`, `>=`, `<=`, or a filter of the form `ST_Distance(geog1, geog2, false) = 0` may mistakenly evaluate to `true` when one or both of the inputs is `NULL` or an empty <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/architecture/glossary#geography" data-versioned="true">geography</a> or <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/architecture/glossary#geometry" data-versioned="true">geometry</a>. More rows could be returned by the query than expected. [#109395](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/109395)
- Fixed an issue where a <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/architecture/distribution-layer#range-splits" data-versioned="true">split</a> can be called on an invalid key that's in the form of `someValidKey.Next()` during <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/restore" data-versioned="true">restore</a>. This split key can land in the middle of a row with <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/column-families" data-versioned="true">column families</a>, and thus result in failing SQL queries when querying the restored table. [#109778](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/109778)
- Fixed an issue where a <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/architecture/distribution-layer#range-splits" data-versioned="true">split</a> can be called on an invalid key that's in the form of `someValidKey.Next()` during <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/restore" data-versioned="true">restore</a> with the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cluster-settings" data-versioned="true">cluster setting</a> `bulkio.restore.use_simple_import_spans=true`. This split key can land in the middle of a row with <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/column-families" data-versioned="true">column families</a>, and thus result in failing SQL queries when querying the restored table. [#109939](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/109939)
- Fixed a bug that caused a flood of requests to refresh <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cluster-settings" data-versioned="true">cluster settings</a> on the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/ui-debug-pages#configuration" data-versioned="true">Advanced Debug page</a>. If a user would like to see the effect of a modified cluster setting in <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/ui-overview" data-versioned="true">DB Console</a>, a page reload is now required. [#108125](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/108125)

### Performance improvements

- <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/backup-and-restore-overview" data-versioned="true">
    Backups
  </a>
  no longer perform work proportional to the number of pending
  <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/architecture/transaction-layer#write-intents" data-versioned="true">
    write intents
  </a>
  that they encounter, so they are more than 100x faster when encountering long-running, bulk writing transactions.
  [#105526](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/105526)
- Queries that access <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/pg-catalog" data-versioned="true">`pg_catalog`</a> and <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/information-schema" data-versioned="true">`information_schema`</a> that perform introspection on other tables in those schemas are now significantly faster. [#109736](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/109736)

### Contributors

This release includes 378 merged PRs by 67 authors.

### Docker image

[Multi-platform images](https://docs.docker.com/build/building/multi-platform) include support for both Intel and ARM. Multi-platform images do not take up additional space on your Docker host.

Within the multi-platform image:

- The ARM image is **Experimental** and not yet qualified for production use and not eligible for support or uptime SLA commitments.
- The Intel image is **Generally Available** for production use.

To download the Docker image:

```shell
docker pull cockroachdb/cockroach:v23.1.8
```

### Source tag

To view or download the source code for CockroachDB v23.1.8 on Github, visit [v23.1.8 source tag](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/releases/tag/v23.1.8).

### Changelog

View a detailed changelog on GitHub: [v23.1.7...v23.1.8](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/compare/v23.1.7...v23.1.8)

### Enterprise edition changes

- <a
    href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cloud-storage-authentication?filters=azure#azure-blob-storage-implicit-authentication"
    data-versioned="true"
  >
    Azure Blob Storage credentials for implicit authentication
  </a>
  can now be stored in a file with the following YAML format:

  ```yaml
  azure_tenant_id: {MY_TENANT_ID},
  azure_client_id: {MY_CLIENT_ID},
  azure_client_secret: {MY_CLIENT_SECRET}
  ```

  Set the environment variable `COCKROACH_AZURE_APPLICATION_CREDENTIALS_FILE` to the path of the file. The implicit authentication method first attempts to authenticate using credentials in the file before attempting to authenticate using any other credentials specified in the [`DefaultAzureCredential` class](https://learn.microsoft.com/dotnet/api/azure.identity.defaultazurecredential?view=azure-dotnet), such as environment variables and Managed Identity. These credentials can also be used for <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/take-and-restore-encrypted-backups#use-key-management-service" data-versioned="true">encrypted backups</a>. [#106688](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/106688)

### Bug fixes

- Fixed a bug where <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/drop-index" data-versioned="true">`DROP INDEX... CASCADE`</a> could drop unrelated <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/foreign-key" data-versioned="true">foreign key constraints</a>. For example, if `DROP INDEX... CASCADE` was executed on a unique index for a `Table A`, and if a `Table B` had a foreign key reference to `Table A`, unrelated outbound foreign key constraints on `Table B` would be dropped. [#107793](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/107793)
- Fixed a bug that would result in corruption of <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/security-reference/encryption#encryption-at-rest" data-versioned="true">encrypted data at rest on a cluster node</a>. If a node with this corrupted state was restarted, the node could fail to rejoin the cluster. If multiple nodes encountered this bug at the same time during roll out, the cluster could lose <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/architecture/replication-layer#overview" data-versioned="true">quorum</a>. For more information, refer to [Technical Advisory 106617](/docs/advisories/a106617). [#107277](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/107277)

### Contributors

This release includes 5 merged PRs by 5 authors.
