### Docker image

[Multi-platform images](https://docs.docker.com/build/building/multi-platform) include support for both Intel and ARM. Multi-platform images do not take up additional space on your Docker host.

Within the multi-platform image:

- The ARM image is **Experimental** and not yet qualified for production use and not eligible for support or uptime SLA commitments.
- The Intel image is **Generally Available** for production use.

To download the Docker image:

```shell
docker pull cockroachdb/cockroach:v23.1.7
```

### Source tag

To view or download the source code for CockroachDB v23.1.7 on Github, visit [v23.1.7 source tag](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/releases/tag/v23.1.7).

### Changelog

View a detailed changelog on GitHub: [v23.1.6...v23.1.7](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/compare/v23.1.6...v23.1.7)

### SQL language changes

- Added the `crdb_internal.reset_activity_tables` <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/functions-and-operators" data-versioned="true">built-in function</a> to allow users to reset the statistics in the `system.{statement|transaction}_activity` tables. Users require the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/security-reference/authorization#admin-role" data-versioned="true">`admin` role</a> to use this built-in function. [#106129](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/106129)
- Added the `sql.telemetry.query_sampling.internal.enabled` <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cluster-settings" data-versioned="true">cluster setting</a>, which is `false` by default. If set to `true`, internal app queries will be reported to <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/logging#telemetry" data-versioned="true">telemetry</a> when query sampling to telemetry is <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/configure-logs" data-versioned="true">enabled</a>. [#107182](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/107182)

### DB Console changes

- Added a timescale label to the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/ui-statements-page#diagnostics" data-versioned="true">**Diagnostics** tab</a> of the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/ui-statements-page" data-versioned="true">**Statement Details** page</a>. The time window for the statement diagnostics is now displayed. [#107082](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/107082)
- Increased the timeout duration for loading the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/ui-hot-ranges-page" data-versioned="true">**Hot Ranges** page</a> to 30 minutes. [#107497](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/107497)

### Bug fixes

- The **Regions/Nodes** column on the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/ui-databases-page" data-versioned="true">**Database** and **Database Details** pages</a> will now render properly. This column displays for clusters with more than 1 node. [#105824](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/105824)
- Fixed a bug where the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/ui-jobs-page#job-details" data-versioned="true">**Job Details** page</a> would flicker between the job details and a loading animation while a job is still executing. [#106153](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/106153)
- Fixed a bug where the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/ui-key-visualizer" data-versioned="true">**Key Visualizer** page</a> would crash due to an invalid conversion to `int` error. [#106357](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/106357)
- Fixed a bug that caused an infinite re-render on the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/ui-key-visualizer" data-versioned="true">**Key Visualizer** page</a> when a custom time period was selected. [#106430](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/106430)
- Fixed a bug on the **SQL Activity**, <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/ui-statements-page" data-versioned="true">**Statements** page</a> where the database filter would not return results even when statements existed for the selected database. This is now fixed so that selecting a database filter from the filters menu on the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/ui-statements-page" data-versioned="true">**Statements** page</a> will function as expected. [#106434](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/106434)
- Fixed a bug where the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/ui-overview-dashboard" data-versioned="true">**Metrics** page</a> was not updating automatically on rolling window options. [#106766](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/106766)
- Fixed a bug where <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/ui-statements-page#diagnostics" data-versioned="true">statement diagnostics</a> on the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/ui-statements-page" data-versioned="true">**Statements** page</a> were not always showing. This is now fixed with statement diagnostics displaying for the correct time period. [#106766](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/106766)
- Fixed a bug where the **Sort** dropdown on the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/ui-network-latency-page" data-versioned="true">**Network Latency** page</a> would not persist the selected value because a page reload was triggered. [#107213](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/107213)
- Fixed a bug where the index recommendation on the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/ui-insights-page" data-versioned="true">**Insights** page</a> would use the fully qualified table name to create an index name, which would cause an error due to the invalid syntax. Indexes can now be created directly from the DB Console without encountering this error. [#107218](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/107213)
- Fixed a bug where <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/change-data-capture-overview" data-versioned="true">changefeeds</a> would fail when upgrading to version [v23.1.5](#v23-1-5) because the job record did not have a `clusterID` field set. [#106399](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/106399)
- Fixed a bug where `UPDATE`, `UPSERT`, `DELETE` statements running concurrently with <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/alter-table#add-column" data-versioned="true">`ALTER TABLE..ADD COLUMN`</a> of a virtual computed column on the same table would fail. [#107403](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/107403)
- Fixed a bug where <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/show-jobs#show-automatic-jobs" data-versioned="true">SQL statistics compaction jobs</a> would fail. This is now fixed by reducing the contention on the `system.statement_statistics` table. [#107573](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/107573)
- Fixed a bug where running a <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/change-data-capture-overview" data-versioned="true">changefeed</a> that targets a table with a user-defined type column and with the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/create-changefeed#envelope" data-versioned="true">`envelope` option</a> set to any value other than `wrapped` would cause a node panic due to a nil dereference. [#119746][119746]

### Contributors

This release includes 16 merged PRs by 11 authors.

### Docker image

[Multi-platform images](https://docs.docker.com/build/building/multi-platform) include support for both Intel and ARM. Multi-platform images do not take up additional space on your Docker host.

Within the multi-platform image:

- The ARM image is **Experimental** and not yet qualified for production use and not eligible for support or uptime SLA commitments.
- The Intel image is **Generally Available** for production use.

To download the Docker image:

```shell
docker pull cockroachdb/cockroach:v23.1.6
```

### Source tag

To view or download the source code for CockroachDB v23.1.6 on Github, visit [v23.1.6 source tag](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/releases/tag/v23.1.6).

### Changelog

View a detailed changelog on GitHub: [v23.1.5...v23.1.6](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/compare/v23.1.5...v23.1.6)

### Bug fixes

- Fixed a bug in v23.1.5 where <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cockroach-debug-zip" data-versioned="true">debug zips</a> were empty in the `crdb_internal.cluster_settings.txt` file. Debug zips now properly show the information from `cluster_settings`. [#107105](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/107105)
- Fixed a bug where some primary indexes would incorrectly be treated internally as secondary indexes, which could cause schema change operations to fail. The bug could occur if <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/alter-table#alter-primary-key" data-versioned="true">`ALTER PRIMARY KEY`</a> was used on v21.1 or earlier, and the cluster was upgraded. [#106426](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/106426)
- Extended the `cockroach debug doctor` to detect <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/indexes" data-versioned="true">indexes</a> which could potentially lose data by being dropped when a column is stored inside them and added a check inside <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/drop-index" data-versioned="true">`DROP INDEX`</a> to prevent dropping indexes with this problem to avoid data loss. [#106863](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/106863)

### Contributors

This release includes 3 merged PRs by 15 authors.

### Docker image

[Multi-platform images](https://docs.docker.com/build/building/multi-platform) include support for both Intel and ARM. Multi-platform images do not take up additional space on your Docker host.

Within the multi-platform image:

- The ARM image is **Experimental** and not yet qualified for production use and not eligible for support or uptime SLA commitments.
- The Intel image is **Generally Available** for production use.

To download the Docker image:

```shell
docker pull cockroachdb/cockroach:v23.1.5
```

### Source tag

To view or download the source code for CockroachDB v23.1.5 on Github, visit [v23.1.5 source tag](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/releases/tag/v23.1.5).

### Changelog

View a detailed changelog on GitHub: [v23.1.4...v23.1.5](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/compare/v23.1.4...v23.1.5)

### Security updates

- The full set of TLS ciphers that was present in v22.1 have been included in the existing cipher suites list, which can be enabled with the `COCKROACH_TLS_ENABLE_OLD_CIPHER_SUITES` environment variable. [#105370](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/105370)

### Enterprise edition changes

- Added new <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cluster-settings" data-versioned="true">cluster settings</a> in the `server.oidc_authentication.generate_cluster_sso_token` namespace that support using OIDC to generate a <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/sso-sql" data-versioned="true">JWT auth token for cluster SSO</a>. [#105643](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/105643)

### SQL language changes

- Improved the inline documentation and error messages related to <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/show-ranges" data-versioned="true">`SHOW RANGES`</a>. [#105278](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/105278)
- Inbound <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/foreign-key" data-versioned="true">foreign keys</a> on TTL tables are now allowed. [#105341](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/105341)
- Added the columns `default_value` and `origin` ( with the values `default`, `override`, `external-override` ) to the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/show-cluster-setting" data-versioned="true">`SHOW CLUSTER SETTING`</a> command. [#105452](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/105452)
- Added the `VIEWACTIVITY` and `VIEWACTIVITYREDACTED` <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/security-reference/authorization#supported-privileges" data-versioned="true">system privileges</a> for the `crdb_internal.cluster_queries` and `crdb_internal.node_queries` <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/crdb-internal" data-versioned="true">tables</a>. [#105467](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/105467)
- Fixed the error message to be more understandable when attempting to create <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/user-defined-functions" data-versioned="true">UDFs</a> under a virtual or temporary schema. [#105627](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/105627)

### Command-line changes

- Running <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cockroach-node#node-decommission" data-versioned="true">`cockroch node decommission <nodeID>`</a> for a node that has already been decommissioned will now exit with code 0, as had been the case in CockroachDB versions prior to v23.1.0. [#103933](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/103933)

### DB Console changes

- The <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/ui-hot-ranges-page#range-report" data-versioned="true">**Range Report** page</a> (route `/reports/range/:rangeID` ) shows the **Hot Ranges** menu item as highlighted in the left-side menu. The back button in the **Range Report** page redirects back to the **Hot Ranges** page. [#104980](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/104980)
- Added description to the tooltip for the `Idle` status only for the Active Transactions view. Excluded `Idle` status filter option for the Active Statements view. [#105062](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/105062)

### Bug fixes

- Added more precision to small percentage values on the percentage bars on the DB Console. [#105078](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/105078)
- Fixed a crash when using `DurationToNumber` with empty duration object on SQL Activity tables. [#105152](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/105152)
- `SpanStats` is no longer subject to stale information, and should be considered authoritative. [#105000](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/105000)
- Fixed a bug in MuxRangefeed implementation that may cause MuxRangefeed to become stuck if enough ranges encountered certain error concurrently. [#105186](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/105186)
- <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/show-jobs" data-versioned="true">
    `SHOW CHANGEFEED JOBS`
  </a>
  no longer fails on v22.2 and v23.1 mixed-version clusters.
  [#105008](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/105008)
- <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/grant" data-versioned="true">
    `GRANT SYSTEM ALL...`
  </a>
  no longer causes the grantee to be unable to log in. This was due to a bug where `ALL` would include the `NOSQLLOGIN`
  <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/security-reference/authorization#supported-privileges" data-versioned="true">
    system privilege
  </a>
  . Since `NOSQLLOGIN` is the only "negative" privilege, it is now excluded from the `ALL` shorthand, and must be
  granted explicitly in order to restrict logins. [#105080](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/105080)
- CockroachDB previously could encounter `zero transaction timestamp in EvalContext` when evaluating the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/copy" data-versioned="true">`COPY FROM`</a> command. The bug was introduced in v23.1.0 and is now fixed. [#105295](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/105295)
- Fixed the data fetching for the **Database** and **Table Details** pages. Prior to this change, some databases/tables could be permanently stuck in a loading state, causing their corresponding page to permanently show a spinner. This change fixes the data fetching for these pages to ensure all databases and tables are loaded correctly. [#105315](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/105315)
- Fixed a bug where <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/insert" data-versioned="true">`INSERT.. ON CONFLICT.. DO UPDATE`</a> queries incorrectly resulted in an "ambiguous column" error. The bug only presented if the target table had a computed column with an expression referencing a column with a `DEFAULT` value. [#105025](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/105025)
- On the **SQL Statistics** pages, a transaction query is now available as long as the statement fingerprints associated with the transaction also exist in the payload. [#105318](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/105318)
- Previously, CockroachDB would crash when evaluating <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/create-table" data-versioned="true">`CREATE TABLE.. AS or CREATE MATERIALIZED VIEW.. AS`</a> statements when the `AS` clause selected data from `crdb_internal.cluster_statement_statistics` or `crdb_internal.cluster_transaction_statistics` virtual tables. The bug has been present since at least v22.1 and is now fixed. [#105325](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/105325)
- Fixed a source of mutex contention within the storage engine that could increase tail latencies on high-CPU, high-throughput deployments. [#105361](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/105361)
- Fixed a bug where nodes could terminate with the following message: `server startup failed: cockroach server exited with error: ‹migration-job-find-already-completed›: key range id:X is unavailable: ‹failed to send RPC: no replica node information available via gossip for rX›`. [#104246](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/104246)
- Previously, cross-database type references were allowed through `CREATE TABLE...AS` statements if the source table was from another database and any of its columns was of a user-defined type. This introduced a bug where the source table could be dropped and the type could not be found for the CTAS table. This commit disallows such CTAS as a fix. [#105621](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/105621)
- CockroachDB can now automatically delete statistics for dropped tables from `system.table_statistics` table. However, out of caution, this mechanism is disabled by default on v23.1 releases. [#105479](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/105479)
- Fixed a race condition that can occur when multiple SQL servers are created simultaneously, causing simultaneous writes to an unprotected global variable used to configure a CCL audit logging feature. [#105725](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/105725)
- Previously, referencing a user-defined type in the body of a <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/user-defined-functions" data-versioned="true">user-defined function</a> would result in an error at the time of creating the function. This is now fixed. [#105617](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/105617)
- CockroachDB now returns an error during <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/user-defined-functions" data-versioned="true">UDF</a> creation if an input argument has type `RECORD`. [#105735](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/105735)

### Performance improvements

- If the `sql.optimizer.uniqueness_checks_for_gen_random_uuid.enabled` <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cluster-settings" data-versioned="true">cluster setting</a> is disabled, the optimizer can now eliminate uniqueness checks for `STRING` and `BYTES` columns when the value is set to `gen_random_uuid()` (with an implicit or explicit cast to `STRING` or `BYTES` ). If you still want the checks, you can set `sql.optimizer.uniqueness_checks_for_gen_random_uuid.enabled` to `true` (the default is `false` ). [#105446](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/105446)

### Contributors

This release includes 115 merged PRs by 44 authors.

        <a href="https://binaries.cockroachdb.com/cockroach-sql-v23.1.4.windows-6.2-amd64.zip">
          cockroach-sql-v23.1.4.windows-6.2-amd64.zip
        </a>
        <br />(
        <a href="https://binaries.cockroachdb.com/cockroach-sql-v23.1.4.windows-6.2-amd64.zip.sha256sum">SHA256</a>)
      </td>
    </tr>
  </tbody>
</table>

### Docker image

[Multi-platform images](https://docs.docker.com/build/building/multi-platform) include support for both Intel and ARM. Multi-platform images do not take up additional space on your Docker host.

Within the multi-platform image:

- The ARM image is **Experimental** and not yet qualified for production use and not eligible for support or uptime SLA commitments.
- The Intel image is **Generally Available** for production use.

To download the Docker image:

```shell
docker pull cockroachdb/cockroach:v23.1.4
```

### Source tag

To view or download the source code for CockroachDB v23.1.4 on Github, visit [v23.1.4 source tag](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/releases/tag/v23.1.4).

### Changelog

View a detailed changelog on GitHub: [v23.1.3...v23.1.4](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/compare/v23.1.3...v23.1.4)

### Security updates

- The new <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cluster-settings#setting-sql-auth-createrole-allows-grant-role-membership-enabled" data-versioned="true">`sql.auth.createrole_allows_grant_role_membership.enabled`</a> cluster setting allows a user with the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/create-user#role-options" data-versioned="true">`CREATEROLE` role option</a> to grant and revoke non-admin roles. This cluster setting defaults to `false`, but is expected to become the default behavior in the future. [#104445](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/104445)

### Enterprise edition changes

- Fixed an initialization race condition in <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/changefeed-examples" data-versioned="true">changefeed schema feeds</a> that could cause a node to crash with a null pointer exception. [#104934](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/104934)

### SQL language changes

- Users with <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/security-reference/authorization#supported-privileges" data-versioned="true">`MODIFYSQLCLUSTERSETTING`</a> can now view only `sql.defaults` <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cluster-settings" data-versioned="true">cluster settings</a> instead of all cluster settings. [#104542](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/104542)

### Operational changes

- The <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cockroach-debug-zip" data-versioned="true">`debug.zip`</a> archive now contains the files formerly located at `nodes/*/ranges/*.json` in one file per node, `nodes/*/ranges.json`. [#104248](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/104248)
- The `http-defaults` and `http-servers` sections of the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/configure-logs" data-versioned="true">log config</a> will now accept a `headers` field containing a map of key-value string pairs which will comprise custom HTTP headers appended to every request. Additionally, a `compression` value can now be set to `gzip` or `none` to select a compression method for the HTTP request body. By default, `gzip` is selected. Previous functionality did not compress by default. [#104814](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/104814)

### Command-line changes

- The new log config option <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/configure-logs#log-buffering-for-network-sinks" data-versioned="true">`buffering`</a> allows you to <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/configure-logs#file-logging-format" data-versioned="true">format buffer output as JSON arrays</a>. This is useful for APIs that consume JSON arrays, such as the Datadog logs API. [#104790](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/104790)

### DB Console changes

- The DB Console overview page now displays a warning when all nodes are running on a new version but the cluster upgrade has not been finalized. [#104874](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/104874)
- The histogram window merge calculation now interpolates quantile values more accurately, and <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/ui-overview#metrics" data-versioned="true">**Metrics** charts</a> in the DB Console are smoother and more accurate. [#104815](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/104815)

### Bug fixes

- Fixed a bug where a transaction retry could miss job rows during the backfill of the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/ui-jobs-page#jobs-table" data-versioned="true">**Jobs** table</a>. [#104757](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/104757)
- Fixed a bug where admin or root user privileges were erroneously required to use <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/show-system-grants" data-versioned="true">`SHOW SYSTEM GRANTS`</a>. [#104732](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/104732)
- Fixed a bug that prevented display of the column selector on the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/ui-jobs-page" data-versioned="true">**Jobs** page</a>. [#104738](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/104738)
- Fixed a bug where an invalid split could crash and prevent restarts of nodes that hold a replica for the right-hand side. [#104850](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/104850)
- Fixed the `debug recover make-plan` command to ignore partial range metadata when the metadata can't be fully read, and instead rely solely on replica info from storage to produce the recovery plan. [#104774](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/104774)
- Fixed a metric bug that could cause volumes such as RAID logical volumes to be counted twice. [#104806](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/104806)
- Fixed a bug in `upstream etcd-io/raft` which could cause an unlimited amount of log to be loaded into memory. This could cause a node to crash with an out-of-memory (OOM) exception. The log scan now has a limited memory footprint. [#104968](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/104968)

### Contributors

This release includes 53 merged PRs by 30 authors.

## v23.1.3

Release Date: June 13, 2023

<Warning>
  A [bug](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/issues/104798) was discovered in a change included in v23.1.3 (this
  release). This bug can affect clusters upgrading to v23.1.3 from{" "}
  <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/releases/v22.2" data-versioned="true">
    v22.2.x
  </a>
  . In an affected cluster, jobs that were running during the upgrade could hang or fail to run after the upgrade is
  finalized. Users upgrading from v22.2.x are advised to use [v23.1.2](#v23-1-2) to upgrade, or to set the{" "}
  <a
    href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/upgrade-cockroach-version#step-3-decide-how-the-upgrade-will-be-finalized"
    data-versioned="true"
  >
    `cluster.preserve_downgrade_option`
  </a>{" "}
  cluster setting to delay finalization of the upgrade until they can upgrade to v23.1.4.
</Warning>

### Docker image

[Multi-platform images](https://docs.docker.com/build/building/multi-platform) include support for both Intel and ARM. Multi-platform images do not take up additional space on your Docker host.

Within the multi-platform image:

- The ARM image is **Experimental** and not yet qualified for production use and not eligible for support or uptime SLA commitments.
- The Intel image is **Generally Available** for production use.

To download the Docker image:

```shell
docker pull cockroachdb/cockroach:v23.1.3
```

### Source tag

To view or download the source code for CockroachDB v23.1.3 on Github, visit [v23.1.3 source tag](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/releases/tag/v23.1.3).

### Changelog

View a detailed changelog on GitHub: [v23.1.2...v23.1.3](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/compare/v23.1.2...v23.1.3)

### Security updates

- The new `server.client_cert_expiration_cache.capacity` <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cluster-settings" data-versioned="true">cluster setting</a> allows you to configure the minimum time until a user's set of client certificates will expire. When `server.client_cert_expiration_cache.capacity` is set to a non-zero value, the new metric `security.certificate.expiration.client` tracks the number of client certificates that have expired. [#104165](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/104165)

### Enterprise edition changes

- Role-based audit logging is now an Enterprise feature. Only Enterprise users will be able to configure role-based audit logging using the `sql.log.user_audit` <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cluster-settings" data-versioned="true">cluster setting</a>. [#104453](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/104453)
- The new `sql.log.user_audit` <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cluster-settings" data-versioned="true">cluster setting</a> enables role-based auditing. When the setting is enabled, you can set an audit logging configuration using a table-like syntax. Each row in the configuration represents an _audit setting_ in the configuration. An audit setting is comprised of the following columns: `USER/ROLE` and `STATEMENT_FILTER`:

  ```sql
  SET CLUSTER SETTING sql.log.user_audit = '
      test_role       ALL
      another_role    NONE
      ALL             NONE
  ';
  ```

  [#104179](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/104179)

- Introduced the `sql.log.user_audit.reduced_config.enabled` <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cluster-settings" data-versioned="true">cluster setting</a>. When enabled, this cluster setting computes a "reduced" <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/eventlog#role_based_audit_event" data-versioned="true">audit configuration</a> based on the user's current role memberships and the current value for the `sql.log.user_audit` cluster setting. The "reduced" audit configuration is computed at the **first SQL event emit by the user, after the setting is enabled**. When the cluster setting is enabled, CockroachDB can compute the audit configuration once at session start, which provides around a 5% increase in throughput. However, changes to the audit configuration (user role memberships or cluster setting configuration) are not reflected within a session. A new session should be started to reflect the configuration changes in auditing behavior. [#104372](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/104372)

### SQL language changes

- When the `sql.trace.stmt.enable_threshold` or `sql.trace.txn.enable_threshold` <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cluster-settings" data-versioned="true">cluster settings</a> is enabled, the logging output is now emitted on the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/logging#sql_exec" data-versioned="true">`SQL_EXEC` channel</a>. Previously, this was emitted to the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/logging#dev" data-versioned="true">`DEV` channel</a>. [#104047](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/104047)
- <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/show-grants" data-versioned="true">
    `SHOW GRANTS`
  </a>
  now lists privileges inherited by role membership. `SHOW GRANTS ON ROLE` statements no longer require any privileges
  and also lists implicit grantees. [#104587](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/104587)

### Operational changes

- The new <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/metrics" data-versioned="true">metric</a> `leases.liveness` shows the number of <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/configure-replication-zones#create-a-replication-zone-for-a-system-range" data-versioned="true">liveness range</a> leases per node to track the liveness range leaseholder. [#104076](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/104076)
- The new a gauge metric `sql.conns_waiting_to_hash` counts the number of connection attempts that are being limited due to the number of concurrent password hashing operations. This behavior has been present since v21.2 to <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/query-behavior-troubleshooting#high-client-cpu-load-connection-pool-exhaustion-or-increased-connection-latency-when-scram-password-based-authentication-is-enabled" data-versioned="true">prevent password hashing from increasing CPU load</a>. The metric is expected to be `0`, or close to `0`, in a healthy setup. If the metric is consistently high and connection latencies are high, then an operator should do one or more of the following:
  - Ensure applications using the cluster have properly configured <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/connection-pooling" data-versioned="true">connection pools</a>.
  - Add more vCPU or more nodes to the cluster.
  - Increase the password hashing concurrency using the `COCKROACH_MAX_PW_HASH_COMPUTE_CONCURRENCY` <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cockroach-commands#environment-variables" data-versioned="true">environment variable</a>. [#104388](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/104388)

### DB Console changes

- Added merge queue failure and merge queue processing time metrics to the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/ui-queues-dashboard#queue-processing-failures" data-versioned="true">**Queue Processing Failures**</a> and <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/ui-queues-dashboard#queue-processing-times" data-versioned="true">**Queue Processing Times**</a> graphs respectively. [#104034](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/104034)
- Removed the **Circuit Breaker Tripped Events** graph from the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/ui-replication-dashboard" data-versioned="true">**Replication**</a> dashboard. [#104038](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/104038)
- Added **Completed time** to <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/ui-jobs-page" data-versioned="true">**Jobs**</a> and <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/ui-jobs-page#job-details" data-versioned="true">**Job details**</a> pages, and updated the time format on those pages to include seconds and milliseconds. [#104063](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/104063)
- Added a **Created SQL Connections** chart on the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/ui-sql-dashboard" data-versioned="true">**SQL**</a> dashboard under **Metrics**. [#104072](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/104072)
- Added **Ranges in Catchup Mode** and **Rangefeed Catchup Scans Duration** charts to the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/ui-cdc-dashboard" data-versioned="true">**Changefeeds**</a> dashboard. [#104122](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/104122)
- The sort setting on the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/ui-hot-ranges-page" data-versioned="true">**Hot Ranges**</a> page is now persisted across page reloads and navigation. [#104112](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/104112)
- The <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/ui-databases-page" data-versioned="true">**Databases**</a> page now supports a large number of tables for a single database. If more than 40 tables are present in a database, the sort on the page will be disabled; however, it is still possible to filter by table name. [#103854](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/103854)
- On the **Statement Details** page, renamed the "Idle Latency" metric to "Client Wait Time" and separated it into its own chart. [#103915](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/103915)
- Added more search criteria options on the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/ui-overview#sql-activity" data-versioned="true">**SQL Activity**</a> page:
  - For the **Top** dropdown: `1000`, `5000`, and `10000`.
  - For the **By** dropdown on the **Statements** tab: Last Execution Time, Max Latency, Max Memory, Min Latency, Network, P50 Latency, P90 Latency, Retries, and Rows Processed.
  - For the **By** dropdown on the **Transactions** tab: Max Memory, Network, Retries, and Rows Processed. [#104054](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/104054)
- Added a new link to the **Range Status** page on the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/ui-replication-dashboard" data-versioned="true">**Replication**</a> dashboard that opens the **Enqueue Ranges** page with the node ID already completed. [#104100](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/104100)
- The DB Console will no longer show `DROP INDEX` recommendations for unique indexes. [#104287](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/104287)
- On the **Transactions** tab of the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/ui-overview#sql-activity" data-versioned="true">**SQL Activity**</a> page, the **Status** will be `Idle` if the executing transaction is not currently executing a statement. Previously, the status would be `Executing`. [#103925](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/103925)
- Fixed the job that updates the `statement_activity` and `transaction_activity` tables on the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/ui-overview#sql-activity" data-versioned="true">**SQL Activity**</a> page. The table size is now constrained when there are a lot of unique queries. This fix helps to prevent slowing down the **SQL Activity** page. [#104340](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/104340)

### Bug fixes

- Fixed a panic that could occur while a <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/copy" data-versioned="true">`COPY`</a> statement is logged for telemetry purposes. [#103848](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/103848)
- Fixed a bug where disk space used by deleted and <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/architecture/storage-layer#garbage-collection" data-versioned="true">garbage collected</a> data would not be reclaimed in a timely manner, especially when a store has low-write workload. [#103865](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/103865)
- Fixed a problem that could lead to erroneously refused lease transfers, causing the following error message: `refusing to transfer lease to [...] because target may need a Raft snapshot: replica in StateProbe`. [#103849](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/103849)
- Fixed a bug where <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/copy" data-versioned="true">`COPY`</a> in v23.1.0 and beta versions would incorrectly encode data with multiple <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/column-families" data-versioned="true">column families</a>. The data must be dropped and re-imported to be encoded correctly. [#103393](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/103393)
- Fixed a bug where running a <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cockroach-commands#commands" data-versioned="true">`debug` command</a> that manipulates a store (e.g., `debug compact` ) without first terminating the node using the store, could result in corruption of the node's store if encryption-at-rest was enabled. [#102877](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/102877)
- Fixed a bug where <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/show-default-privileges" data-versioned="true">`SHOW DEFAULT PRIVILEGES`</a> did not work correctly if the database name or schema name being inspected had upper-case or special characters. [#103952](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/103952)
- Fixed a bug that could cause queries with <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/joins" data-versioned="true">joins</a> or <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/subqueries" data-versioned="true">subqueries</a> to omit rows where column values are `NULL` in very rare cases. This bug was present since v20.2. [#103803](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/103803)
- Fixed a bug that could cause goroutines to hang during <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/security-reference/scram-authentication" data-versioned="true">SCRAM authentication</a>. [#104197](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/104197)
- The `sys.cpu.combined.percent-normalized` metric now uses `GOMAXPROCS`, if lower than the number of CPU shares when calculating CPU utilization. [#104191](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/104191)
- The warning message about a missing `--advertise-addr` flag is no longer displayed when the flag is specified on server start. [#104227](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/104227)
- Fixed a rare bug where stale multi-column table <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cost-based-optimizer" data-versioned="true">statistics</a> could cause table statistics forecasts to be inaccurate, leading to un-optimal query plans. [#104229](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/104229)
- Fixed a bug in v23.1.0 where the `node_id` field would be omitted from logs. The `node_id` value has now been restored to the logs. [#103798](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/103798)
- Fixed a bug where the collection of `KV bytes read` and `KV gRPC calls` execution statistics during <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/explain-analyze" data-versioned="true">`EXPLAIN ANALYZE`</a> could be incorrect (it would remain at zero) in some cases. The bug was introduced in the v23.1.0 release. [#104194](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/104194)
- Fixed an incorrect results bug in v22.2.10 and v23.1.2 and above when the `optimizer_use_improved_computed_column_filters_derivation` <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/set-vars" data-versioned="true">session setting</a> is `true`. Predicates on <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/computed-columns" data-versioned="true">computed columns</a> are derived when an ORed predicate on a column in the computed column expression is present. [#104276](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/104276)
- The <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/ui-key-visualizer" data-versioned="true">`keyvisualizer` job</a> no longer panics if an error is encountered while cleaning up stale samples. Instead, if the job encounters an error, the job will try again later. [#104374](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/104374)
- Fixed a bug where it was possible for a SQL row to be split across two ranges. When this occurred, SQL queries could return unexpected errors. The real keys are now inspected rather than just request keys to determine load-based split points. [#103876](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/103876)
- Fixed a bug which could cause a panic when a <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/create-function" data-versioned="true">`CREATE FUNCTION`</a> statement used the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/functions-and-operators" data-versioned="true">`setval()` built-in function</a>. [#104297](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/104297)
- Fixed a rare race condition that could allow large <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/restore" data-versioned="true">restore</a> jobs to fail with an `unable to find store` error. [#100955](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/100955)
- Fixed a bug where CockroachDB would not ignore the messages that it should, if there was an error while in the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/postgresql-compatibility" data-versioned="true">PostgreSQL extended protocol</a>. [#104459](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/104459)
- Fixed a bug in which some <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/use-cloud-storage" data-versioned="true">Google Cloud Platform</a> -related errors would be returned with an uninformative error. [#104065](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/104065)
- Fixed a bug where in rare cases a panic could occur during shutdown in relation to the SQL activity computation. This bug was introduced in v23.1.0. [#104515](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/104515)
- The backfill of `system.job_info` upgrade migration that runs during upgrades from v22.2 now processes rows in batches to avoid cases where it could become stuck due to <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/performance-best-practices-overview#transaction-contention" data-versioned="true">contention</a> and transaction retries. [#104574](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/104574)
- Fixes a bug in which <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/show-backup" data-versioned="true">`SHOW BACKUP`</a> would fail to show a <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/take-and-restore-locality-aware-backups" data-versioned="true">locality-aware backup</a> that contained <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/take-full-and-incremental-backups" data-versioned="true">incremental backups</a>. [#103761](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/103761)

### Performance improvements

- If <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/transactions#limit-the-number-of-rows-written-or-read-in-a-transaction" data-versioned="true">`transaction_rows_read_err`</a> is set to a non-zero value, CockroachDB now ensures that any single scan never reads more than `transaction_rows_read_err` + 1 rows. This prevents transactions that would error due to the `transaction_rows_read_err` setting from causing a large performance overhead due to large scans. [#104364](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/104364)
- Improved the efficiency of the an internal job that during upgrades deleted descriptors of dropped functions. Previously, the job would check every single ID until the max descriptor ID, which was particularly inefficient when this was large. Now, the job only queries the upper bound ID of each batch. [#104590](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/104590)

### Contributors

This release includes 111 merged PRs by 41 authors.
