        <a href="https://binaries.cockroachdb.com/cockroach-v23.1.0-alpha.9.darwin-10.9-amd64.tgz">
          cockroach-v23.1.0-alpha.9.darwin-10.9-amd64.tgz
        </a>
        <br />(
        <a href="https://binaries.cockroachdb.com/cockroach-v23.1.0-alpha.9.darwin-10.9-amd64.tgz.sha256sum">SHA256</a>)

        <a href="https://binaries.cockroachdb.com/cockroach-sql-v23.1.0-alpha.9.darwin-10.9-amd64.tgz">

### Docker image

[Multi-platform images](https://docs.docker.com/build/building/multi-platform) include support for both Intel and ARM. Multi-platform images do not take up additional space on your Docker host.

Within the multi-platform image:

- The ARM image is **Experimental** and not yet qualified for production use and not eligible for support or uptime SLA commitments.
- The Intel image is **Generally Available** for production use.

To download the Docker image:

```shell
docker pull cockroachdb/cockroach-unstable:v23.1.0-alpha.9
```

### Source tag

To view or download the source code for CockroachDB v23.1.0-alpha.9 on Github, visit [v23.1.0-alpha.9 source tag](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/releases/tag/v23.1.0-alpha.9).

### Changelog

View a detailed changelog on GitHub: [v23.1.0-alpha.8...v23.1.0-alpha.9](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/compare/v23.1.0-alpha.8...v23.1.0-alpha.9)

### Backward-incompatible changes

- The output of the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/show-ranges" data-versioned="true">`SHOW RANGES`</a> command for the `crdb_internal.ranges` and `crdb_internal.ranges_no_leases` tables has been updated, and the previous output is deprecated. To enable the new command output, set the `sql.show_ranges_deprecated_behavior.enabled` <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cluster-settings" data-versioned="true">cluster setting</a> to `false`. The new output will become default in v23.2. [#99618](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/99618)

### Enterprise edition changes

- The <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/create-changefeed" data-versioned="true">`CREATE CHANGEFEED`</a> statement now allows you to limit the nodes that can execute a changefeed by including a locality filter in the `WITH` clause. A node can execute the changefeed only if it was started with a matching [`--locality`](https://cockroachlabs.com/docs/v23.1/cockroach-start#locality) flag. Replace `{locality}` with a comma-separated list of key-value pairs. [#99935](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/99935)

### SQL language changes

- The new `prepared_statements_cache_size` <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/set-vars" data-versioned="true">session setting</a> helps to prevent <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/savepoint#savepoints-and-prepared-statements" data-versioned="true">prepared statement</a> leaks by automatically deallocating the least-recently-used prepared statements when the cache reaches a given size. [#99254](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/99254)

### Operational changes

- The new `COCKROACH_DISABLE_NODE_AND_TENANT_METRIC_LABELS` <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cockroach-commands#environment-variables" data-versioned="true">environment variable</a> allows you to suppress metrics from a cluster's <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/monitoring-and-alerting#prometheus-endpoint" data-versioned="true">Prometheus endpoint</a> if they conflict with labels that are applied by external tools that collect metrics from the endpoint. Set the environment variable to a comma-separated list of key-value pairs. [#99820](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/99820)

### DB Console changes

- The <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/ui-databases-page#index-details" data-versioned="true">**Index Details**</a> section of the **Databases** page now displays the list of most-frequently-used index fingerprints to all users, rather than only to `admin` users, because the page now queries a view rather than a system table directly. [#99485](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/99485)
- When you search or filter within the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/ui-statements-page" data-versioned="true">**Statements** page</a> or <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/ui-transactions-page" data-versioned="true">**Transactions** page</a>, if you interactively sort the results using a column that was not part of the original query, a warning displays if you are viewing only a subset of the results, along with a suggestion to update the original query. [#99795](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/99795)

### Miscellaneous

- Several computed columns have been added to the `statement_statistics_persisted` and `transaction_statistics_persisted` views in the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/crdb-internal" data-versioned="true">`crdb_internal`</a> system catalog and indexed in the corresponding system tables:
  - `execution_count`
  - `service_latency`
  - `cpu_sql_nanos`
  - `contention_time`
  - `total_estimated_execution_time`
  - `p99_latency`

    [#99417](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/99417)

### Bug fixes

- Fixed pagination bugs when searching or filtering within the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/ui-databases-page" data-versioned="true">**Databases** page</a> or viewing the details of a database. [#99513](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/99513)
- Fixed a rare bug introduced in v22.2.0 that could cause a node to crash with an `attempting to append refresh spans after the tracked timestamp has moved forward` error when querying virtual tables in the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/crdb-internal" data-versioned="true">`crdb_internal`</a> or <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/pg-catalog" data-versioned="true">`pg_catalog`</a> system catalogs. If you are experiencing this bug, set the `sql.distsql.use_streamer.enabled` <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cluster-settings" data-versioned="true">cluster setting</a> to `false` before upgrading a cluster to v23.1. [#99443](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/99443)
- Fixed a bug that could erroneously cause multiple garbage-collection jobs to be created when executing a <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/drop-schema" data-versioned="true">`DROP SCHEMA... CASCADE`</a> command, one job for each table and one for the cascaded `DROP` itself. [#99706](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/99706)
- Fixed a bug in the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/ui-insights-page#schema-insights-tab" data-versioned="true">**Insights** page</a> that prevented a recommendation to drop an index from being executed if the index's name contained a space. [#100023](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/100023)
- Fixed a rare bug that prevented the garbage-collection job for a <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/truncate" data-versioned="true">`TRUNCATE`</a> command from successfully finishing if the table descriptor had already been garbage-collected. The garbage-collection job now succeeds in this situation. [#100009](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/100009)
- Fixed a rare bug that could cause a query of a virtual table in the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/crdb-internal" data-versioned="true">`crdb_internal`</a> or <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/pg-catalog" data-versioned="true">`pg_catalog`</a> system catalog to hang indefinitely if the query returned an error. [#99969](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/99969)
- Fixed a bug introduced prior to v21.2 that could cause the SQL gateway node to crash if you <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/create-view" data-versioned="true">created a view</a> with a circular or self-referencing dependencies. This situation no longer crashes the node, and a `cyclic view dependency for relation` error is now logged. [#100159](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/100159)
- Several rare bugs have been fixed that could cause corruption in the existing primary index when a rollback occurs concurrent to adding or removing a <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/column-families" data-versioned="true">column family</a>. This could lead to subsequent unavailability of the table. [#100030](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/100030)
- Fixed a bug that could cause a node to crash with an out-of-memory (OOM) exception when viewing details in the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/ui-statements-page" data-versioned="true">**Statements** page</a> or <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/ui-transactions-page" data-versioned="true">**Transactions** page</a>. [#99550](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/99550)

### Contributors

This release includes 75 merged PRs by 41 authors.

### Docker image

[Multi-platform images](https://docs.docker.com/build/building/multi-platform) include support for both Intel and ARM. Multi-platform images do not take up additional space on your Docker host.

Within the multi-platform image:

- The ARM image is **Experimental** and not yet qualified for production use and not eligible for support or uptime SLA commitments.
- The Intel image is **Generally Available** for production use.

To download the Docker image:

```shell
docker pull cockroachdb/cockroach-unstable:v23.1.0-alpha.8
```

### Source tag

To view or download the source code for CockroachDB v23.1.0-alpha.8 on Github, visit [v23.1.0-alpha.8 source tag](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/releases/tag/v23.1.0-alpha.8).

### Changelog

View a detailed changelog on GitHub: [v23.1.0-alpha.7...v23.1.0-alpha.8](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/compare/v23.1.0-alpha.7...v23.1.0-alpha.8)

### Security updates

- Previously, users could gain unauthorized access to <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/ui-statements-page#diagnostics" data-versioned="true">statement diagnostic bundles</a> they did not create if they requested the bundle through an HTTP request to `/_admin/v1/stmtbundle/<id>` and correctly guessed its (non-secret) `ID`. This change ensures that only authorized SQL users can request statement diagnostic bundles. [#99051](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/99051)

### General changes

- Increased the specificity of log messages to help troubleshoot <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/sso-db-console" data-versioned="true">DB Console SSO</a> issues. [#98522](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/98522)

### Enterprise edition changes

- The MuxRangefeed client, which is enabled with the `changefeed.mux_rangefeed.enabled` <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cluster-settings" data-versioned="true">cluster setting</a>, is now more efficient when running against large-scale workloads. [#97957](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/97957)
- The `server.oidc_authentication.claim_json_key` <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cluster-settings" data-versioned="true">cluster setting</a> for DB Console SSO now accepts list-valued token claims. [#98522](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/98522)
- Added the `WITH` key_column option to override the message metadata key for <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/changefeed-examples" data-versioned="true">changefeeds</a>. This changes the key hashed to determine Kafka partitions. It does not affect the output of `key_in_value` or the domain of the per-key ordering guarantee. [#98806](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/98806)
- The <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/ui-cluster-overview-page#node-map" data-versioned="true">Node Map</a> now shows normalized CPU usage. [#98225](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/98225)

### SQL language changes

- Fixed a bug where the check constraint on an `OID` type column results in a panic in the legacy schema changer. [#98800](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/98800)
- Added a new `WITH REDACT` option to the following statements: <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/show-create" data-versioned="true">`SHOW CREATE`</a>, <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/show-create#show-the-create-table-statement-for-a-table" data-versioned="true">`SHOW CREATE TABLE`</a>, and <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/show-create#show-the-create-view-statement-for-a-view" data-versioned="true">`SHOW CREATE VIEW`</a> which replaces constants and literals in the printed `CREATE` statement with the redacted marker, `‹×›`. [#98251](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/98251)
- Added support for the `REDACT` flag to the following variants of <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/explain" data-versioned="true">`EXPLAIN`</a>: `EXPLAIN (OPT)`, `EXPLAIN (OPT, CATALOG)`, `EXPLAIN (OPT, MEMO)`, `EXPLAIN (OPT, TYPES)`, and `EXPLAIN (OPT, VERBOSE)`. These `EXPLAIN` statements will have constants, literal values, parameter values, and any other user data redacted in the output. [#97549](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/97549)
- Disallowed the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/restore" data-versioned="true">`RESTORE`</a> of backups taken on a cluster version older than the minimum binary version the current cluster can interoperate with. This is described in an updated version of the policy outlined in <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/restoring-backups-across-versions" data-versioned="true">"Restoring Backups Across Versions"</a>. [#98597](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/98597)
- Bulk <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/copy" data-versioned="true">`COPY FROM`</a> statements are now processed with a vectorized insert and can be anywhere from 0.5x to 5x faster. Typical hardware and schemas should see a 2x improvement. Vectorized inserts are only used for `COPY` statements and are not yet applied to regular inserts. Both the `vectorize` and `copy_fast_path_enabled` session variables can be used to disable this feature. [#98605](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/98605)
- Added [stemming and stopword-eliminating](https://www.cockroachlabs.com/blog/full-text-indexing-search) text search configurations for English, Danish, Dutch, Finnish, French, German, Hungarian, Italian, Norwegian, Portuguese, Russian, Spanish, Swedish, and Turkish. [#97677](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/97677)
- Added the `system.statement_activity` and `system.transaction_activity` tables. These tables are used to populate the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/ui-statements-page" data-versioned="true">SQL Activity</a> pages, and contain the top N statements and transactions based on different key columns. [#99179](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/99179)
- Added helper text for <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/update" data-versioned="true">`UPDATE`</a> to include `FROM <source>`. [#99301](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/99301)
- Added the `default_text_search_config` variable for compatibility with single-argument variants to the following text search functions: `to_tsvector`, `to_tsquery`, `phraseto_tsquery`, and `plainto_tsquery`, which use the value of `default_text_search_config` instead of expecting one to be included as in the two-argument variants. The default value of this setting is `english`. [#99323](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/99323)
- Added the `ts_rank` function for ranking text search query results. [#99323](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/99323)
- Renamed the `coordinator_locality` option in `BACKUP` to <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/take-locality-restricted-backups" data-versioned="true">`EXECUTION LOCALITY`</a>. This option allows the user to control the nodes involved in the execution of a backup job, including the processing of row data and job coordination. For example, defining an execution locality for a backup job could reduce latency when a cluster is running heavy workloads and has a frequent backup schedule. [#99176](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/99176)

### Operational changes

- Checkpoint directories that can be created in the rare event of range inconsistency are now clearly indicated as `pending` until they are fully populated. This helps operators distinguish valid checkpoints from corrupted ones. [#99119](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/99119)
- <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/monitor-cockroachdb-with-prometheus" data-versioned="true">
    Prometheus
  </a>
  metrics available at the `_status/vars` path now contain a `node_id` label that identifies the node they were scraped
  from. [#99235](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/99235)

### DB Console changes

- The <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/ui-statements-page#statement-fingerprint-page" data-versioned="true">Statement &amp; Transaction Fingerprints</a> pages no longer poll data, to simplify the user experience and reduce any performance impact. [#98331](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/98331)
- Data on the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/ui-statements-page#statement-fingerprints-view" data-versioned="true">Statement Fingerprint Details</a> page no longer updates automatically every 5mins. [#99298](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/99298)
- Updated the Jobs table column name from "Last Modified Time" to "Last Execution Time". [#99021](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/99021)
- On the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/ui-overview#sql-activity" data-versioned="true">SQL Activity Fingerprints</a> pages, users will not see stats that have not yet been flushed to disk. [#98815](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/98815)
- Users can now request `top-k statements by % runtime` on the SQL Activity Fingerprints pages. [#98815](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/98815)
- Added Search Criteria to the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/ui-statements-page" data-versioned="true">Statements</a> and <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/ui-transactions-page" data-versioned="true">Transactions</a> pages, and updated the UX with improvements. [#98815](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/98815)
- Added badges for each selected filter on the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/ui-overview#sql-activity" data-versioned="true">SQL Activity</a> and <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/ui-insights-page" data-versioned="true">Insights</a> pages. [#98988](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/98988)
- The default request sort for the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/ui-statements-page#statement-fingerprints-view" data-versioned="true">Statement Fingerprints Overview</a> page is now `% of All Runtime`. [#99298](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/99298)
- Fixed a bug where the table's `CREATE` statement would not display correctly on the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/ui-databases-page#table-details" data-versioned="true">Table Details</a> page. [#99434](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/99434)
- Added an assertion on the KV side to prevent other existing or future attempts of LeafTxn issuing locking requests. This ensures the KV API is used as agreed upon and can be helpful in debugging latency issues caused by holding locks. [#99412](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/99412)

### Bug fixes

- Fixed a rare panic in `upstream etcd-io/raft` when a message appends race with log compaction. [#98721](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/98721)
- In the DB Console Stats pages, issuing a new request for stats while one is pending is now allowed and will replace the pending request. [#98331](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/98331)
- Fixed a bug in which <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/set-vars" data-versioned="true">`SET avoid_buffering = true`</a> could produce a crash on subsequent operations. [#98290](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/98290)
- Fixed a bug where using <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/functions-and-operators#st_transform" data-versioned="true">`ST_Transform`</a> could result in a memory leak. [#98740](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/98740)
- Fixed internal errors in <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/show-jobs" data-versioned="true">`SHOW JOBS`</a> statements that have a `WITH` clause. [#98389](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/98389)
- Previously, the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/alter-table#add-column" data-versioned="true">`ADD COLUMN... DEFAULT cluster_logical_timestamp()`</a> statement would crash the node and leave the table in a corrupt state. The root cause is a `nil` pointer dereference. The bug is now fixed by returning an unimplemented error and hence disallowing using the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/functions-and-operators#array-functions" data-versioned="true">builtin function</a> as the default value when backfilling. [#98696](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/98696)
- Fixed a bug that could prevent a cached query with a user-defined type reference from being invalidated even after a schema change that should prevent the type from being resolved. [#96045](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/96045)
- Fixed a bug that could prevent a cached query from being invalidated when a <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/user-defined-functions" data-versioned="true">UDF</a> referenced by that query was altered or dropped. [#96045](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/96045)
- Fixed the replacement of in-flight requests for `KeyedCachedDataReducer` s to prevent permanent loading on requests stuck on an `inFlight` status. [#99095](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/99095)
- Improved the reliability of latency data in v23.1 clusters. [#99294](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/99294)

### Performance improvements

- The Raft tick interval has been increased from `200ms` to `500ms` in order to reduce per-replica CPU costs, and can now be adjusted via `COCKROACH_RAFT_TICK_INTERVAL`. Dependant parameters such as the Raft election timeout ( `COCKROACH_RAFT_ELECTION_TIMEOUT_TICKS` ), reproposal timeout ( `COCKROACH_RAFT_REPROPOSAL_TIMEOUT_TICKS` ), and heartbeat interval ( `COCKROACH_RAFT_HEARTBEAT_INTERVAL_TICKS` ) have been adjusted such that their wall-time value remains the same. [#98584](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/98584)
- The Raft scheduler is now sharded to relieve contention during range Raft processing, which can significantly improve performance at high CPU core counts. [#98854](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/98854)

### Build changes

- Running `./dev ui test` (or `bazel test //pkg/ui/workspaces/db-console:jest` ) now uses less memory. [#98880](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/98880)

### Contributors

This release includes 174 merged PRs by 65 authors. We would like to thank the following contributors from the CockroachDB community:

- Eric.Yang

### Docker image

[Multi-platform images](https://docs.docker.com/build/building/multi-platform) include support for both Intel and ARM. Multi-platform images do not take up additional space on your Docker host.

Within the multi-platform image:

- The ARM image is **Experimental** and not yet qualified for production use and not eligible for support or uptime SLA commitments.
- The Intel image is **Generally Available** for production use.

To download the Docker image:

```shell
docker pull cockroachdb/cockroach-unstable:v23.1.0-alpha.7
```

### Source tag

To view or download the source code for CockroachDB v23.1.0-alpha.7 on Github, visit [v23.1.0-alpha.7 source tag](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/releases/tag/v23.1.0-alpha.7).

### Changelog

View a detailed changelog on GitHub: [v23.1.0-alpha.6...v23.1.0-alpha.7](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/compare/v23.1.0-alpha.6...v23.1.0-alpha.7)

### Security updates

- The default value for the `server.user_login.password_hashes.default_cost.scram_sha_256` <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cluster-settings" data-versioned="true">cluster setting</a> is now 10610. (Previously the default was 119680.) The old value was found to have been too high for many types of client hardware, and in some cases could cause regressions in connection latency. The new value was chosen by running tests with clients that have 1 or 2 vCPUs provisioned. Additionally, the new cluster setting `server.user_login.rehash_scram_stored_passwords_on_cost_change.enabled` was added, and defaults to `true`. If it is `true` and the stored SCRAM password for a user has a different cost than the configured default cost, then the next time the user logs in, their password will automatically be rehashed using the configured default cost. If the rehashing is not desired, then operators should update the `server.user_login.password_hashes.default_cost.scram_sha_256` cluster setting to the value they desire before upgrading. This change is being backported to <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/releases/v22.2" data-versioned="true">v22.2</a>. [#98254](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/98254)

### General changes

- CockroachDB now uses the soft memory limit of Go runtime by default. This feature of Go has been available since v22.2 by setting the `GOMEMLIMIT` environment variable. Now it is enabled by default, which should reduce the likelihood of the CockroachDB process <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cluster-setup-troubleshooting#out-of-memory-oom-crash" data-versioned="true">OOMing</a>. This soft memory limit can be disabled by specifying `--max-go-memory=0` to <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cockroach-start" data-versioned="true">`cockroach start`</a>. [#97666](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/97666)
- Previously, the output of <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/show-jobs#show-changefeed-jobs" data-versioned="true">`SHOW CHANGEFEED JOBS`</a> was limited to show unfinished jobs and finished jobs from the last 14 days. This change makes the command show all changefeed jobs, regardless of if they finished and when they finished. Note that jobs still obey the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cluster-settings#setting-jobs-retention-time" data-versioned="true">cluster setting</a> `jobs.retention_time`. Completed jobs older than that time are deleted. Fixes: https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/issues/97883 [#98175](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/98175)

### Enterprise edition changes

- Sinkless <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/create-changefeed" data-versioned="true">changefeeds</a> that use the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/selection-queries" data-versioned="true">`AS SELECT`</a> syntax now require an enterprise license. [#98241](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/98241)
- <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/create-external-connection" data-versioned="true">
    External connections
  </a>
  can now be used as the URI value for a Confluent schema registry. For example, `CREATE EXTERNAL CONNECTION reg AS
  "https://example.cloud?opt=val"; CREATE CHANGEFEED FOR foo WITH
  format='avro',confluent_schema_registry='external://reg'`
  [#97140](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/97140)
- <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/create-schedule-for-backup" data-versioned="true">
    Backup schedules
  </a>
  created or altered to have the option `on_previous_running` will have the full backup schedule created with the user
  specified option, but will override the incremental backup schedule to always default to `on_previous_running = wait`.
  This ensures correctness of the backup chains created by the incremental schedule by preventing duplicate incremental
  jobs from racing against each other. [#98249](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/98249)
- <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/changefeed-sinks#kafka" data-versioned="true">
    Changefeeds
  </a>
  to a Kafka sink now support the `OAUTHBEARER` `sasl_mechanism`.
  [#98053](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/98053)
- <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/changefeed-examples" data-versioned="true">
    Changefeeds
  </a>
  running with the `changefeed.mux_rangefeed.enabled`
  <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cluster-settings" data-versioned="true">
    cluster setting
  </a>
  set to `true` are more efficient, particularly when executing against large tables.
  [#96756](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/96756)

### SQL language changes

- A regions field was added to the `statistics` column of <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/crdb-internal#statement_statistics" data-versioned="true">`crdb_internal.statement_statistics`</a>, reporting the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/show-regions" data-versioned="true">regions</a> of the nodes on which the statement was executed. [#95449](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/95449)
- The `enforce_home_region` <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/set-vars#enforce-home-region" data-versioned="true">session setting</a> was extended with a new optional preview feature and session setting, which is disabled by default, to dynamically detect and report the home region for <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/selection-queries" data-versioned="true">`SELECT`</a> queries based on the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/show-locality" data-versioned="true">locality</a> of the queried rows, if different from the region of the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/ui-sessions-page#session-details-gateway-node" data-versioned="true">gateway node</a>. [cockroachdb/cockroach#97827](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/97827)
- Added a URL to errors related to the `enforce_home_region` <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/set-vars#enforce-home-region" data-versioned="true">session setting</a> that users can view to see additional information about the error. [#97827](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/97827)
- Added a new <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/set-vars" data-versioned="true">session setting</a> `enforce_home_region_follower_reads_enabled` as a preview feature to allow errors triggered by the `enforce_home_region` <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/set-vars#enforce-home-region" data-versioned="true">session setting</a> to perform reads using <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/follower-reads" data-versioned="true">`AS OF SYSTEM TIME follower_read_timestamp()`</a> in order to find and report a query's <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/multiregion-overview#table-localities" data-versioned="true">home region</a>. [#97827](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/97827)
- Added a new aggregate <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/functions-and-operators#array-functions" data-versioned="true">builtin function</a> `array_cat_agg`. It behaves similarly to `array_agg(unnest(array_column))`: it takes arrays as its input, unnests them into the array elements which are then aggregated into a single result array. It's similar to concatenating all input arrays into a single array. [#97826](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/97826)
- Added a new <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/set-vars" data-versioned="true">session setting</a> `optimizer_always_use_histograms`, which ensures that the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cost-based-optimizer" data-versioned="true">optimizer</a> always uses histograms when available to calculate the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cost-based-optimizer#table-statistics" data-versioned="true">statistics</a> of every plan that it explores. Enabling this setting can prevent the optimizer from choosing a suboptimal <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/indexes" data-versioned="true">index</a> when statistics for a table are stale. [#98194](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/98194)
- Added the `MODIFYSQLCLUSTERSETTING` <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/security-reference/authorization#supported-privileges" data-versioned="true">system privilege</a>. This privilege allows users the ability to view all <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cluster-settings" data-versioned="true">cluster settings</a>, but only modify those settings with the `sql.defaults.*` prefix. This re-introduces the modify functionality seen with `MODIFYCLUSTERSETTING` CockroachDB <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/releases/v22.2" data-versioned="true">v22.2</a>. [#97521](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/97521)
- Added a `status` column to the following <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/crdb-internal" data-versioned="true">`crdb_internal`</a> virtual tables: `crdb_internal.cluster_txn_execution_insights` and `crdb_internal.node_txn_execution_insights`. [cockroachdb/cockroach#98217](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/98217)
- Added a new session variable `allow_role_memberships_to_change_during_transaction` which can be used to make the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/grant" data-versioned="true">granting</a> and <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/revoke" data-versioned="true">revoking</a> of <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/security-reference/authorization#roles" data-versioned="true">role memberships</a> faster at the cost of some <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/architecture/transaction-layer#isolation-levels" data-versioned="true">isolation</a> claims. By default, when granting or revoking a role from another role, CockroachDB waits for all <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/transactions" data-versioned="true">transactions</a> that are consulting the current set of role memberships to complete. This means that by the time the transaction which performed the grant or revoke operation returns successfully, the user has a proof that no ongoing transaction is relying on the state that existed prior to the change. The downside of this waiting is that it means that `GRANT` and `REVOKE` will take longer than the longest currently executing transaction. In some cases, users do not care about whether concurrent transactions will immediately see the side-effects of the operation, and would instead prefer that the grant or revoke finish rapidly. In order to aid in those cases, the session variable `allow_role_memberships_to_change_during_transaction` has been added. Now, the grant or revoke will only need to wait for the completion of statements in <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/show-sessions" data-versioned="true">sessions</a> which do not have this option set. One can set the option as enabled by default in all sessions in order to accelerate and grant and revoke role operations. [#98370](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/98370)
- Fixed a bug where CockroachDB panicked when a user tried to <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/truncate" data-versioned="true">truncate a table</a> which had an ongoing <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/row-level-ttl" data-versioned="true">Row-level TTL</a> change. CockroachDB still does not support truncating a table in this scenario, but instead of panicking an "unimplemented" error is returned. [#98537](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/98537)

### Operational changes

- <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/architecture/overview#architecture-leaseholder" data-versioned="true">
    Range leases
  </a>
  will no longer be transferred to
  <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cockroach-start#store" data-versioned="true">
    stores
  </a>
  which are IO overloaded. [#97587](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/97587)
- The environment variable `COCKROACH_IGNORE_CLUSTER_SETTINGS` can be used to <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cockroach-start" data-versioned="true">start a node</a> so that it ignores all stored <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cluster-settings" data-versioned="true">cluster setting</a> values in an emergency. [#97805](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/97805)
- Introduce two <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cluster-settings" data-versioned="true">cluster settings</a> to control disk utilization thresholds for <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/architecture/replication-layer" data-versioned="true">replica allocation</a>: `kv.allocator.rebalance_to_max_disk_utilization_threshold`, which controls the maximum disk utilization before a store will never be used as a rebalance target, and `kv.allocator.max_disk_utilization_threshold`, which controls maximum disk utilization before a store will never be used as a rebalance or allocation target _and_ will actively have <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/architecture/overview#architecture-replica" data-versioned="true">replicas</a> moved off of it. [#97409](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/97409)
- The <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cluster-settings" data-versioned="true">cluster setting</a> `kv.trace.slow_request_stacks.threshold` can be used to attach available stack history from <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/show-trace" data-versioned="true">tracer snapshots</a> to traces of <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/logging#sql_perf" data-versioned="true">slow requests</a>. [#97895](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/97895)
- Added a new <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/metrics" data-versioned="true">metric</a> `changefeed.schema_registry.retry_count`. This measures the number of request retries performed when sending requests to the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/changefeed-examples" data-versioned="true">changefeed schema registry</a>. Observing a nonzero value may indicate improper configuration of the schema registry or changefeed parameters. [#98338](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/98338)
- The `kv.range_split.load_cpu_threshold` <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cluster-settings#setting-kv-range-split-load-cpu-threshold" data-versioned="true">cluster setting</a> now has a minimum setting value of `10ms`. [#98250](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/98250)
- The `kv.allocator.lease_io_overload_threshold_enforcement` <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cluster-settings" data-versioned="true">cluster setting</a> value which disables enforcement is updated to be spelled correctly as "ignore" rather than "ingore". [cockroachdb/cockroach#98543](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/98543)
- The <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/architecture/overview#architecture-leaseholder" data-versioned="true">range lease</a> duration can now be adjusted via the environment variable `COCKROACH_RANGE_LEASE_DURATION`. Users are advised to exercise caution when adjusting this, and consider the relationship with e.g. <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/architecture/replication-layer#raft" data-versioned="true">Raft</a> election timeouts and network timeouts. [#98616](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/98616)

### Command-line changes

- <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cockroach-sql" data-versioned="true">
    `cockroach sql`
  </a>
  and
  <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cockroach-demo" data-versioned="true">
    `cockroach demo`
  </a>
  now support the client-side command `\s` to display the previous command history.
  [#98035](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/98035)
- Added a new flag `--max-go-memory` to the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cockroach-start" data-versioned="true">`cockroach start`</a> command. It controls the soft memory limit on the Go runtime which adjusts the behavior of the Go garbage collector to try keeping the memory usage under the soft memory limit (the limit is "soft" in a sense that it is not enforced if live objects (RSS) exceed it). Similar to the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cockroach-start" data-versioned="true">`--max-sql-memory` flag</a>, the new flag `--max-go-memory` accepts numbers interpreted as bytes, size suffixes (e.g. `1GB` and `1GiB`) or a percentage of physical memory (e.g. `.25`). If left unspecified, the flag defaults to 2.25x of `--max-sql-memory` (subject to `--max-go-memory + 1.15 x --cache` not exceeding 90% of available RAM). Set to `0` to disable the soft memory limit (not recommended). If the `GOMEMLIMIT` env var is set and `--max-go-memory` is not, then the value from the env var is used; if both are set, then the flag takes precedence. [#97666](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/97666)
  - Here are a few examples of how the default value is calculated on a machine with 16GiB of RAM. In the first two lines we use the default formula `2.25x --max-sql-memory`. In the third line, the default formula results in exceeding the upper bound on total usage (including the cache), so we use the upper bound determined as `0.9 * total RAM - 1.15 * cache size`. In the fourth line, the default formula results in 225MiB which is smaller than the lower bound of 256MiB, so we bump the value to that lower bound. In the fifth line, we use the value specified by the user (even though it is smaller than the lower bound on the default value).

    <table>
      <thead>
        <tr>
          <th>Command line flags</th>
          <th>Computed max SQL memory</th>
          <th>Computed cache size</th>
          <th>Computed max Go memory</th>
        </tr>
      </thead>
      <tbody>
        <tr>
          <td>--max-sql-memory=.25 --cache=.25</td>
          <td>4GiB</td>
          <td>4GiB</td>
          <td>9GiB</td>
        </tr>
        <tr>
          <td>--max-sql-memory=.1 --cache=.5</td>
          <td>1.6GiB</td>
          <td>8GiB</td>
          <td>3.6GiB</td>
        </tr>
        <tr>
          <td>--max-sql-memory=.25 --cache=.4</td>
          <td>4GiB</td>
          <td>6.4GiB</td>
          <td>7.04GiB</td>
        </tr>
        <tr>
          <td>--max-sql-memory=100MiB</td>
          <td>100MiB</td>
          <td>128MiB</td>
          <td>256MiB</td>
        </tr>
        <tr>
          <td>--max-sql-memory=.4 --cache=.2 --max-go-memory=100MiB</td>
          <td>6.4GiB</td>
          <td>3.2GiB</td>
          <td>100MiB</td>
        </tr>
      </tbody>
    </table>

- The `--drain-wait` argument to the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cockroach-node" data-versioned="true">`cockroach node drain`</a> command will be automatically increased if the command detects that it is smaller than the sum of the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/node-shutdown#cluster-settings" data-versioned="true">cluster settings</a> `server.shutdown.drain_wait`, `server.shutdown.connection_wait`, `server.shutdown.query_wait` times two, and `server.shutdown.lease_transfer_wait`. If the `--drain-wait` argument is 0, then no timeout is used. This recommendation <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/node-shutdown#drain-timeout" data-versioned="true">was already documented</a>, but now the advice will be applied automatically. [#98390](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/98390)

### DB Console changes

- Fixed the error `Cannot read properties of undefined (reading 'length')` which could cause <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/ui-overview" data-versioned="true">DB Console</a> pages to fail to load. [#98222](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/98222)
- Added a new metric to the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/ui-hardware-dashboard" data-versioned="true">Hardware dashboard</a> showing the system-wide CPU usage in addition to the existing CockroachDB CPU usage. [#98187](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/98187)
- Users will see an upgrade error message when a response from the SQL-over-HTTP API (from `/api/v2/sql/` ) says that a relation or column does not exist. [cockroachdb/cockroach#98312](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/98312)
- The description of the average QPS graph in the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/ui-replication-dashboard" data-versioned="true">Replication Metrics Dashboard</a> no longer claims the average is exponentially weighted. [#98270](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/98270)
- The metric `rebalancing.cpunanospersecond` is now included in the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/ui-replication-dashboard" data-versioned="true">Replication Metrics Dashboard</a>. [#98270](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/98270)
- Added an error code column to the insights table for a failed execution to the statement and transaction detail views on the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/ui-insights-page" data-versioned="true">Insights Page</a>. Added a status column to the statement and transaction workload insights tables on the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/ui-insights-page" data-versioned="true">Insights Page</a>. [cockroachdb/cockroach#97138](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/97138)

### Bug fixes

- RPC connections between nodes now require RPC connections to be established in both directions, otherwise the connection will be closed. This is done to prevent asymmetric network partitions where nodes are able to send outbound messages but not receive inbound messages, which could result in persistent unavailability. This behavior can be disabled by the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cluster-settings" data-versioned="true">cluster setting</a> `rpc.dialback.enabled`. [#94778](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/94778)
- The owner of the public schema can now be changed using <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/alter-schema" data-versioned="true">`ALTER SCHEMA public OWNER TO new_owner`</a>. [#98000](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/98000)
- Fixed a bug in which <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/common-table-expressions" data-versioned="true">common table expressions</a> (CTEs) marked as `WITH RECURSIVE` which were not actually recursive could return incorrect results. This could happen if the CTE used a `UNION ALL`, because the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cost-based-optimizer" data-versioned="true">optimizer</a> incorrectly converted the `UNION ALL` to a `UNION`. This bug had existed since support for recursive CTEs was first added in v20.1. [#98042](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/98042)
- Internal queries that are executed in order to serve a client-initiated query already appeared in <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cost-based-optimizer#table-statistics" data-versioned="true">statistics</a> with an `application_name` prefixed by the string `$$`. But this name was not used in the output of <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/show-statements" data-versioned="true">`SHOW QUERIES`</a>. Now, `SHOW QUERIES` also shows the `$$` prefix for these types of queries.
- Fixed a bug in evaluation of `ANY`, `SOME`, and `ALL` <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/functions-and-operators#operators" data-versioned="true">sub-operators</a> that would cause expressions like `NULL = ANY(ARRAY[]::INT[])` to return `NULL` instead of `False`. [cockroachdb/cockroach#97948](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/97948)
- Fixed a bug that could crash the process when a query contained a literal <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/scalar-expressions#tuple-constructors" data-versioned="true">tuple expression</a> with more than two elements and only a single label, e.g., `((1, 2, 3) AS foo)`. [#98142](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/98142)
- Fixed a bug where certain special character combinations in the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/connection-parameters#supported-options-parameters" data-versioned="true">`options` field in connection URLs</a> were not properly supported by CockroachDB. [#98302](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/98302)
- Fixed a bug where the stats columns on the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/ui-transactions-page#transaction-fingerprints-view" data-versioned="true">Transaction Fingerprints overview page</a> was continuously incrementing. The fix was to ensure we don't re-use the stats object between re-renders by creating a new copy of the stats for every aggregation. [cockroachdb/cockroach#98307](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/98307)
- Fixed a bug where <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/transactions" data-versioned="true">transactions</a> that performed a <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/select-for-update" data-versioned="true">`SELECT FOR UPDATE`</a> across multiple <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/architecture/overview#architecture-range" data-versioned="true">ranges</a> but never performed writes could fail to eagerly clean up their <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/architecture/transaction-layer#writing" data-versioned="true">locks</a> after commit. Future transactions that encountered these abandoned locks could be delayed for 50ms before unlocking them. [#98044](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/98044)
- Fixed a bug which could result in some <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/create-index" data-versioned="true">`CREATE INDEX`</a> statements to fail with the error `failed to verify keys for Scan`. [#98262](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/98262)
- Fixed a bug where CockroachDB could encounter an internal error `concurrent txn use detected`. The bug was introduced in <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/releases/v22.2" data-versioned="true">v22.2.0</a>. [#98120](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/98120)
- Fixed a bug where if an <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/update" data-versioned="true">`UPDATE`</a> was performed during an on-going <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/alter-table#add-column" data-versioned="true">`ADD COLUMN`</a> or <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/alter-table#drop-column" data-versioned="true">`DROP COLUMN`</a> on a table, the update could incorrectly fail due to a duplicate key error. [#98354](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/98354)
- Fixed a bug where it was possible for CockroachDB to temporarily not respect <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/configure-replication-zones" data-versioned="true">zone configurations</a> other than <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/configure-replication-zones#view-the-default-replication-zone" data-versioned="true">the default zone config</a>. This could only happen for a short window of a few seconds after nodes with existing <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/architecture/overview#architecture-replica" data-versioned="true">replicas</a> were <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cockroach-start" data-versioned="true">restarted</a>, and self-rectified (also within seconds). [#98422](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/98422)
  - This manifested in a few ways:
  - If <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/configure-replication-zones#num_replicas" data-versioned="true">`num_replicas`</a> was set to something other than 3, we would still add or remove replicas to get to 3x replication.
  - If <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/configure-replication-zones#num_voters" data-versioned="true">`num_voters`</a> was set explicitly to get a mix of voting and <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/architecture/replication-layer#non-voting-replicas" data-versioned="true">non-voting replicas</a>, it would be ignored. CockroachDB could possibly even remove non-voting replicas.
  - If <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/configure-replication-zones#range-min-bytes" data-versioned="true">`range_min_bytes`</a> or <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/configure-replication-zones#range-max-bytes" data-versioned="true">`range_max_bytes`</a> were changed from their default values of 128 MiB and 512 MiB respectively, we would instead try to size ranges to be within [128 MiB, 512MiB]. This could appear as an excess amount of <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/architecture/distribution-layer#range-splits" data-versioned="true">range splits</a> or <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/architecture/distribution-layer#range-merges" data-versioned="true">merges</a>, as visible in the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/ui-replication-dashboard" data-versioned="true">Replication Dashboard</a> under "Range Operations".
  - If <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/configure-replication-zones#gc-ttlseconds" data-versioned="true">`gc.ttlseconds`</a> was set to something other than the default 90000 seconds (25h), we would still only GC data older than 90000s. If the GC TTL was set to something larger than 25h, <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/as-of-system-time" data-versioned="true">`AS OF SYSTEM TIME`</a> queries going further back could start failing. For GC TTLs less than the default, clusters would observe increased disk usage due to more retained <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/performance-recipes#too-many-mvcc-values" data-versioned="true">MVCC garbage</a>.
  - If <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/configure-replication-zones#constraints" data-versioned="true">`constraints`</a>, <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/configure-replication-zones#lease_preferences" data-versioned="true">`lease_preferences`</a> or <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/configure-replication-zones#voter_constraints" data-versioned="true">`voter_constraints`</a> were set, they would be ignored. Range data and <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/architecture/glossary#architecture-leaseholder" data-versioned="true">leases</a> would possibly be moved outside where prescribed.
- Allow users with the `VIEWACTIVITY` / `VIEWACTIVITYREDACTED` <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/security-reference/authorization#role-options" data-versioned="true">permissions</a> to access the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/crdb-internal" data-versioned="true">`crdb_internal.ranges_no_leases`</a> table, necessary to view important DB Console pages (specifically, the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/ui-databases-page" data-versioned="true">Databases Page</a>, including database details, and database tables). [#98535](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/98535)
- Fixed a bug that caused incorrect results when comparisons of <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/scalar-expressions#tuple-constructors" data-versioned="true">tuples</a> were done using the `ANY` <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/functions-and-operators#operators" data-versioned="true">operator</a>. For example, an expression like `(x, y) = ANY (SELECT a, b FROM t WHERE...)` could return `true` instead of the correct result of `NULL` when `x` and `y` were `NULL`, or `a` and `b` were `NULL`. This could only occur if the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/subqueries#correlated-subqueries" data-versioned="true">subquery was correlated</a>, i.e., it references columns from the outer part of the query. This bug was present since the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cost-based-optimizer" data-versioned="true">cost-based optimizer</a> was introduced in <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/releases/v2.1" data-versioned="true">v2.1</a>. [#98700](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/98700)

### Miscellaneous

- Added two views to the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/crdb-internal" data-versioned="true">`crdb_internal`</a> catalog: `crdb_internal.statement_statistics_persisted`, which surfaces data in the persisted `system.statement_statistics` table, and `crdb_internal.transaction_statistics_persisted`, which surfaces the `system.transaction_statistics` table. [cockroachdb/cockroach#98261](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/98261)

### Contributors

This release includes 245 merged PRs by 65 authors.

### Docker image

[Multi-platform images](https://docs.docker.com/build/building/multi-platform) include support for both Intel and ARM. Multi-platform images do not take up additional space on your Docker host.

Within the multi-platform image:

- The ARM image is **Experimental** and not yet qualified for production use and not eligible for support or uptime SLA commitments.
- The Intel image is **Generally Available** for production use.

To download the Docker image:

```shell
docker pull cockroachdb/cockroach-unstable:v23.1.0-alpha.6
```

### Source tag

To view or download the source code for CockroachDB v23.1.0-alpha.6 on Github, visit [v23.1.0-alpha.6 source tag](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/releases/tag/v23.1.0-alpha.6).

### Changelog

View a detailed changelog on GitHub: [v23.1.0-alpha.5...v23.1.0-alpha.6](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/compare/v23.1.0-alpha.5...v23.1.0-alpha.6)

### SQL language changes

- Previously, an `ALTER TABLE.. ADD UNIQUE.. NOT VALID` statement would be processed by ignoring the `NOT VALID` qualifier. This is not in keeping with PostgreSQL, which would throw an error instead. Now, CockroachDB throws the same error as PostgreSQL for such a statement: "UNIQUE constraints cannot be marked NOT VALID". [#97758](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/97758)
- Introduced a new internal virtual table `crdb_internal.node_memory_monitors`, which exposes all of the current reservations with the memory accounting system on a single node. Access to the table requires the `VIEWACTIVITY` <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/security-reference/authorization#supported-privileges" data-versioned="true">system privilege</a> (or the legacy `VIEWACTIVITY` <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/security-reference/authorization#role-options" data-versioned="true">role option</a> ), or the `VIEWACTIVITYREDACTED` <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/security-reference/authorization#supported-privileges" data-versioned="true">system privilege</a> (or the legacy `VIEWACTIVITYREDACTED` <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/security-reference/authorization#role-options" data-versioned="true">role option</a> ) defined. [#97657](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/97657)
- Each type cast is now expressible as a function, e.g., `now()::date` can be expressed as `date(now())`. [#97093](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/97093)
- Added support for a new syntax to provide options to the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/copy" data-versioned="true">`COPY`</a> statement. The options can now be given in a comma-separated list enclosed by parentheses. The old syntax is still supported. [#97863](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/97863)
- Added support for the syntax `CREATE DATABASE IF NOT EXISTS... WITH OWNER`. [#97951](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/97951)
- Added a new internal <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/functions-and-operators#trigrams-functions" data-versioned="true">built-in function</a>, `crdb_internal.redactable_sql_constants`, which can be used to redact SQL statements passed in as strings. [#97834](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/97834)
- Added an `error_code` column to the `crdb_internal.cluster_execution_insights` and `crdb_internal.node_execution_insights` virtual tables, which contains the error code for a failed execution. Also added a `last_error_code` column to the `crdb_internal.cluster_txn_execution_insights` and `crdb_internal.node_txn_execution_insights` virtual tables, which contains the error code of the last failed statement in that transaction. [#97046](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/97046)
- Added a new internal <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/functions-and-operators#trigrams-functions" data-versioned="true">built-in function</a>, `crdb_internal.redact`, which replaces substrings surrounded by redaction markers with the redacted marker. [#98008](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/98008)

### Command-line changes

- The <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cockroach-node" data-versioned="true">`cockroach node decommission`</a> operation now validates the ability of the node to complete a decommission before attempting it, given the cluster configuration and the ranges with replicas present on the node. When errors are detected that would result in the inability to complete node decommission, they will be printed to stderr and the command will exit, instead of marking the node as `decommissioning` and beginning the node decommission process. Strict readiness evaluation mode can be used by setting `--checks=strict`. In this case, any ranges that need preliminary actions prior to replacement for the decommission process (e.g., ranges that are not yet fully up-replicated) will block the decommission process. Validation can be skipped by using the flag `--checks=skip`. [#96100](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/96100)

### DB Console changes

- Updated the description for <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/ui-insights-page" data-versioned="true">Suboptimal Insight</a> and added a **Learn more** link to it. [#97719](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/97719)

### Bug fixes

- The unquoted value `none` is now allowed as the value in a <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/set-vars" data-versioned="true">`SET`</a> statement. [#97816](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/97816)
- `IMPORT INTO... DELIMITED DATA` will now correctly handle quoted fields that contain unescaped newlines. [#97545](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/97545)
- Previously, casting an `inet` to a string type omitted the mask if a mask was not provided. This was not in keeping with PostgreSQL and is now resolved. [#97093](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/97093)
- Fixed link encoding on links to database/table/index pages. [#97893](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/97893)
- Fixed the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/show-create" data-versioned="true">`SHOW CREATE ALL {TYPES|SCHEMAS|TABLES}`</a> commands so they handle database names that have mixed-case, hyphens, or quotes. [#97915](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/97915)
- Tables referenced in index recommendations are now fully qualified, ensuring that they are not ambiguous. [#97262](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/97262)
- Changed the database used for <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/sql-statements" data-versioned="true">SQL API</a> calls, to no longer use `defaultdb`, which was causing error messages on some pages when that database no longer exists. [#97990](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/97990)

### Build changes

- Changes to source files in `pkg/ui/workspaces/db-console` now properly bust the build cache, and are consistently included in local builds. [#97956](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/97956)

### Contributors

This release includes 69 merged PRs by 39 authors.

### Docker image

[Multi-platform images](https://docs.docker.com/build/building/multi-platform) include support for both Intel and ARM. Multi-platform images do not take up additional space on your Docker host.

Within the multi-platform image:

- The ARM image is **Experimental** and not yet qualified for production use and not eligible for support or uptime SLA commitments.
- The Intel image is **Generally Available** for production use.

To download the Docker image:

```shell
docker pull cockroachdb/cockroach-unstable:v23.1.0-alpha.5
```

### Source tag

To view or download the source code for CockroachDB v23.1.0-alpha.5 on Github, visit [v23.1.0-alpha.5 source tag](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/releases/tag/v23.1.0-alpha.5).

### Changelog

View a detailed changelog on GitHub: [v23.1.0-alpha.4...v23.1.0-alpha.5](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/compare/v23.1.0-alpha.4...v23.1.0-alpha.5)

### Security updates

- The new <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cluster-settings" data-versioned="true">cluster setting</a> `server.user_login.downgrade_scram_stored_passwords_to_bcrypt.enabled`, which allows you to migrate passwords from SCRAM to bcrypt during user authentication, defaults to `true`. If it is `true` and if `server.user_login.password_encryption` is `crdb-bcrypt`, then during login, the stored hashed password will be migrated from SCRAM to bcrypt. [#97429](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/97429)

### General changes

- Users with the `CONTROLJOB` <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/create-role#role-options" data-versioned="true">role option</a> can now <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/show-jobs" data-versioned="true">view jobs</a> owned by admins. [#96382](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/96382)
- Users with the `VIEWJOB` <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/create-role#role-options" data-versioned="true">role option</a> can now <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/show-jobs" data-versioned="true">view all jobs</a>. This role can be revoked by granting the `NOVIEWJOB` role option. [#96382](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/96382)

### Enterprise edition changes

- Jobs that utilize a protected timestamp system (such as `BACKUP`, `CHANGEFEED`, or `IMPORT` ) now produce metrics that can be monitored to detect cases when a job leaves a stale protected timestamp that will prevent garbage collection from occurring. [#97148](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/97148)
- <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/create-changefeed" data-versioned="true">
    Changefeeds
  </a>
  now automatically expire protected timestamp records for paused jobs if the changefeed is configured with the
  `gc_protect_expires_after` option. [#97148](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/97148)
- User-defined functions (UDFs) can now be referenced from column <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/default-value" data-versioned="true">`DEFAULT`</a> expressions when creating a new table or issuing the `SET DEFAULT` command. Backup and restore operations also back up and restore UDF IDs that are referenced in a column's DEFAULT expression. If UDF dependencies are missing and the `skip_missing_udfs` flag is provided, the `DEFAULT` expressions are dropped during a restore operation. [#97501](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/97501)

### SQL language changes

- String literals are now allowed for region names in DDL syntax, in addition to quoted syntax. [#97021](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/97021)
- It is now possible to use `*` inside a <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/create-view" data-versioned="true">`CREATE VIEW`</a> statement. The list of columns is expanded at the time the view is created, so that new columns added after the view was defined are not included in the view. This behavior is the same as in PostgreSQL. [#97515](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/97515)
- The default value of `sql.stats.cleanup.rows_to_delete_per_txn` has been increased to `10000` to increase efficiency of the cleanup job for SQL statistics. [#97642](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/97642)
- The new <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/set-vars" data-versioned="true">session setting</a> `optimizer_use_improved_split_disjunction_for_joins` allows the optimizer to split disjunctions ( `OR` expressions) in more `JOIN` conditions by building a `UNION` of two `JOIN` expressions. If this setting is true, all disjunctions in inner, semi, and anti `JOIN` s will be split. Otherwise, only disjunctions that potentially contain an equijoin condition will be split. [#97696](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/97696)
- Builtins have been added for `tsvector`, `to_tsquery`, `phraseto_tsquery`, and `plainto_tsquery`, which parse input documents into tsvectors and tsqueries, respectively. The new `ts_parse` builtin is used to debug the text search parser. [#92966](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/92966)
- The new <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/set-vars" data-versioned="true">session variable</a> `inject_retry_errors_on_commit_enabled` returns a <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/transaction-retry-error-reference" data-versioned="true">transaction retry error</a> if it is run inside of an explicit transaction when it is set to `true`. The transaction retry error continues to be returned until `inject_retry_errors_on_commit_enabled` is set to `false`. This setting allows you to test your transaction retry logic. [#97226](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/97226)
- Previously, <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/primary-key" data-versioned="true">`ADD PRIMARY KEY NOT VALID`</a> ignored the `NOT VALID` qualifier. This behavior was not compatible with PostgreSQL. CockroachDB now throws the error `PRIMARY KEY constraints cannot be marked NOT VALID`. [#97746](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/97746)

### Operational changes

- The following <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cluster-settings" data-versioned="true">cluster settings</a>, which control rebalancing and upreplication behavior in the face of IO-overloaded storage, have been deprecated:
  - `kv.allocator.l0_sublevels_threshold`
  - `kv.allocator.l0_sublevels_threshold_enforce` These cluster settings have been replaced by internal mechanisms. [#97142](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/97142)
- Max timeout-to-intent resolution has been added to prevent intent resolution from becoming stuck indefinitely and blocking other ranges attempting to resolve intents. [#91815](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/91815)
- Nodes are now considered suspect when rejoining a cluster and cannot accept lease transfers for one `server.time_after_store_suspect` window, which defaults to 30 seconds. [#97532](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/97532)

### Command-line changes

- The SQL shell ( <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cockroach-sql" data-versioned="true">`cockroach sql`</a>, <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cockroach-demo" data-versioned="true">`cockroach demo`</a> ) now supports the client-side commands `\l`, `\dn`, `\d`, `\di`, `\dm`, `\ds`, `\dt`, `\dv`, `\dC`, `\dT`, `\dd`, `\dg`, `\du` and `\dd` in a similar manner to PostgreSQL, including the modifier flags `S` and `+`, for convenience for users migrating from PostgreSQL. A notable difference is that when a pattern argument is specified, it should use the SQL `LIKE` syntax (with `%` representing the wildcard character) instead of PostgreSQL's glob-like syntax (with `*` representing wildcards). [#88061](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/88061)

### DB Console changes

- The following new metrics track memory usage of prepared statements in sessions:
  - `sql.mem.internal.session.prepared.current`
  - `sql.mem.internal.session.prepared.max-avg`
  - `sql.mem.internal.session.prepared.max-count`
  - `sql.mem.internal.session.prepared.max-max`
  - `sql.mem.internal.session.prepared.max-p50`
  - `sql.mem.internal.session.prepared.max-p75`
  - `sql.mem.internal.session.prepared.max-p90`
  - `sql.mem.internal.session.prepared.max-p99`
  - `sql.mem.internal.session.prepared.max-p99.9`
  - `sql.mem.internal.session.prepared.max-p99.99`
  - `sql.mem.internal.session.prepared.max-p99.999`
  - `sql.mem.sql.session.prepared.current`
  - `sql.mem.sql.session.prepared.max-avg`
  - `sql.mem.sql.session.prepared.max-count`
  - `sql.mem.sql.session.prepared.max-max`
  - `sql.mem.sql.session.prepared.max-p50`
  - `sql.mem.sql.session.prepared.max-p75`
  - `sql.mem.sql.session.prepared.max-p90`
  - `sql.mem.sql.session.prepared.max-p99`
  - `sql.mem.sql.session.prepared.max-p99.9`
  - `sql.mem.sql.session.prepared.max-p99.99`
  - `sql.mem.sql.session.prepared.max-p99.999`

    [#97590](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/97590)

- Active execution information is now shown on the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/ui-statements-page" data-versioned="true">Statements page</a> even when there is a max size limit error. [#97662](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/97662)
- "Retrying" is no longer a status shown in the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/ui-jobs-page" data-versioned="true">Jobs</a> page. [#97505](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/97505)

### Bug fixes

- Transaction uncertainty intervals are now correctly configured for reverse scans, to prevent reverse scans from serving stale reads when clocks in a cluster are skewed. [#97443](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/97443)
- The formatting of uniqueness violation errors now matches the corresponding errors from PostgreSQL. [#96914](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/96914)
- Previously, when a new column name would require quoting due to mixed-case or special characters, <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/alter-table#add-column" data-versioned="true">`ALTER TABLE... ADD COLUMN`</a> would not run in an explicit or multi-statement transaction. This is now fixed. [#97514](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/97514)
- Fixed a bug when formatting <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/create-type" data-versioned="true">`CREATE TYPE` statements for user-defined types</a> which require quoting which might prevent those statements from round-tripping. [#97514](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/97514)
- Using subqueries in user-defined functions without an `AS` clause is now supported, for consistency with the syntax supported outside of user-defined functions. [#97515](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/97515)
- Fixed a rare bug introduced before v22.1.x that could cause a projected expression to replace column references with the wrong values. [#97554](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/97554)
- Cross-descriptor validation on lease renewal is now disabled, because it can starve <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/online-schema-changes" data-versioned="true">online schema changes</a> when there are many descriptors with many foreign key references. [#97630](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/97630)
- Fixed a bug with pagination on the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/ui-insights-page" data-versioned="true">Insights</a> page. [#97640](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/97640)
- Columns referenced in partial index predicates and partial unique constraint predicates can no longer be dropped. The <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/alter-table#drop-column" data-versioned="true">`ALTER TABLE.. DROP COLUMN`</a> statement now returns an error with a suggestion to drop the indexes and constraints first. This is a temporary safeguard to prevent users from hitting [#96924](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/issue/97808). This restriction will be lifted when that bug is fixed. [#97372](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/97372)
- The <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/ui-jobs-page" data-versioned="true">Jobs</a> page now displays an error state when an error is encountered during data fetching. [#97486](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/97486)
- Fixed a bug introduced in v22.1 that caused the internal error `no bytes in account to release...`. [#97750](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/97750)
- The <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/copy" data-versioned="true">`COPY FROM`</a> command now respects the `statement_timeout` and `transaction_timeout` <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cluster-settings" data-versioned="true">cluster settings</a>. [#97808](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/97808)
- <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/copy" data-versioned="true">
    `COPY FROM`
  </a>
  commands now appear in the output of the
  <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/show-statements" data-versioned="true">
    `SHOW STATEMENTS`
  </a>
  command. [#97808](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/97808)
- Fixed an error where querying a `pg_catalog` table included information about a temporary table created in another session. [#97727](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/97727)

### Performance improvements

- If the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/set-vars" data-versioned="true">session setting</a> `optimizer_use_improved_split_disjunction_for_joins` is `true`, the optimizer now creates a better query plan in some cases where an inner, semi, or anti join contains a join predicate with a disjuction ( `OR` condition). [#97696](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/97696)

### Miscellaneous

- UDFs can now return the `RECORD` result type, which represents any tuple. For example, `CREATE FUNCTION f() RETURNS RECORD AS 'SELECT * FROM t' LANGUAGE SQL;` is equivalent to `CREATE FUNCTION f() RETURNS t AS 'SELECT * FROM t' LANGUAGE SQL;`. [#97199](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/97199)
- The parameters for <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/architecture/replication-layer#snapshots" data-versioned="true">delegated snapshots</a> have been marked as internal. [#97408](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/97408)
- Fixed an error when calling <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/create-function" data-versioned="true">`CREATE OR REPLACE FUNCTION`</a> with a <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/create-type" data-versioned="true">user-defined return type</a> if the user-defined type was modified after the original <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/create-function" data-versioned="true">user-defined function</a> was created. The command now succeeds as long as the function body returns output that matches the modified user-defined type. [#97274](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/97274)
- Columns with referenced constraints can now be dropped. [#97579](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/97579)
- Index cascades with a dependent inbound foreign key can now be dropped. [#97065](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/97065)

### Contributors

This release includes 120 merged PRs by 51 authors. We would like to thank the following contributors from the CockroachDB community:

- Eric.Yang (first-time contributor)
