### Docker image

[Multi-platform images](https://docs.docker.com/build/building/multi-platform) include support for both Intel and ARM. Multi-platform images do not take up additional space on your Docker host.

Within the multi-platform image:

- The ARM image is **Experimental** and not yet qualified for production use and not eligible for support or uptime SLA commitments.
- The Intel image is **Generally Available** for production use.

To download the Docker image:

```shell
docker pull cockroachdb/cockroach-unstable:v23.1.0-alpha.4
```

### Source tag

To view or download the source code for CockroachDB v23.1.0-alpha.4 on Github, visit [v23.1.0-alpha.4 source tag](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/releases/tag/v23.1.0-alpha.4).

### Changelog

View a detailed changelog on GitHub: [v23.1.0-alpha.3...v23.1.0-alpha.4](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/compare/v23.1.0-alpha.3...v23.1.0-alpha.4)

### Enterprise edition changes

- Some of the transformations specific to changefeeds have been deprecated and replaced. These functions were released in limited access in v22.2. Deprecated changefeed transformations continue to function. Closely monitor changefeeds that are created during upgrade. While effort was made to maintain backward compatibility, the updated changefeed transformation may produce slightly different output, such as different column names. [#96295](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/96295)
- Add support for implicit authentication to Azure Storage and KMS. [#96825](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/96825)
- Add support for `CREATE EXTERNAL CONNECTION... AS "postgresql://"` or `"postgres://"`. These external connections may be specified as the source in streaming replication. [#96551](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/96551)
- Add support for referencing <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/user-defined-functions" data-versioned="true">user defined functions (UDFs)</a> from other objects. Backup and restore operations can now read and write UDF descriptors. [#97038](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/97038)

### SQL language changes

- UDFs can now return a set of results by setting the return type to `SETOF`. [#96698](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/96698)
- UDFs with implicit record return types will return an error when called if the return type has been altered and is no longer compatible with the body of the UDF. [#96696](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/96696)
- The `COPY... TO STDOUT` statement allows you to export a table or arbitrary query in the PostgreSQL wire-compatible format. Text and CSV formats are supported. [#94408](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/94408)
- Add the read-only "ssl" session variable. Value is "off" if the server was started in insecure mode (which disables TLS), or "on" otherwise. This is based on the Postgres variable of the same name. [#97257](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/97257)
- Add a hard limit of how much data can be flushed to system tables for sql stats. [#97123](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/97123)
- Add support for the `REDACT` flag to the following variants of `EXPLAIN`:
  - `EXPLAIN`
  - `EXPLAIN (PLAN)`
  - `EXPLAIN (VEC)`
  - `EXPLAIN ANALYZE`
  - `EXPLAIN ANALYZE (PLAN)`

    These explain statements (along with `EXPLAIN ANALYZE (DEBUG)`, which already supported `REDACT`) will have constants, literal values, parameter values, and any other user data redacted in output. [#95136](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/95136)

- Previously UDFs are not allowed in tables and any other object. This patch enables UDF usage in CHECK constraints of tables in both legacy schema changer and delcarative schema changer. Circular ependencies are not allowed, namely if a UDF depends on a table, then the table can't use that UDF. [#97038](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/97038)
- A version gate has been added to prevent UDF usage in CHECK constraints before a cluster is fully upgraded to v23.1 or above. [#97038](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/97038)
- Previously users were able to use UDFs from tables with `SET DEFAULT` and `SET ON UPDATE` even when they are disallowed from `CREATE TABLE` and `ADD COLUMN`. This patch disallows those two cases from `ALTER TABLE ALTER COLUMN`. [#97390](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/97390)

  ### Operational changes

- Add `COCKROACH_RAFT_LOG_QUEUE_CONCURRENCY` env var which controls the number of parallel workers doing Raft log truncations. It can be used to make the in-memory log truncations more agressive and reduce the amount of Raft log data flushed to disk. [#97029](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/97029)
- The new timeseries metric `storage.keys.tombstone.count` shows the current count of point and range deletion tombstones across the storage engine. [#97306](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/97306)
- The value of `kv.range_split.load_cpu_threshold` controls the CPU per-second threshold above which a range will be split. Its default value has been increased from `250ms` to `500ms`, based on performance experiments. [#97113](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/97113)
- CPU balancing is enabled as the default load based rebalancing objective. This can be reverted by setting `kv.allocator.load_based_rebalancing.objective` to `qps`. [#97424](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/97424)

### DB Console changes

- Add columns p50, p90, p99, max and min latency for Statement table on SQL Activity page. [#97082](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/97082)
- Show a warning for Statement Insights when the SQL API returns a "max size exceed" error. [#97153](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/97153)
- Show a warning for Transaction Insights when the SQL API returns a "max size exceed" error. [#97277](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/97277)
- Show a warning for Schema Insights when the SQL API returns a "max size exceed" error. [#97312](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/97312)

### Bug fixes

- Fixed a bug where the `AS OF SYSTEM TIME` clause was handled incorrectly in an implicit transaction that had multiple statements. [#97063](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/97063)
- This patch fixes asymmetric typing of `>` and `<` expressions which may cause erroring of expressions which are legal. [#97022](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/97022)
- This patch fixes possible internal errors in `SOME`, `ANY` and `ALL` expressions of the form: `expr > SOME(expr1, expr2, expr3...)` [#97022](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/97022)
- Fixed the syntax error for `SELECT... QUERY` (without `AS` ) statement. [#97041](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/97041)
- Decommissions that would violate constraints set on a subset of replicas for a range (e.g. `num_replicas = 3, <constraint>: 1` ) will no longer be able to execute, respecting constraints during and after the decommission. [#94810](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/94810)
- Adjusted the size reported for `TIME`, `TIMETZ`, `TIMESTAMP`, `TIMESTAMPTZ`, and `DATE` types in the pgwire protocol. [#97145](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/97145)
- The ParameterStatus message is now only sent over the pgwire protocol if the value of the parameter changed. (The parameters that are sent this way are timezone, intervalstyle, datestyle, is_superuser, and application_name.) [#97145](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/97145)
- Users can now go to the next page of results when there are more than 20 active statements or transactions in the Active Execution page. [#97122](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/97122)
- Since 22.1 when rangefeed enablement overrides in span configs were introduced, rangefeed requests that reached spans outside the range would not cause range cache invalidation due to the setting being checked first, thus requests could repeatedly hit the same incorrect range, causing errors until cache invalidation or node restart. This fix correctly checks that the span is within the range prior to checking the enablement settings, thus invalidating the cache when a request reaches an incorrect range and causing subsequent requests to successfully reach the correct range. [#97212](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/97212)
- A bug has been fixed that caused errors when creating multiple user-defined functions with the same name and different argument types in the same type family. For example, it was impossible to create both functions `f(i INT2)` and `f(INT4)`. [#96481](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/96481)
- The following spammy log message was removed: &gt; lease [...] expired before being followed by lease [...]; foreground traffic may have been impacted [#97358](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/97358)
- Previously, `ALTER TABLE... INJECT STATISTICS` command would fail if a column with COLLATED STRING type had histograms to be injected, and this is now fixed. The bug has been present since at least 21.2. [#96695](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/96695)
- Fixed a bug in the query engine that could cause incorrect results in some cases when a zigzag join was planned. The bug could occur when the two indexes used for the zigzag join had a suffix of matching columns but with different directions. For example, planning a zigzag join with `INDEX(a ASC, b ASC)` and `INDEX(c ASC, b DESC)` could cause incorrect results. This bug has existed since at least v19.1. It is now fixed, because the optimizer will no longer plan a zigzag join in such cases. [#97151](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/97151)

### Performance improvements

- The optimizer now plans inverted index scans for queries that filter by JSON fetch value operators `(->)` that contain both a string and an integer index value after the IN operator. For example the optimizer plans inverted index scans for the following filters: `json_col->0 IN ('1', '2')`, `json_col->'a' IN ('1', '2')`. [#96471](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/96471)

### Build changes

- Starting with CockroachDB v23.1.0-alpha.4, a FIPS compliant tarball and Docker image are produced for the Linux x86_64 platform. The tarball uses OpenSSL libraries for crypto operations by dynamically loading the corresponding FIPS-validated dynamic libraries. The Docker image comes with the FIPS-validated OpenSSL library pre-installed. [#96107](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/96107)

### Miscellaneous

- [#97229](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/97229)
- Fix a bug in which `RESTORE`, `BACKUP`, and `IMPORT` jobs would fail if the coordinator node of the job was drained. [#97033](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/97033)

### Contributors

This release includes 124 merged PRs by 48 authors. We would like to thank the following contributors from the CockroachDB community:

- DQ (first-time contributor)

### Docker image

[Multi-platform images](https://docs.docker.com/build/building/multi-platform) include support for both Intel and ARM. Multi-platform images do not take up additional space on your Docker host.

Within the multi-platform image:

- The ARM image is **Experimental** and not yet qualified for production use and not eligible for support or uptime SLA commitments.
- The Intel image is **Generally Available** for production use.

To download the Docker image:

```shell
docker pull cockroachdb/cockroach-unstable:v23.1.0-alpha.3
```

### Source tag

To view or download the source code for CockroachDB v23.1.0-alpha.3 on Github, visit [v23.1.0-alpha.3 source tag](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/releases/tag/v23.1.0-alpha.3).

### Changelog

View a detailed changelog on GitHub: [v23.1.0-alpha.2...v23.1.0-alpha.3](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/compare/v23.1.0-alpha.2...v23.1.0-alpha.3)

### General changes

- Added new metrics to count <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/pause-job" data-versioned="true">paused jobs</a> for every job type. For example, the metric for paused changefeed jobs is `jobs.changefeed.currently_paused`. These metrics are updated at an interval defined by the cluster setting `jobs.metrics.interval.poll`, which defaults to 10 seconds. [#89752](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/89752)

### Enterprise edition changes

- Added support for Azure Key Vault KMS, which will allow users to <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/take-and-restore-encrypted-backups#use-key-management-service" data-versioned="true">encrypt and decrypt their backups</a> using keys stored in Azure Key Vault. App Registration authentication (Azure RBAC) for Azure Storage is also now supported. [#96459](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/96459)
- Introduced a new locality filter option ( `coordinator_locality` ) that can be specified when a <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/backup" data-versioned="true">backup job</a> is created. This option restricts the backup metadata writing to the designated nodes. [#95791](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/95791)
- Fixed a bug that caused the server to crash if trying to restore a table from a backup generated by `BACKUP TABLE` from a schema that includes <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/user-defined-functions" data-versioned="true">user-defined functions</a>, and the restore target database does not have a schema with the same name. [#96911](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/96911)
- Changefeeds with the `unordered` option can use multi-region <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/changefeed-sinks" data-versioned="true">Google Cloud Pub/Sub topics</a>. [#96567](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/96567)
- Fixed a bug in changefeeds where long running <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/create-changefeed#initial-scan" data-versioned="true">initial scans</a> will fail to generate checkpoints. Failure to generate <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/how-does-an-enterprise-changefeed-work" data-versioned="true">checkpoints</a> is particularly bad if the changefeed restarts. Without checkpoints, the changefeed will restart from the beginning, and in the worst case, when exporting substantially sized tables, the changefeed initial scan may not complete. [#96995](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/96995)

### SQL language changes

- Added <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cockroachcloud/statements-page#statement-statistics" data-versioned="true">latency information</a> in seconds to the statement statistics on `crdb_internal.statement_statistics`, `system.statement_statistics`, and `crdb_internal.cluster_statement_statistics`, with information about: `min`, `max`, `p50`, `p90`, and `p99. Also added the columns:` latency_seconds_min `,` latency_seconds_max `,` latency_seconds_p50 `,` latency_seconds_p90 `, and` latency_seconds_p99 `to` crdb_internal.node_statement_statistics&#96;. [#96396](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/96396)
- Deprecated the `PGDUMP` and `MYSQLDUMP` formats for <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/import" data-versioned="true">`IMPORT`</a>. They are still present, but will be removed in a future release. See the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/molt/migration-overview" data-versioned="true">Migration Overview</a> page for alternatives. [#96386](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/96386)
- <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/copy" data-versioned="true">
    `COPY... FROM... QUOTE '"'`
  </a>
  will no longer error. [#96572](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/96572)
- Added `last_error_code` column to the `crdb_internal.node_statement_statistics` table. Added `last_error_code` field to the `statistics` JSON blob in the `crdb_internal.statement_statistics` and `system.statement_statistics` tables. [#96436](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/96436)
- Added support for expressions of the form `COLLATE "default"`, `COLLATE "C"`, and `COLLATE "POSIX"`. Since the default <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/collate" data-versioned="true">collation</a> cannot be changed currently, these expressions are all equivalent. The expressions are evaluated by treating the input as a normal string, and ignoring the collation. This means that comparisons between strings and collated strings that use `"default"`, `"C"`, or `"POSIX"` are now supported. Creating a column with the `"C"` or `"POSIX"` collations is still not supported. [#96828](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/96828)
- The insights subsystem in `sqlstats` is now able to detect failed executions, regardless if they were slow or not. [#97039](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/97039)
- The internal `statement_statistics` and `transaction_statistics` tables now include sampled execution statistics on storage iteration. [#96016](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/96016)
- Introduced the `declare_cursor_statement_timeout_enabled` <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/set-vars" data-versioned="true">session variable</a> that disables statement timeouts during `FETCH` when using `DECLARE CURSOR`. [#96607](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/96607)

### Operational changes

- A <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/backup" data-versioned="true">`BACKUP`</a> that encounters too many retryable errors will now fail instead of pausing to allow subsequent backups the chance to succeed. [#96673](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/96673)
- Added an option to balance CPU time ( `cpu` ) instead of queries per second ( `qps` ) among stores in a cluster. This is done by setting `kv.allocator.load_based_rebalancing.objective='cpu'`. `kv.allocator.cpu_rebalance_threshold` is also added, similar to `kv.allocator.qps_rebalance_threshold` to control the target range for store CPU above and below the cluster mean. [#96127](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/96127)
- The <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/load-based-splitting" data-versioned="true">load-based splitter</a> now supports using request CPU usage to split ranges. This is introduced with the previous cluster setting `kv.allocator.load_based_rebalancing.objective`, which when set to `cpu`, will use request CPU usage. The threshold above which CPU usage of a range is considered for splitting is defined in the cluster setting `kv.range_split.load_cpu_threshold`, which has a default value of `250ms`. [#96128](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/96128)
- Added the flag `--disable-max-offset-check` to disable node self-termination when it detects <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/operational-faqs#what-happens-when-node-clocks-are-not-properly-synchronized" data-versioned="true">clock skew</a> with the rest of the cluster beyond `--max-offset`. The operator assumes responsibility for ensuring that real clock skew never exceeds `--max-offset`. [#96141](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/96141)

### DB Console changes

- Added execution insights to the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cockroachcloud/statements-page#sql-statement-fingerprints" data-versioned="true">Statement Fingerprint Details</a> and <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/ui-transactions-page#transaction-fingerprints-view" data-versioned="true">Transaction Fingerprint Details</a> pages. [#96440](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/96440)
- Transaction insights that were not found will now display a message `Insight not found`. [#96832](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/96832)
- Added a waiting statement ID and fingerprint to the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/ui-insights-page#transaction-executions-view" data-versioned="true">Insights Transaction</a> details page. Added a blocking transaction ID and fingerprint to the the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/ui-insights-page#statement-executions-view" data-versioned="true">Insights Statement</a> page. [#96872](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/96872)

### Bug fixes

- Fixed a bug where casting a <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/time" data-versioned="true">`TIMETZ`</a> to an <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/array" data-versioned="true">`ARRAY`</a> results in displaying second offsets, even if they are zero. [#96583](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/96583)
- Allowed <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/alter-table" data-versioned="true">`ALTER TABLE.. ADD/DROP CONSTRAINT.. NOT VALID`</a> and <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/alter-table#validate-constraints" data-versioned="true">`VALIDATE CONSTRAINT..`</a> to behave consistently with PostgreSQL. Previously, the `VALIDATE CONSTRAINT` would fail and cause the whole statement to fail. [#96648](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/96648)
- Resolved the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/timestamp" data-versioned="true">`TIMESTAMPTZ`</a> to match PostgreSQL. We previously included the minute/second offset for `TIMESTAMPTZ` in certain places when casting it to <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/string" data-versioned="true">`STRING`</a>, even when they were zero. [#96833](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/96833)
- Resolved using negative years instead of BC when casting a <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/timestamp" data-versioned="true">`TIMESTAMPTZ`</a> to a <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/string" data-versioned="true">`STRING`</a>. [#96833](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/96833)
- Fixed the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/show-grants" data-versioned="true">`SHOW GRANTS FOR public`</a> command so it works correctly. Previously, this would return an error saying that the `public` role does not exist. [#96957](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/96957)
- Statement source (square bracket) syntax is no longer allowed in <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/user-defined-functions" data-versioned="true">user-defined functions</a>. Prior to this fix, using this syntax in a UDF would cause a panic. This restriction will be lifted in the future. [#96824](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/96824)

### Performance improvements

- The execution of multiple <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/foreign-key" data-versioned="true">`FOREIGN KEY`</a> and <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/unique" data-versioned="true">`UNIQUE`</a> constraint checks have been parallelized in some cases. As a result, these checks should be completed faster, particularly in multi-region environments where the checks require cross-region reads. [#96123](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/96123)

### Contributors

This release includes 137 merged PRs by 56 authors. We would like to thank the following contributors from the CockroachDB community:

- Ivan Gorbachev (first-time contributor)
