        <a href="https://binaries.cockroachdb.com/cockroach-v23.1.0-alpha.1.windows-6.2-amd64.zip">
          cockroach-v23.1.0-alpha.1.windows-6.2-amd64.zip
        </a>
        <br />(
        <a href="https://binaries.cockroachdb.com/cockroach-v23.1.0-alpha.1.windows-6.2-amd64.zip.sha256sum">SHA256</a>)
      </td>
      <td>
        <a href="https://binaries.cockroachdb.com/cockroach-sql-v23.1.0-alpha.1.windows-6.2-amd64.zip">
          cockroach-sql-v23.1.0-alpha.1.windows-6.2-amd64.zip
        </a>
        <br />(
        <a href="https://binaries.cockroachdb.com/cockroach-sql-v23.1.0-alpha.1.windows-6.2-amd64.zip.sha256sum">
          SHA256
        </a>
        )
      </td>
    </tr>
  </tbody>
</table>

### Docker image

[Multi-platform images](https://docs.docker.com/build/building/multi-platform) include support for both Intel and ARM. Multi-platform images do not take up additional space on your Docker host.

Within the multi-platform image:

- The ARM image is **Experimental** and not yet qualified for production use and not eligible for support or uptime SLA commitments.
- The Intel image is **Generally Available** for production use.

To download the Docker image:

```shell
docker pull cockroachdb/cockroach-unstable:v23.1.0-alpha.1
```

### Source tag

To view or download the source code for CockroachDB v23.1.0-alpha.1 on Github, visit [v23.1.0-alpha.1 source tag](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/releases/tag/v23.1.0-alpha.1).

### Backward-incompatible changes

- Replaced the `cdc_prev()` <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/functions-and-operators" data-versioned="true">function</a> in favor of a `cdc_prev` tuple. This is an incompatible change that may break <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/change-data-capture-overview" data-versioned="true">changefeeds</a> that use the previous `cdc_prev()` function. [#85177](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/85177)
- <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/show-ranges" data-versioned="true">
    `SHOW RANGES FOR TABLE`
  </a>
  now includes rows for all indexes that support the table. Prior to this change, `SHOW RANGES FOR TABLE foo` was an
  alias for `SHOW RANGES FOR INDEX foo@primary`. This was causing confusion, as it would miss data for secondary
  indexes. It is still possible to filter to just the primary index using `SHOW RANGES FOR INDEX foo@primary`. The
  statement output now also includes the index name. [#93545](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/93545)

### Security updates

- It is now possible to create <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/security-reference/transport-layer-security" data-versioned="true">TLS client certificates</a> for identity principals that are not a valid SQL username using <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cockroach-cert" data-versioned="true">`cockroach cert create-client`</a> and the new flag `--disable-username-validation`. This is meant to be used in combination with the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cluster-settings" data-versioned="true">cluster setting</a> `server.identity_map.configuration` and the `map` option in HBA rules ( `server.host_based_authentication.configuration` ). To test this feature, use `cockroach sql`. Cockroach Labs recommends passing the username separately from the connection URL. [#90439](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/90439)
- There is a new SQL <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/set-vars" data-versioned="true">session variable</a> `system_identity` defined to contain the identity principal presented by the SQL clients during the initial connection. This may be different from `session_user` when the identity was mapped, either using GSSAPI and `include_realm=0`, or when using an identity map. [#90439](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/90439)

### General changes

- Upgraded gRPC to v1.49.0 [#88562](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/88562)
- The connection timeout for cluster-internal connections between nodes has been reduced to 5s to potentially reduce the impact of network issues. Previously, CockroachDB employed a 20s connection timeout. [#88625](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/88625)
- CockroachDB no longer shares a TCP connection for the KV and Gossip subsystems. Each subsystem now uses their own connection, so the total number of outgoing and incoming TCP connections at each node in the cluster will increase by 30 to 50 percent. [#88625](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/88625)
- Bulk operations now log the (sanitized) destinations they are connecting to. For example: `backup planning to connect to destination gs://test/backupadhoc?AUTH=specified&CREDENTIALS=redacted`. [#89531](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/89531)

### Enterprise edition changes

- <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/show-jobs#show-changefeed-jobs" data-versioned="true">
    `SHOW CHANGEFEED JOBS`
  </a>
  no longer reveals Confluent schema registry user information, including a user's secret key. This information is now
  redacted, meaning it will not be stored in CockroachDB internal tables at all.
  [#86603](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/86603)
- <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/change-data-capture-overview" data-versioned="true">
    Changefeeds
  </a>
  JSON encoder performance is improved by 50%. [#88064](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/88064)
- Changefeeds, using cloud storage sink, now have better throughput. [#88395](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/88395)
- Added the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cluster-settings" data-versioned="true">cluster setting</a> `changefeed.event_consumer_workers` which allows changefeeds to process events concurrently. [#87994](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/87994)
- Changefeed) exports are up to 25% faster due to uniform work assignment. [#88672](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/88672)
- Changefeeds can emit files compressed with the ZSTD algorithm, which provides good compression and is much faster than GZIP. In addition, a new, faster implementation of GZIP is used by default. [#88635](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/88635)
- When a changefeed is run with the option `virtual_columns = "null"`, the virtual column will be ordered last in each row. [#89329](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/89329)
- For Kafka <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/changefeed-sinks" data-versioned="true">sinks</a>, you can now add the optional JSON field `"Compression"` to the `kafka_sink_config` option. This field can be set to `"none"` (default), `"GZIP"`, `"SNAPPY"`, `"LZ4"`, or `"ZSTD"`. Setting this field will result in the specified compression protocol to be used when emitting events. [#90270](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/90270)
- Fixed a bug that could cause changefeeds to fail during a rolling restart. [#89913](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/89913)
- Changefeeds will now treat all errors, unless otherwise indicated, as retryable errors. [#90810](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/90810)
- CockroachDB now supports passing in the optional external ID when <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cloud-storage-authentication" data-versioned="true">assuming a role</a>. This is done by extending the values of the comma-separated string value of the `ASSUME_ROLE` parameter to the format `<role>;external_id=<id>`. Users can still use the previous format of just `<role>` to specify a role without any external ID. When using role chaining, each role in the chain can be associated with a different external ID. [#91040](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/91040)
- <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/sso-sql" data-versioned="true">
    JWT authentication
  </a>
  <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cluster-settings" data-versioned="true">
    cluster settings
  </a>
  can now be modified from within tenants to better support serverless use cases.
  [#92406](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/92406)
- <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cdc-queries" data-versioned="true">
    CDC queries
  </a>
  are now planned and evaluated using the SQL optimizer and distSQL execution. The state of the previous row is now
  exposed as the `cdc_prev` tuple. [#85177](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/85177)
- Changefeeds no longer require the `COCKROACH_EXPERIMENTAL_ENABLE_PER_CHANGEFEED_METRICS` environment variable to be set in order to use the `metrics_label` option. [#93423](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/93423)
- Changefeeds can now be scheduled at intervals specified in crontab notation. [#92232](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/92232)

### SQL language changes

- Added the `crdb_internal.to_json_as_changefeed_with_flags` <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/functions-and-operators" data-versioned="true">function</a> to help debug JSON <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/change-data-capture-overview" data-versioned="true">changefeeds</a>. [#84509](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/84509)
- Added the `regions` column to the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/show-backup" data-versioned="true">`SHOW BACKUP`</a> command which will output a string of `ALTER DATABASE` commands if the database is a multi-region database and `NULL` for everything else. Previously, the user did not have an easy way to see if a backed up database is multi-region. [#88136](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/88136)
- Types with length modifiers can now be used to prefix literals. [#82028](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/82028)
- A new column `plan_gist` was added to `crdb_internal.{node,cluster}_queries` representing the compressed logical plan. [#88770](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/88770)
- You can generate easy-to-read <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/create-index" data-versioned="true">`CREATE INDEX`</a> statements for a table's (secondary) indexes using the `SHOW CREATE INDEXES FROM <table_name>` and `SHOW CREATE SECONDARY INDEXES FROM <table_name>` statements. [#88861](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/88861)
- `enum_first`, `enum_last`, and `enum_range` may now take `NULL` arguments as long as their type can be inferred from the expression. [#89124](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/89124)
- <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/online-schema-changes" data-versioned="true">
    Declarative schema changer
  </a>
  support for `ALTER PRIMARY KEY` statements now extends to tables which have secondary indexes.
  [#86176](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/86176)
- The `backup.restore_span.target_size` cluster setting now defaults to `384 MiB`. This should reduce the number of ranges created during <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/restore" data-versioned="true">restore</a> and thereby reduce the merging of ranges that needs to occur after the restore. [#89333](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/89333)
- The `transaction_timeout` <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/set-vars" data-versioned="true">session variable</a> was added. `transaction_timeout` aborts an explicit transaction when it runs longer than the configured duration. When the timer times out, the current statement is cancelled and the transaction enters an aborted state. This timeout does not have any effect when no statement is being executed, so it should be used with `idle_in_transaction_timeout` for the best results. [#89033](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/89033)
- The `crdb_internal.check_consistency` <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/functions-and-operators" data-versioned="true">function</a> now does not include the diff between inconsistent replicas, should they occur. If an inconsistency occurs, the storage engine checkpoints should be inspected. This change is made because the maximum range size limit has been increased from 64 MiB to 512 MiB, so inlining diffs in consistency checks does not scale. [#89502](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/89502)
- CockroachDB now shows a hash-sharded check constraint in <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/show-create" data-versioned="true">`SHOW CREATE TABLE`</a> if it is set to `NOT VALID`. [#89517](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/89517)
- Added the `SHOW FUNCTIONS` and `SHOW FUNCTIONS FROM <schema>` statements, which list <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/user-defined-functions" data-versioned="true">user-defined functions</a>. [#89557](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/89557)
- The default value of `sql.metrics.statement_details.plan_collection.enabled` is now `false`. [#89847](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/89847)
- CockroachDB now supports executing statements of the form `DELETE FROM... USING`. [#88974](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/88974)
- The <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cluster-settings" data-versioned="true">cluster setting</a> `sql.ttl.default_range_concurrency` and table storage parameter `ttl_range_concurrency` are no longer configurable. [#89392](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/89392)
- CockroachDB drops the associated scheduled incremental backup when <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/drop-schedules" data-versioned="true">`DROP SCHEDULE`</a> or `DROP SCHEDULES` is called. Previously, whenever a user dropped a <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/create-schedule-for-backup" data-versioned="true">scheduled full backup</a>, the corresponding scheduled incremental backup would not be dropped. [#89768](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/89768)
- Added the `sql.auth.change_own_password.enabled` <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cluster-settings" data-versioned="true">cluster setting</a>. It defaults to `false`. When set to `true`, any user is allowed to change their own password to a non-null value. Changing other role options still has the same privilege requirements as before (either `CREATEROLE` or `CREATELOGIN`, depending on the option). [#90485](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/90485)
- The `sql.distsql.max_running_flows` <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cluster-settings" data-versioned="true">cluster setting</a> has been removed. [#84888](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/84888)
- The query field in the `crdb_internal.node_queries`, `crdb_internal.cluster_queries`, and `SHOW QUERIES` commands now includes the original comments in the queries. [#86968](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/86968)
- Added a new `descriptor_validation` <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/set-vars" data-versioned="true">session variable</a> which can be set to `read_only` or `off` to disable descriptor validation, which may be useful when mitigating or recovering from catalog corruption. [#90488](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/90488)
- CockroachDB now supports using <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/alter-table#drop-constraint" data-versioned="true">`DROP CONSTRAINT, ADD CONSTRAINT`</a> to add a new primary key without moving the existing primary key to a secondary index if the primary key name is a reserved SQL keyword. Previously, a `constraint already exists` error was returned. [#90865](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/90865)
- Added the `contention_events` column to the `cluster_execution_insights` table to see which transaction is blocking the specific statement. [#90660](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/90660)
- `crdb_internal.scan` and `crdb_internal.list_sql_keys_in_range` return the timestamp for the time at which the value for a key was written, in addition to the raw key and value. [#90956](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/90956)
- Previously, the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/as-of-system-time" data-versioned="true">`AS OF SYSTEM TIME`</a> value was set at the start of the TTL job (with a TTL cutoff - 30s), but this results in an error for TTL jobs that run longer than `gc.ttlseconds`: `error selecting rows to delete: ttl select defaultdb.public.events: batch timestamp 1666883527.780656000,0 must be after replica GC threshold 1666883574.542825089,0`. CockroachDB now makes the `AS OF SYSTEM TIME` value relative to when each `SELECT` query is run (query time - 30s) to prevent this error from happening, but each `SELECT` query will run against a different table state. This should be ok because if records are missed during one job invocation they should still be picked up the next. [#90981](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/90981)
- The `system.sql_instances` table now includes pre-allocated ID entries, where all the fields except `id` will be `NULL`. [#90427](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/90427)
- The `to_char(timestamp, string)` <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/functions-and-operators" data-versioned="true">function</a> has been added. [#91382](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/91382)
- The `to_char(interval, string)` built-in <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/functions-and-operators" data-versioned="true">function</a> has been added. [#91382](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/91382)
- The `system.table_statistics` table now contains a column called `partialPredicate` to store a predicate for a partial statistic collection. [#91248](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/91248)
- A new `NumericStat`, `idleLat`, was introduced to the statistics column of `crdb_internal.statement_statistics`. This reports the time spent waiting for the client to send the statement while holding a transaction open. Developers may use this stat to identify opportunities for restructuring their apps to reduce contention. [#91098](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/91098)
- The set of supported compression algorithms in compress/decompress built-in <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/functions-and-operators" data-versioned="true">functions</a> is expanded to include `lz4`, `snappy`, and `zstd`. [#91162](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/91162)
- A new column `database` was added to `crdb_internal.{node,cluster}_queries` and list sessions <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cluster-api" data-versioned="true">endpoint</a>. [#91629](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/91629)
- Fixed a bug in the legacy schema changer where comments were not dropped together with the database. [#91689](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/91689)
- The `round(decimal` ) built-in <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/functions-and-operators" data-versioned="true">function</a> no longer returns negative 0 for any input. [#86106](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/86106)
- Added an estimate for the number of request units consumed by a query to the output of <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/explain-analyze" data-versioned="true">`EXPLAIN ANALYZE`</a> for tenant sessions. [#89256](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/89256)
- Enabled forward indexes on arrays. [#91762](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/91762)
- Users can now manually create partial single-column statistics at the extreme values on columns that are prefixes of their index. The output of <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/show-statistics" data-versioned="true">`SHOW STATISTICS`</a> now includes a column indicating the partial predicate for a partial statistic, or `NULL` for a full statistic. [#91228](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/91228)
- A new SQL statement `SHOW COMMIT TIMESTAMP` has been added. This statement can be used to retrieve the commit timestamp of the current explicit transaction, current multi-statement implicit transaction, or previous transaction. The statement may be used in a variety of settings to maximize its utility in the face of connection pooling. When used as a part of an explicit transaction, the statement implicitly commits the transaction internally before being able to return a causality token. [#80848](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/80848)
- Added support for the `pg_blocking_pids` built-in <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/functions-and-operators" data-versioned="true">function</a>. It is hardcoded to return an empty array because CockroachDB has no equivalent concept of PIDs as in PostgreSQL. [#92253](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/92253)
- Added a list of indexes used by the query on the statistics column on the `system.statement_statistics` and `crdb_internal.statement_statistics` tables. The format is `tableID@indexID`. [#92351](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/92351)
- Added a list of used indexes (with the format `tableID@indexID` ) to the sampled query telemetry log. [#92464](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/92464)
- A new `NumericStat`, `idleLat`, was introduced to the statistics column of `crdb_internal.transaction_statistics`. It reports the time spent waiting for the client to send statements while holding a transaction open. [#92695](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/92695)
- Added an in-memory-only evaluation of `tsvector` and `tsquery` datatypes and the `@@` matches operator. [#90842](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/90842)
- Implemented the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/alter-table" data-versioned="true">`ALTER TABLE... ADD CHECK`</a> statement in the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/online-schema-changes" data-versioned="true">declarative schema changer</a>. [#91153](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/91153)
- `to_char` now has caching for parse formats, marking a speedup when running `to_char` with the same format between sessions. [#91564](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/91564)
- Casts from index name to `REGCLASS` are now supported. Previously, only table names could be cast to `REGCLASS`. [#90649](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/90649)
- Added user-defined composite column types. [#90491](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/90491)
- SQL queries running on remote nodes now show up in CPU profiles with `distsql.*` labels. Currently this includes `appname`, `gateway`, `txn`, and stmt. [#92775](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/92775)
- CockroachDB now permits non-indexed storage of `tsvector` and `tsquery` datatypes [#92957](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/92957)
- Implemented the `parse_ident` built-in <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/functions-and-operators" data-versioned="true">function</a>, which splits a qualified identifier into an array of identifiers, removing any quoting of individual identifiers. By default, extra characters after the last identifier are considered an error; but if the second parameter is `false`, then such extra characters are ignored. [#93300](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/93300)

### Operational changes

- Reduced the length of the `raft.process.handleready.latency` metric help text to avoid it being rejected by certain Prometheus services. [#87166](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/87166)
- Logs produced by increasing the vmodule setting for `s3_storage` are now directed to the `DEV` channel rather than `STDOUT`. [#88798](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/88798)
- Added observability for when load-based splitting cannot find a key to indicate the reasons why the load splitter could not find a split key, which provides more insight into why a range is not splitting easier. [#88720](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/88720)
- Added five new fields to the `sampled_query` telemetry events:
  - `ScanCount`: Number of scans in the query plan.
  - `ScanWithStatsCount`: Number of scans using statistics (including forecasted statistics) in the query plan.
  - `ScanWithStatsForecastCount`: Number of scans using forecasted statistics in the query plan.
  - `TotalScanRowsWithoutForecastsEstimate`: Total number of rows read by all scans in the query, as estimated by the optimizer without using forecasts.
  - `NanosSinceStatsForecasted`: The greatest quantity of nanoseconds that have passed since the forecast time (or until the forecast time, if it is in the future, in which case it will be negative) for any table with forecasted stats scanned by this query. [#88539](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/88539)
- Added a new debug tool to allow for decrypting files in a store using <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/security-reference/encryption" data-versioned="true">encryption-at-rest</a>. This tool is intended for use while debugging, or for providing debug artifacts to Cockroach Labs to aid with support investigations. It is intended to be run "in-situ" (i.e., on site), as it prevents having to move sensitive key material. [#89668](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/89668)
- Added a new command that can be used by an operator to list the files present in the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/security-reference/encryption" data-versioned="true">encryption-at-rest</a> file registry. [#89873](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/89873)
- Release version binaries can now be instructed via the enviroment variable `COCKROACH_FORCE_DEV_VERSION` to override their cluster version support to match that of development builds, which can allow a release binary to be started in a cluster that is run (or has previously run) a development build. [#90002](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/90002)
- The consistency check failure message is now more informative, and suggests a few actions that operators should perform in the unlikely event a failure occurs. [#89899](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/89899)
- Updated metric descriptions of `rebalancing.*` to include the recording period. [#90619](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/90619)
- CockroachDB now prioritizes non-voters in voter additions, meaning that when selecting a store to add a voter on (in the allocator), CockroachDB will prioritize candidate stores that contain a non-voter replica higher. This reduces the number of snapshots that need to be sent over the WAN. [#89650](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/89650)
- CockroachDB now uses response data rather than just the request span in the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/load-based-splitting" data-versioned="true">load-based splitter</a> to pass more accurate data about the keys iterated over to the load splitter to find a suitable split key, enabling the load splitter to find a split key under heavy range query workloads. [#89217](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/89217)
- Added the `replicas.leaders_invalid_lease` metric, which indicates how many replicas are Raft group leaders but holding invalid leases. [#91179](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/91179)
- The <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cluster-settings" data-versioned="true">cluster settings</a> `server.web_session.purge.period` and `server.web_session.purge.max_deletions_per_cycle`, which were specific to the cleanup function for `system.web_sessions`, have been replaced by `server.log_gc.period` and `server.log_gc.max_deletions_per_cycle` which apply to the cleanup function for `system.eventlog`, `system.rangelog` and `system.web_sessions` equally. [#90789](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/90789)
- The <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cluster-settings" data-versioned="true">cluster setting</a> `server.web_session.auto_logout.timeout` has been removed. [#90789](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/90789)
- Splunk dashboard templates are available in the public repository under `/monitoring/splunk-dashboard/`. [#92330](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/92330)
- The network timeout for RPC connections between cluster nodes has been reduced from 3 seconds to 2 seconds, with a connection timeout of 4 seconds, in order to reduce unavailability and tail latencies during infrastructure outages. This can now be changed by setting the `COCKROACH_NETWORK_TIMEOUT` environment variable, which defaults to `2s`. [#92542](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/92542)
- The Raft election timeout has been reduced from 3 seconds to 2 seconds, and the lease interval from 9 seconds to 6 seconds, with a corresponding reduction in the node heartbeat interval from 4.5 seconds to 3 seconds. This reduces the period of unavailability following leaseholder loss, but places tighter restrictions on network latencies (no more than 500ms roundtrip time). This can be adjusted by setting the `COCKROACH_RAFT_ELECTION_TIMEOUT_TICKS` environment variable, which now defaults to 10 and will scale all of these intervals proportionally. [#91947](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/91947)
- The RPC heartbeat and gRPC keepalive ping intervals have been reduced to 1 second to detect failures faster. This is adjustable via the new `COCKROACH_PING_INTERVAL` environment variable. The timeouts remain unchanged. [#93399](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/93399)

### Command-line changes

- The interactive <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cockroach-sql" data-versioned="true">SQL shell</a> now retains a maximum of 1000 entries. There was no limit previously. [#88173](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/88173)
- The deprecated CLI command `debug unsafe-remove-dead-replicas` has been removed. Use `debug recover` instead. [#89150](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/89150)
- The `\df` metacommand was added to the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cockroach-sql" data-versioned="true">SQL shell</a>, which will list all <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/user-defined-functions" data-versioned="true">user-defined functions</a> in the current database. [#89557](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/89557)
- In the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cockroach-workload#kv-workload" data-versioned="true">`kv` workload</a>, you can now enable `--splits` with the `--sequential` flag and adjust splitting to uniformly partition the keyspace. [#90000](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/90000)
- Added the `--insert-count` flag to insert rows before the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cockroach-workload#kv-workload" data-versioned="true">`kv` workload</a> begins. [#90055](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/90055)
- CockroachDB will now include recommended remediation actions alongside log messages for some errors. [#82891](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/82891)
- The input syntax of `\set` is now more flexible: it is now more accepting of space characters in various positions of the syntax and it supports quoted values, e.g., via `\set prompt1 "a b c"`. [#90520](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/90520)
- <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cockroach-demo" data-versioned="true">
    `cockroach demo --global`
  </a>
  will now start up more quickly. The latency that will be injected will not be injected until after the initial cluster
  is set up internally. [#92231](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/92231)
- The engine used as line editor in the interactive shell ( <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cockroach-sql" data-versioned="true">`cockroach sql`</a> and <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cockroach-demo" data-versioned="true">`cockroach demo`</a> ) has been updated. It includes numerous bug fixes and new features. The previous engine can still be accessed by setting the `COCKROACH_SQL_FORCE_LIBEDIT` environment variable to true. This support will be removed in a later version. [#86457](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/86457)
- The interactive <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cockroach-sql" data-versioned="true">SQL shell</a> now supports an advanced debug mode for troubleshooting when `--debug-sql-cli` is specified on the command line. The debug mode can be enabled with Ctrl+@ or Ctrl+\_ (Ctrl+space on macOS). [#86457](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/86457)
- The following fields have been redacted and were added to the redacted debug zip:
  - `crdb_internal.create_statements`:
    - `create_statement`
      - `create_nofks`
    - `alter_statements` (each element is redacted)
  - `crdb_internal.create_function_statements`:
    - c `reate_statement`
  - `crdb_internal.{node,cluster}_distsql_flows`:
    - `stmt`
  - `crdb_internal.{cluster,node}_sessions`:
    - `last_active`
    - `active_queries`
  - `crdb_internal.{cluster,node}_queries`:
    - `query` [#92263](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/92263)
- The interactive <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cockroach-sql" data-versioned="true">SQL shell</a> now supports a rudimentary form of tab completion to input the name of SQL objects and functions. [#87606](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/87606)
- The command-line flag `--empty` to <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cockroach-demo" data-versioned="true">`cockroach demo`</a> is not marked as deprecated anymore; it is more convenient than `--no-example-database`. However, the latter remains supported as an alias. [#93255](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/93255)
- The command-line flags `--logtostderr`, `--log-file-verbosity`, `--no-color`, `--redactable-logs`, `--log-file-max-size`, `--log-group-max-size`, `--log-dir`, `--sql-audit-dir` are not marked as deprecated anymore; instead, they are defined as convenience aliases for various `--log` specifications. [#93255](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/93255)
- <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cockroach-demo" data-versioned="true">
    `cockroach demo`
  </a>
  now supports `--pid-file` for symmetry with
  <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cockroach-start" data-versioned="true">
    `cockroach start`
  </a>
  . [#93343](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/93343)
- The debug utility script `hot-ranges.sh` partitions output by statistics: `queries_per_second`, `writes_per_second`, `read_bytes_per_second`, `write_bytes_per_second`. It also decreased the number of ranges shown under each heading from 20 to 10. [#93528](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/93528)

### DB Console changes

- The High Contention Time insight description now accurately reflects the event's contention duration in the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/ui-overview" data-versioned="true">DB Console</a>. [#89035](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/89035)
- **Overview** and **Explain Plan** tabs were added to the **Active Statement Details** page. [#89021](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/89021)
- The **Apply** button was added on the **Table Details** page ( <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/ui-overview" data-versioned="true">DB Console</a> only) when there is a recommendation to drop an unused index. [#90070](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/90070)
- **Overview** and **Explain Plan** tabs were added to the **Statement Insight Details** page. [#90250](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/90250)
- The <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/ui-jobs-page" data-versioned="true">Jobs Page</a> now includes a column picker. [#89678](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/89678)
- The fingerprint ID values for statements and transactions on the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/ui-insights-page" data-versioned="true">Insights</a> pages are links that open the respective details page on the time period of the execution of that statement or transaction. [#90403](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/90403)
- Requests to fetch table and database statistics now have limited concurrency. This may make loading the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/ui-databases-page" data-versioned="true">Databases</a> page slower, but in return should result in making those pages less disruptive. [#90210](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/90210)
- The **Transaction** filter label on the **SQL Activity** page was fixed. [#91255](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/91255)
- The metric graph tooltip styling was fixed to prevent content collapse. [#91290](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/91290)
- Index recommendations were added to the **Statement Active Execution Details** page, and the plan gist was added as the first line of the explain plan. [#91629](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/91629)
- Transaction insights pages now show insights about slow execution with unknown causes, index recommendations, and failed executions. The following fields have also been added on the **Details** page, but are not available for transactions where the insight is "High Contention" (i.e., user name, session ID, rows processed, rows read, rows written, retries, last retry reason, full scan, and transaction priority). [#91698](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/91698)
- The fingerprint ID in hex format was added to the **Statement Details** page and **Transaction Details** page. [#91885](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/91885)
- The contention time, schema, database, table, and index info was added to the **Insights Statement Details** page. [#91668](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/91668)
- The query column in the insight recommendations table was removed. Instead, the statement is included in the description if the transaction being reported has multiple statements. [#91955](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/91955)
- Graphs on the **Metrics** page now downsample using max value instead of average. Previously, zooming out on a graph would cause any spikes in the graph to smooth out, potentially hiding anomalies. These anomalies are now visible even when looking at a zoomed out interval. [#92017](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/92017)
- The **Statement Execution** and **Planning Time** chart on the **Statement Fingerprint** page now includes a third value ("Idle") representing the time spent by the application waiting to execute this statement while holding a transaction open. [#92284](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/92284)
- A list of used index per explain plan was added, under the **Explain Plan** tab on the **Statement Details** page, with links to the table or index details pages. [#92463](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/92463)
- The <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/ui-insights-page" data-versioned="true">Insights</a> pages in the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/ui-overview" data-versioned="true">DB Console</a> now show the seconds and milliseconds for all timestamp values. [#92571](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/92571)
- Links were added on the fingerprint ID in the **High Contention** table on the **Transaction Insights Details** page. [#92612](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/92612)
- The following new charts were added to the Metrics page, under SQL view: **Service Latency: SQL Statements, 99.9th percentile** and **Service Latency: SQL Statements, 99.99th percentile**. [#92591](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/92591)
- Renamed the chart on the **Statement Details** page from **Statement Execution and Planning Time** to **Statement Times**. [#92765](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/92765)
- The **Transaction resource usage** card on the **Transaction Fingerprin** t page now includes an "Idle latency" row, representing the time spent by the application performing other work while holding this transaction open. [#92951](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/92951)
- The **Databases table** page now displays all the grants in a single row per user. [#92871](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/92871)
- Added a goroutine scheduling latency graph to the **Overload** dashboard in the DB Console. It shows what the per-node p99 scheduling latency is for goroutines. [#93217](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/93217)
- CockroachDB now prevents polling `/settings`, `/nodes_ui,` and `/cluster` endpoints on incorrect login. [#93211](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/93211)
- The **Statement** and **Transaction** pages for tenant clusters gained region columns and filters for multi-region tenants. [#92357](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/92357)

### Bug fixes

- The flag `--sql-advertise-addr` now properly works even when the SQL and RPC ports are shared (because `--sql-addr` was not specified). Note that this port sharing is a deprecated feature in v22.2. [#87412](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/87412)
- Fixed a bug introduced in v21.2 that could cause an internal error in rare cases when a query required a constrained index scan to return results in order. [#87562](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/87562)
- Fixed a bug that existed from before v21.1 that could cause an internal error when executing a query with a limit ordering on the output of a window function. [#87320](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/87320)
- Fixed an incorrect default value of `cloudstorage.gs.chunking.retry_timeout` to 60 seconds [#87817](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/87817)
- Fixed a bug in `pg_catalog` tables that could result in an internal error if a schema is concurrently dropped. [#88568](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/88568)
- Fixed a bug that caused `ALTER CHANGEFEED` to fail if the changefeed was created with a cursor option and had been running for more than `gc.ttlseconds`. [#88402](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/88402)
- Fixed a bug that could cause a panic when running a query with `EXPLAIN` that attempts to order on a non-output column. [#88441](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/88441)
- Fixed missing automatic statistics collection at cluster startup when the `sql.stats.automatic_collection.enabled` cluster setting is false, but there are tables with the storage parameter `sql_stats_automatic_collection_enabled` set to true. [#88673](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/88673)
- Fixes an issue where when a statement bundle was collected for a query that results in an error due to a `statement_timeout`, the bundle would not be saved. [#88080](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/88080)
- CockroachDB now excludes check constraints of hash-shared indexes from being invalidated when executing `IMPORT INTO`. [#89231](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/89231)
- CockroachDB now flushes WAL when writing storage checkpoints on consistency checker failures. [#89369](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/89369)
- Fixed optimizer selectivity and cost estimates of zigzag joins in order to prevent query plans from using it when it would perform poorly (e.g., when many rows are qualified). [#89261](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/89261)
- Changefeeds will now never permanently error on a "failed to send RPC" error. [#87763](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/87763)
- Fixed a bug that could occur when dropping a role that owned two schemas with the same name in different databases. The bug was introduced in v22.1.0. [#89504](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/89504)
- CockroachDB now avoids a source of internal connectivity problems that would resolve after restarting the affected node. [#89539](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/89539)
- CockroachDB now shows the correct value on table stats on UI, when there are no values to show. [#89867](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/89867)
- Charts on the **Statement Details** page in the DB Console are no longer overlapping. [#90014](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/90014)
- It is now possible to create tables, views, columns, etc. with the name `nothing` (e.g., `CREATE TABLE nothing...` ) without having to quote the name, like in PostgreSQL. This bug was introduced in CockroachDB v2.0. [#89903](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/89903)
- Fixed detection and erroring out of queries using locality-optimized joins when the session setting `enforce_home_region` is true and the input table to the join has no home region or its home region does not match the gateway region. [#90107](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/90107)
- Fixed an issue with the `enforce_home_region` session setting which may cause `SHOW CREATE TABLE` or other non-DML statements to error out if the optimizer plan for the statement involves accessing a multi-region table. [#90007](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/90007)
- Fixed a bug in `changefeed.batch_reduction_retry` which resulted in only a single level of retry being able to occur. [#90153](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/90153)
- During JWT based auth, CockroachDB now infers the algorithm type if it is not specified by the JWKS. This enables support for a wider range of keys. [#89989](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/89989)
- Fixed an extremely rare out of bounds crash in the protected timestamp subsystem. [#90357](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/90357)
- Fixed the calculation of the `pg_attribute.attnum` column for indexes so that the `attnum` is always based on the order the column appears in the index. Also fixed the `pg_attribute` table so that it includes stored columns in secondary indexes. [#90287](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/90287)
- Fixed a bug in the DB Console where when the height of the filter was big, you had to scroll to get to the **Apply** button. [#90457](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/90457)
- Fixed a bug in the DB Console to now send the proper start and end values to the endpoint used on the **SQL Activity** page so it returns the full hour as described on the UI. [#90403](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/90403)
- Fixed a rare bug where concurrent follower read/split operations could lead to invalid read results. [#89886](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/89886)
- Fixed a bug that could cause `UPDATE.. FROM` clauses to update the same row multiple times, resulting in incorrect `UPDATED` row counts and duplicate output rows for statements with a `RETURNING` clause. The bug only appeared when the target table had a hidden primary key column (e.g., an implicit `rowid` primary key column). The bug has been present since support for `UPDATE.. FROM` was added in v19.0. [#89780](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/89780)
- Protected timestamps are now created during index validation. Before, index validation could be starved if it took longer than any GC jobs for a given table. [#89540](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/89540)
- Fixed a bug where `SELECT *` operations on tables with virtual computed columns undergoing schema changes could potentially fail. [#90670](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/90670)
- Fixed a bug where in large, multi-region clusters it was possible for the leasing mechanism used for jobs to get caught in a live-lock scenario whereby jobs could not be adopted. [#90875](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/90875)
- CockroachDB now ensures changefeeds shut down when one of the aggregator nodes returns an error. [#90767](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/90767)
- Fixed a bug the occurred when attempting to reduce the size of a fixed-size `VARCHAR` column. [#91078](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/91078)
- Fixed a bug that caused ranges to remain without a leaseholder in cases of asymmetric network partitions. [#87244](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/87244)
- Fixed a bug that would prevent data from a failed restore from being cleaned up quickly. [#88342](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/88342)
- Fixed a bug which, in rare cases, could result in a changefeed missing rows which occur around the time of a split in writing transactions which take longer than the closed timestamp target duration (defaults to 3s). [#91116](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/91116)
- Fixed a bug where point lookups on the `pg_catalog.pg_type` table would fail to find the implicit record type that gets created for tables in the `pg_catalog`, `information_schema`, and `crdb_internal` schemas. [#90924](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/90924)
- Fixed a bug that prevented the usage of implicit record types for tables in the `pg_catalog`, `information_schema`, and `crdb_internal` schemas. [#90924](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/90924)
- Fixed a bug that could result in transient errors when dropping a database and immediately recreating a database with the same name and connecting to it for use. [#91174](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/91174)
- Fixes a bug that resulted in the regions listed for databases and tables including an incorrect list of regions due to the logic including information about tables which are adjacent in the keyspace. [#91130](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/91130)
- Fixed a bug where the experimental `scrub` command did not handle type descriptors in the database. [#91085](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/91085)
- Fixed a panic that could occur when calling `st_distancespheroid` or `st_distancesphere` with a spatial object containing an `NaN` coordinate. This now produces an error, with the message "input is out of range". [#90218](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/90218)
- Fixed a bug that could result in infrequent progress updates for very large backup or restore jobs. [#89971](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/89971)
- Added leading zeros to fingerprint IDs with less than 16 characters. [#91885](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/91885)
- Fixed a bug causing changefeeds to fail when a value is deleted while running on a non-primary column family with multiple columns. [#91870](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/91870)
- Fixed a bug that existed since before v21.1 where the `cgroup` memory limit was undetected when using `systemd`. [#91789](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/91789)
- Fixed a bug that existed since v20.2 that could cause incorrect results in rare cases for queries with inner joins and left joins. [#91425](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/91425)
- Fixed an unhandled error that could happen if `ALTER DEFAULT PRIVILEGES` was run on the system database. [#92075](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/92075)
- CockroachDB now prevents schema changes on the `crdb_internal_expiration` table. [#91720](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/91720)
- When configured to true, the `sql.metrics.statement_details.dump_to_logs` cluster setting no longer causes a mutex deadlock. [#92272](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/92272)
- Fixed a bug that could lead to errors when running multiple schema change statements in a single command using a driver that uses the extended pgwire protocol internally (for example the Npgsql C# driver). The error messages was "attempted to update job for mutation 2, but job already exists with mutation 1". [#92300](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/92300)
- Fixed the **Statement Activity** page so that it no longer shows multi-statement implicit transactions as "explicit." [#92408](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/92408)
- Server crashes that occur during startup are now more clearly reported in logs and the standard error output. [#91823](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/91823)
- Fixed incorrect cancellation logic when attempting to detect stuck rangefeeds. [#92582](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/92582)
- Fixed an internal error when comparing a tuple type with a non-tuple type. [#92635](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/92635)
- Fixed incorrect selectivity estimation for queries with `OR` predicates all referencing a common single table. [#89358](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/89358)
- Added sort setting to tables on the **Transaction** and **Statement Insights Details** pages. [#92573](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/92573)
- Fixed an issue where `changefeed.emitted_messages` would be increased twice per message for changefeed cloud storage sinks. [#92685](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/92685)
- Fixed a bug where `attidentity` in `pg_attribute` for the `GENERATED BY DEFAULT AS IDENTITY` column should be `d`. [#92545](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/92545)
- CockroachDB previously could incorrectly evaluate queries that performed left semi and left anti "virtual lookup" joins on tables in `pg_catalog` or `information_schema`. These join types can be planned when a subquery is used inside of a filter condition. The bug was introduced in v20.2.0 and is now fixed. [#92713](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/92713)
- Fixed a link to index details on the **Drop Index Insights** in the Cloud Console. [#92953](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/92953)
- Fixed a bug where encoding of `ARRAY` type to Parquet format would fail in some cases during the `EXPORT` command. [#92948](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/92948)
- Fixed a rare panic only present in v22.2.0 that occurs when using particular forms of existing statistics in table statistics forecasting. [#92707](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/92707)
- In the presence of several backup files, CockroachDB now speeds up slow listing calls that could manifest as restore queries hanging during execution. [#93072](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/93072)
- Prepared statements that use type hints can now succeed type-checking in more cases when the placeholder type is ambiguous. [#92834](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/92834)
- Fixed a bug where glob patterns that matched no tables in `GRANT` or `REVOKE` statements would return an internal error with a confusing message as opposed to the appropriate "no objects matched" error. [#93173](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/93173)
- Fixed a bug where empty `COPY` commands would not escape after an EOF character or error if encountering a `\.` with no input. [#93100](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/93100)
- Fixed a bug where in PostgreSQL extended protocol mode it was possible for auto-commits to not execute certain logic for DDL, when certain DML (insert/update/delete) and DDL were combined in an implicit transaction. [#93283](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/93283)
- Fixed the `pg_table_is_visible` built-in function so it correctly reports visibility of indexes based on the current `search_path`. [#90649](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/90649)
- Fixed a bug that would result in incomplete backups when non-default, non-public resource limiting settings ( `kv.bulk_sst.max_request_time` or `admission.elastic_cpu.enabled` ) were enabled. [#92825](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/92825)
- The `pg_function_is_visible` function now correctly reports visibility based on the functions that are visible on the current `search_path`. [#90657](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/90657)
- Fixed a rare bug that could cause upgrades from v22.1 to v22.2 to fail if the job coordinator node crashes in the middle of a specific upgrade migration. [#93487](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/93487)
- Fixed a bug for queries with disjunctions (i.e., contains `OR` ) where all the columns referenced in the disjunctions are known to have a single value. [#93480](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/93480)
- Fixed a bug introduced in v22.1.0 in which the non-default nulls ordering, `NULLS LAST`, was ignored in window and aggregate functions. This bug would cause incorrect query results when `NULLS LAST` was used. [#93426](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/93426)
- Fixed a bug that caused an internal error when trying to execute a UDF with an empty function body. This bug was present since UDFs were introduced in v22.2.0. [#93331](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/93331)
- Fixed an issue where `DISTINCT ON` queries would fail with the error "SELECT DISTINCT ON expressions must match initial ORDER BY expressions" when the query included an `ORDER BY` clause containing `ASC NULLS LAST` or `DESC NULLS FIRST`. [#93567](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/93567)
- Fixed a bug where selecting a small timeframe in the past in a timeseries query resulted in no data in the graphs. [#93293](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/93293)
- Fixed a bug where CockroachDB would error when receiving Geometry/Geography using binary parameters. [#93563](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/93563)
- Fixed an internal error that could occur when comparing a column of type void to `NULL` using `col IS NULL` or `col IS NOT NULL`. [#93652](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/93652)
- Fixed a bug where a query would incorrectly pass if a given interval for `AS OF SYSTEM TIME` interval was a small positive duration. [#93146](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/93146)

### Performance improvements

- The <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cost-based-optimizer" data-versioned="true">optimizer</a> will now plan <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/inverted-indexes" data-versioned="true">inverted index</a> scans for queries with JSON subscripting filters, like `json_col['field'] = '"value"`. [#87957](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/87957)
- CockroachDB now avoids wasteful contention on the gossip mutex caused by checking if the network needs tightening hundreds of times per second. [#88472](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/88472)
- Some types of queries with comparisons with constant values now execute faster. [#88638](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/88638)
- The <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cost-based-optimizer" data-versioned="true">optimizer</a> now explores plans with a single <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/joins#lookup-joins" data-versioned="true">lookup join</a> expressions in rare cases where it previously planned two lookup join expressions. [#88491](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/88491)
- Consistency checks are now properly cancelled on timeout, preventing them from piling up. [#86591](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/86591)
- Raft ticks now adapt to scheduling delays. This helps preventing re-elections, and the corresponding performance effects, in the event of relatively short (sub-second) processing delays. [#86240](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/86240)
- HTTP requests with `Accept-encoding: gzip` previously resulted in valid GZIP-encoded, but uncompressed, responses. This resulted in inefficient HTTP transfer times, as far more bytes were transferred than necessary. Those responses are now properly compressed, resulting in smaller network responses. [#88950](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/88950)
- `pg_catalog.col_description` is now much faster when resolving columns for tables in the `pg_catalog`, `crdb_internal`, or `information_schema` namespaces. [#89465](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/89465)
- The <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cost-based-optimizer" data-versioned="true">optimizer</a> now does less copying of histograms while planning queries, which will reduce memory pressure a little. [#88526](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/88526)
- Added early inlining of `VALUES` clauses and unnested arrays in `WITH` queries in order to eliminate unnecessary joins. [#87790](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/87790)
- Added significantly faster JSON parsing, which should help with any workloads that insert large amounts of JSON data, including <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/import" data-versioned="true">`IMPORT`</a> workloads. [#89884](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/89884)
- Loading the **Database Details** page in the DB Console is now somewhat less expensive when there are a large number of databases and a large number of tables in each database and a large number of ranges in the cluster. [#90198](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/90198)
- Tables in `pg_catalog` and `information_schema` (when not explicitly referenced as `"".information_schema` ) may now be much faster if the current database has a small number of relations relative to the total number in the cluster. [#90116](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/90116)
- The overhead of running <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/explain-analyze" data-versioned="true">`EXPLAIN ANALYZE`</a> and `EXPLAIN ANALYZE (DISTSQL)` has been significantly reduced. The overhead of `EXPLAIN ANALYZE (DEBUG)` did not change. [#91117](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/91117)
- Enabled more efficient <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/joins#lookup-joins" data-versioned="true">lookup joins</a> by deriving new join constraints when equijoin predicates exist on the column(s) of a unique constraint on one table which are a proper subset of the referencing columns of a foreign key constraint on the other table. If an index exists on those foreign key constraint referencing columns, equijoin predicates are derived between the primary key and foreign key columns not currently bound by `ON` clause predicates. [#90599](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/90599)
- The setup of the distributed query execution is now fully parallelized which should reduce the query latencies, especially in multi-region setups. [#89649](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/89649)
- Performance of the `LIKE` and `ILIKE` operators using patterns without any wildcards has been improved. [#91895](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/91895)
- The <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cost-based-optimizer" data-versioned="true">optimizer</a> can now better calculate the properties of recursive <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/common-table-expressions" data-versioned="true">common table expressions</a> in the presence of a `LIMIT`. [#90725](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/90725)
- Certain types of reads will now have a far smaller contention footprint with conflicting concurrent writers. [#85993](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/85993)
- In some cases, the key-value store client now needs to look up where to send requests. Prior to this change, such lookup requests were always routed to the leaseholder of the metadata range storing that information. Now the client can attempt to look up this metadata from followers. This can improve tail latency in multi-region clusters in cases where the range addressing cache is cold. [#91638](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/91638)
- The garbage collection score triggering a MVCC GC run has been lowered. The GC Score is a ratio computed from MVCC stats and uses the ratio of live objects and estimated garbage age to estimate collectability of existing data. The reduced score will trigger garbage collection earlier, lowering the interval between runs 3 times, giving 2 times reduced peak garbage usage at the expense of 30% increase of wasteful data scanning on constantly updated data. [#92118](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/92118)
- CockroachDB in some cases now correctly incorporates the value of the `OFFSET` clause when determining the number of rows that need to be read when the `LIMIT` clause is also present. Note that there was no correctness issue here, only that extra unnecessary rows could be read. [#92779](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/92779)
- In 22.2, privileges on virtual tables (system catalogs like `pg_catalog`, `information_schema`, and `crdb_internal` ) were introduced. A problem with this new feature is that we now must fetch those privileges into a cache before we can use those tables or determine their visibility in other system catalogs. This process used to occur on-demand, when the privilege was needed. Now, CockroachDB will fetch these privileges eagerly during startup to mitigate latency when accessing `pg_catalog` right after the server boots up. [#93557](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/93557)
